													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
			isDedicatedForArticle: false,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["US","GB","CA","AU","DE","SG","MY","VN","ID","PH","TH","ES","FR","AR","MX","CO","PE","NZ","IN","DE","VN","FR","BR","ES","PL","CL"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping && (videoDetails.isDedicatedForArticle || isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry())
					&& !hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Naruto Uzumaki</b> (<span lang="ja">うずまきナルト</span>&#44; <i>Uzumaki Naruto</i>) is a <a href="/wiki/Shinobi" title="Shinobi">shinobi</a> of <a href="/wiki/Konohagakure" title="Konohagakure">Konohagakure</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Uzumaki_clan" class="mw-redirect" title="Uzumaki clan">Uzumaki clan</a>. He became the <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails" class="mw-redirect" title="Nine-Tails">Nine-Tails</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tailed_Demon_Fox%27s_Attack" title="Nine-Tailed Demon Fox&#39;s Attack">day of his birth</a> — a fate that caused him to be shunned by most of Konoha throughout his childhood. After joining <a href="/wiki/Team_Kakashi" class="mw-redirect" title="Team Kakashi">Team Kakashi</a>, Naruto worked hard to gain the village's acknowledgement all the while chasing his dream to become <a href="/wiki/Hokage" title="Hokage">Hokage</a>. In the following years, through many hardships and ordeals, he became a capable ninja, regarded as a hero both by the villagers, and soon after, the rest of the world, becoming known as the <b>Hero of the Hidden Leaf</b> (<span lang="ja">木ノ葉隠れの英雄</span>&#44; <i>Konohagakure no Eiyū</i>&#44; <i>literally meaning:</i> Hero of the Hidden Tree Leaves). He soon proved to be one of the main factors in winning the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>, leading him to achieve his dream and become the village's <b>Seventh Hokage</b> (<span lang="ja">七代目火影</span>&#44; <i>Nanadaime Hokage</i>&#44; <i>literally meaning:</i> Seventh Fire Shadow).
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_and_Kushina2.png/revision/latest?cb=20160129152021" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Kushina2" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Kushina2.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Kushina2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_and_Kushina2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160129152021" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_and_Kushina2.png/revision/latest?cb=20160129152021" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Kushina2" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_and_Kushina2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160129152021" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Kushina2.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Kushina2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_and_Kushina2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160129152021" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Kushina2.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto, newborn with his mother Kushina.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto was born on the night of October 10th to <a href="/wiki/Minato_Namikaze" title="Minato Namikaze">Minato Namikaze</a> (the Fourth Hokage) and <a href="/wiki/Kushina_Uzumaki" title="Kushina Uzumaki">Kushina Uzumaki</a> (the second jinchūriki of the Nine-Tails). He was named after <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Musasabi" title="Naruto Musasabi">Naruto Musasabi</a>, the protagonist of <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>'s <a href="/wiki/The_Tale_of_the_Utterly_Gutsy_Shinobi" title="The Tale of the Utterly Gutsy Shinobi">first book</a>, which made the <a href="/wiki/Sannin" title="Sannin">Sannin</a> his godfather.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Third_Hokage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Hokage">Third Hokage</a> made special arrangements for Minato to preserve Kushina's seal containing the Nine-Tails while she gave birth to Naruto in a remote location, assisted by midwives and <a href="/wiki/Anbu" title="Anbu">Anbu</a>. A masked man, <a href="/wiki/Tobi" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobi">Tobi</a>, tracked down their location, however, killed the midwives and Anbu, and captured Naruto, forcing Minato to quickly rescue him and <a href="/wiki/Flying_Thunder_God_Technique" title="Flying Thunder God Technique">teleport</a> him to a <a href="/wiki/Minato%27s_Safe_House" class="mw-redirect" title="Minato&#39;s Safe House">safe house</a>.
</p>
<table align="right"><tbody><tr><th></th><td><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="/wiki/File:Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png" title="File:Minato and Kushina protect Naruto.png"><img alt="Minato and Kushina protect Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minato and Kushina protect Naruto.png" data-image-key="Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240124003940" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="/wiki/File:Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png" title="File:Minato and Kushina protect Naruto.png"><img alt="Minato and Kushina protect Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240124003940" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minato and Kushina protect Naruto.png" data-image-key="Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240124003940" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minato_and_Kushina_protect_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minato and Kushina protect Naruto from the Nine-Tails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>With Minato gone, Tobi captured Kushina and <a href="/wiki/Tail_Releasing_Method" title="Tail Releasing Method">released</a> the Nine-Tails from her, using it to <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tailed_Demon_Fox%27s_Attack" title="Nine-Tailed Demon Fox&#39;s Attack">devastate Konoha</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ch500_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch500-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Minato saved Kushina and left Naruto in her care before he went to protect the village,<sup id="cite_ref-ch501_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch501-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> eventually defeating Tobi and <a href="/wiki/Contract_Seal" title="Contract Seal">freeing</a> the Nine-Tails from Tobi's control. Returning to Naruto and Kushina's location, Minato realised the only way to stop the Nine-Tails was to seal it within Naruto, believing that his son would someday need the fox's power to defeat Tobi when he returned.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Since the Nine-Tails' <a href="/wiki/Chakra" title="Chakra">chakra</a> was too immense to be sealed into an infant, Minato <a href="/wiki/Dead_Demon_Consuming_Seal" title="Dead Demon Consuming Seal">sacrificed his soul</a> to split the fox's chakra in half, sealing the <a href="/wiki/Yin" class="mw-redirect" title="Yin">Yin</a> half within himself and the <a href="/wiki/Yang" class="mw-redirect" title="Yang">Yang</a> half <a href="/wiki/Eight_Trigrams_Sealing_Style" title="Eight Trigrams Sealing Style">within</a> Naruto. After telling Naruto how much they loved him, Minato and Kushina succumbed to their wounds from protecting their son from the Nine-Tails and passed away.
</p><p>Orphaned, and not having anyone else to provide for him, Naruto received monthly income from the village in order to afford daily necessities. Naruto grew up not knowing who his parents were, receiving only his mother's surname, as Hiruzen wanted to protect Naruto from his father's enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Minato's dying wish that Naruto be regarded as a hero was honoured by the very few who could put aside their pain and losses caused by the disaster, while the majority of Konoha, however having no knowledge of the circumstances surrounding his birth, openly ostracised and resented Naruto for containing the beast that devastated the village and took many lives; some even viewed Naruto as the Nine-Tails itself. Soon, the Third Hokage forbade anyone from mentioning the Nine-Tails, hoping that the younger generation would not blindly hate Naruto as their parents did.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> However, Naruto's peers emulated their parents' hatred of him, despite not knowing why. This social isolation caused Naruto to crave acknowledgement, which he would gain by pulling pranks.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711120110" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s first encounter with Hinata" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s first encounter with Hinata.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120110" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711120110" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s first encounter with Hinata" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120110" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s first encounter with Hinata.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120110" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_first_encounter_with_Hinata.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets Hinata.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the day of his enrolment in the <a href="/wiki/Ninja_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Ninja Academy">Ninja Academy</a><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> - Naruto first met <a href="/wiki/Hinata_Hy%C5%ABga" title="Hinata Hyūga">Hinata Hyūga</a>, who was being picked on by three bullies. Despite not knowing her, Naruto immediately came to her defence, but he was outnumbered and knocked unconscious, and the bullies damaged his red scarf. When Naruto awoke, Hinata thanked him for helping her and returned his scarf to him, but he let her keep it. He was unaware that the girl's growing affection for him began at that moment.<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table align="right"><tbody><tr><th></th><td><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="/wiki/File:Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png" title="File:Young sasuke and Naruto.png"><img alt="Young sasuke and Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Young sasuke and Naruto.png" data-image-key="Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210925220045" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="/wiki/File:Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png" title="File:Young sasuke and Naruto.png"><img alt="Young sasuke and Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210925220045" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Young sasuke and Naruto.png" data-image-key="Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210925220045" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Young_sasuke_and_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke in the Academy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In the Academy, Naruto became a student of <a href="/wiki/Iruka_Umino" title="Iruka Umino">Iruka Umino</a>, who acted as a surrogate older brother to keep him in line and help him work harder. Naruto also met his classmate <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Uchiha" title="Sasuke Uchiha">Sasuke Uchiha</a> and tried to befriend him, since Sasuke was alone as well. Jealous of Sasuke's skills and popularity, however,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> he developed a one-sided rivalry in his pursuit to prove himself just as good as, if not better than, Sasuke, wishing that someday, Sasuke would accept him as an equal.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Naruto also grew close with the owner of <a href="/wiki/Ramen_Ichiraku" title="Ramen Ichiraku">Ramen Ichiraku</a>, <a href="/wiki/Teuchi" title="Teuchi">Teuchi</a> and his daughter <a href="/wiki/Ayame" title="Ayame">Ayame</a>, being welcomed as their favourite customer.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1e/Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20150405165827" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Ninja Registration Photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Ninja Registration Photo.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1e/Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150405165827" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1e/Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20150405165827" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Ninja Registration Photo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1e/Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150405165827" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Ninja Registration Photo.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1e/Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150405165827" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_Ninja_Registration_Photo.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's ninja registration photo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto is noted as boisterous, exuberant, and unorthodox, quite similar to <a href="/wiki/Hashirama_Senju" title="Hashirama Senju">Hashirama Senju</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He inherited his mother's verbal tic, as he ends his sentences with "<a href="/wiki/Dattebayo_and_Believe_It" class="mw-redirect" title="Dattebayo and Believe It">Dattebayo!</a>" (<span lang="ja">だってばよ!</span>) when emotional. Though he responds best to competition and is not afraid to ask for assistance, Naruto is relatively naïve and slow to understand principles or situations. He often requires an oversimplified analogy in order to grasp explanations<sup id="cite_ref-ch409_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch409-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and can even prove forgetful.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Naruto is aware of his faults and admits he acts strong to mask his embarrassment and frustration about them.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ch440_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch440-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Despite his naivety, Naruto can be quite observant, picking up on things others miss and retaining information casually gathered through conversation.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Growing up as an orphan who suffered years of hatred and social isolation has influenced Naruto's character in a number of ways: he is heedless to formality and social standings, addressing <a href="/wiki/Rock_Lee" title="Rock Lee">certain</a> <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">people</a> with nicknames instead of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honorific" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Honorific">honourifics</a>, although by the time of his adulthood, Naruto has slightly outgrown this trait.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He has picky eating habits of ramen, his favourite food; he has a perverted side that manifests as attempts to peep into women's baths, although these moments are rare.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Despite his quirks and the criticism they earn him to the point of being labelled the <i>ultimate problem child</i>, Naruto is said to have a personality that draws people to him,<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> inspiring friendship and loyalty through acts of genuine kindness that could change a person's world view and thus built <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Uzumaki%27s_Relationships" title="Naruto Uzumaki&#39;s Relationships">meaningful relationships</a> that he lacked in early life; the <a href="/wiki/Sage_of_Six_Paths" class="mw-redirect" title="Sage of Six Paths">Sage of Six Paths</a> believes Naruto's kindness is a special gift that allows him to save <a href="/wiki/Kurama" title="Kurama">Kurama</a> from its hatred.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Naruto deeply cherishes these bonds and will go to great lengths to protect them, best seen with Sasuke after his defection from Konoha.
</p><p>Another of Naruto's prominent traits is his desire for acknowledgement; his pranks around the village were for people to notice him, even if it meant by scolding him. Therefore, he dreamed of one day becoming Konoha's Hokage, the epitome of acknowledgement and respect from everyone in the village.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Knowing his dream is a long, arduous and seemingly impossible path, Naruto developed his own <a href="/wiki/Nind%C5%8D" title="Nindō">nindō</a> of never going back on his word. This life-long philosophy serves as the cornerstone of Naruto's great self-confidence; he believes he can accomplish any goal with enough hard work and perseverance, no matter what. This trait guides him in many aspects of life, such as his promise to bring Sasuke back to Konoha. Over time, his goal to be Hokage grew from a desire for the acknowledgement of others to a desire to help and protect the people close to him, which <a href="/wiki/Tobi" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobi">Tobi</a> attributed to the <a href="/wiki/Will_of_Fire" title="Will of Fire">Will of Fire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> His nindō has since been reinforced by his understanding that shinobi were meant to endure through hardships.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> His belief in hard work and perseverance made him detest shortcuts to achieving, as he disqualified his son from the <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%ABnin_Exams" title="Chūnin Exams">Chūnin Exams</a> for using the banned <a href="/wiki/Kote" class="mw-redirect" title="Kote">Kote</a>, and expressed disgust at <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki" class="mw-redirect" title="Momoshiki">Momoshiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kinshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki">Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki</a> for their reliance on harvesting from <a href="/wiki/Chakra_Fruit" class="mw-redirect" title="Chakra Fruit">Chakra Fruits</a> to lazily gain power.<sup id="cite_ref-BorutoMovie_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorutoMovie-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the death of his master <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>, talking to his father <a href="/wiki/Minato" class="mw-redirect" title="Minato">Minato</a> and listening to <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">Nagato</a>'s tragic story, Naruto grew to understand the destructive cycle of hatred and he vowed to break it in order to bring true peace to the world.<sup id="cite_ref-ch448_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch448-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> To that end, his participation in the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a> is not only to protect his friends but also to bear and erase the world's hatred all by himself. After encountering a <a href="/wiki/Summoning:_Impure_World_Reincarnation" title="Summoning: Impure World Reincarnation">reincarnated</a> <a href="/wiki/Itachi_Uchiha" title="Itachi Uchiha">Itachi Uchiha</a>, however, Naruto realises that he cannot handle everything alone and that he must allow his friends to support and fight alongside him. As he does so in war's climax, his fighting spirit inspires the <a href="/wiki/Allied_Shinobi_Forces" title="Allied Shinobi Forces">Allied Shinobi Forces</a> to join him and keep fighting to end the war as well, ultimately becoming an example for many people to admire, follow, and believe in.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/36/Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png/revision/latest?cb=20150821103014" class="image"><img alt="Naruto watching Hinata knit" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto watching Hinata knit.png" data-image-key="Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/36/Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821103014" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/36/Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png/revision/latest?cb=20150821103014" class="image"><img alt="Naruto watching Hinata knit" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/36/Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821103014" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto watching Hinata knit.png" data-image-key="Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/36/Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821103014" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_watching_Hinata_knit.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto becomes shy around Hinata.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto first met <a href="/wiki/Hinata_Hy%C5%ABga" title="Hinata Hyūga">Hinata Hyūga</a> when they were children, where his open kindness and courageous spirit earned him her admiration, which grew into love. On his part, Naruto remained mostly oblivious to Hinata's feelings for him and even considered her "weird" because of her shyness around him and his socially ostracised childhood. However, that change during the Chūnin Exams in Part I when they began to interact more and support each other, causing Naruto to like her as a friend.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> In Part II, as Hinata becomes willing to risk her life to protect Naruto, he, in turn, sees her as an actively strong person despite his speechlessness at her love confession. Naruto grew to love Hinata subconsciously. Still, he was unaware of it because he kept "fighting" for Sakura, which was just another way for him to compete with Sasuke. During <i><a href="/wiki/The_Last:_Naruto_the_Movie" title="The Last: Naruto the Movie">The Last: Naruto the Movie</a></i>, Naruto finally recognises the love that Hinata has always had for him, causing him to become more bashful and protective of her, just as she was for him. Realising that she alone has ever had faith in him and that she has always been there for him, he reciprocates her feelings and desires to be with her for the rest of his life. This new-found desire made him willing to make healthier lifestyle choices such as eating vegetables and reeling in his impulsiveness, something others have had little success with doing.
</p><p>As an adult, Naruto becomes wiser and more mature, though he retains some of his negligence for honourifics.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Although he finally achieves his dream of becoming Hokage, its many tasks would often overwhelm Naruto to the point of him being unable to spend time with his family. He admits that part of this stems was from not having grown up with a father himself, making him unsure of how to interact appropriately with his children.<sup id="cite_ref-BE10_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BE10-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Naruto also tends to be more responsible in his duties as Hokage than as a father. Nevertheless, Naruto profoundly loves his family, as he creates shadow clones to tend to them while he's busy, protects them in times of danger, spends time with them when he can, and expresses pride in his children's successes.<sup id="cite_ref-BorutoMovie_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorutoMovie-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He adopts Hiruzen's philosophy that everyone in the village is his family, believing that genuine relationships are made up of love rather than blood relations.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> His refusal to give his son any special treatment due to their blood-relationships, along with the insistence that the boy professionally addresses him as "Seventh" or "Hokage" while in the office, is a testament of Naruto's lack of bias and prejudice.<sup id="cite_ref-BorutoMovie_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorutoMovie-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Likewise, even in the face of people close to him committing horrible deeds, Naruto remains loyal to them, pushing aside his grief enough to see the nature of what they did.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> However, after facing <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki">Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki</a> and realising how his overly-committed nature serving the entire village was significantly affecting his own family's happiness, Naruto came to accept that he needed to give them more attention. As such, by allowing more help from others, Naruto was able to enjoy more time with his family, restoring the same healthy relationship he had with them before he became Hokage.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_Naruto">Dark Naruto</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d4/Dark_Naruto_appears.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125040012" class="image"><img alt="Dark Naruto appears" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dark Naruto appears.png" data-image-key="Dark_Naruto_appears.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d4/Dark_Naruto_appears.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125040012" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d4/Dark_Naruto_appears.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125040012" class="image"><img alt="Dark Naruto appears" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d4/Dark_Naruto_appears.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125040012" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dark Naruto appears.png" data-image-key="Dark_Naruto_appears.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d4/Dark_Naruto_appears.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125040012" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dark_Naruto_appears.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"Dark Naruto" reveals himself in the waterfall.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although he struggled to overcome the hatred of people and the shinobi world, seeking to achieve the peace that his master Jiraiya dreamed of so much, Naruto was also not free from his own hatred. When Naruto understands that it is necessary to definitively master the power of the Nine-Tails, he goes to the <a href="/wiki/Genbu" title="Genbu">Island Turtle</a> and discovers the <a href="/wiki/Falls_of_Truth" title="Falls of Truth">Falls of Truth</a> as part of the process. There, Naruto encounters his darker half: <b>Dark Naruto</b> (<span lang="ja">闇ナルト</span>&#44; <i>Yami Naruto</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> This was the personification of all of Naruto's negative feelings, such as the grudge he secretly still held against the villagers of Konoha who had always rejected him since childhood. Dark Naruto was the Nine-Tails' favourite aspect of Naruto, claiming him to be the "real" Naruto. No matter how much he resisted, the Nine-Tails would tap into the hatred that existed hidden in the depths of his heart.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's conclusion to dealing with his inner hatred was not to ignore him, but rather accept his existence, understanding that this same grudge was what made him get to where he was and value his entire journey up until that moment.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> This whole process served as basis for Naruto to shape who he truly wanted to be from then on.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>According to <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>, Naruto strongly resembles his father:<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> he has yellow-blond, spiky hair and blue eyes, while inheriting the shape of his mother's eyes and face.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> His trademark characteristics are the three whisker markings on his cheeks. During the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dan_Kat%C5%8D" title="Dan Katō">Dan Katō</a> initially mistook Naruto for <a href="/wiki/Nawaki" title="Nawaki">Nawaki</a> due to their stark resemblance.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Naruto was rather short for his age during Part I,<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> though he grew to be taller than <a href="/wiki/Sakura" class="mw-redirect" title="Sakura">Sakura</a> in Part II.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Naruto originally wore green goggles on his forehead, though he discards them upon becoming a genin.
</p>
<div type="slideshow" position="right" widths="240" mode="slideshow" seq-no="0" id="slideshow-0" hash="3093106b1c54dd19640c3162134f4d90" class="wikia-slideshow wikia-gallery floatright" 0px;" data-image-name="Naruto - The Last.png" data-image-key="Naruto_-_The_Last.png" data-relevant="1" alt="Naruto in the Blank Period." data-caption="Naruto in the Blank Period." /></a><div class="wikia-slideshow-overlay"><div class="wikia-slideshow-image-caption">Naruto in the Blank Period.</div></div></li><li><a class="image lightbox" title="Expand slideshow" id="slideshow-0-3" height="180" style="border: 0px;" data-image-name="Naruto epilogue.PNG" data-image-key="Naruto_epilogue.PNG" data-relevant="1" alt="Naruto in the New Era." data-caption="Naruto in the New Era."
