class="wikia-slideshow-toolbar-counter" data-counter="$1/4">1/4</span></div></div></div></div>
<p>In Part I, Naruto wore an orange and blue jacket with a white collar, a white swirl with a tassel on the left side, and a red Uzumaki crest on the back. He also wore orange pants with a shuriken holster on his right knee, blue sandals, and a blue <a href="/wiki/Forehead_protector" class="mw-redirect" title="Forehead protector">forehead protector</a>, given to him by Iruka after graduating from the Academy. In Part II, Naruto wears a more form fitting outfit after wearing out his original one while training with Jiraiya,<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> with a T-shirt or mesh armour underneath. While retaining the swirls and orange pants, the blue pieces of his outfit changes to black: his forehead protector (which is now longer), sandals, and orange jacket, the black colour showing more prominence than the blue did originally. During his battle with Pain, Naruto briefly wore a short-sleeved red coat with a black flame pattern around the hem and carried a large scroll on his back.
</p><p>Naruto lost his right arm after the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>, though it is later replaced by a fully manoeuvrable prosthetic arm made of <a href="/wiki/Hashirama_Senju" title="Hashirama Senju">Hashirama Senju</a>'s cells, wrapped completely in bandages. In <i><a href="/wiki/The_Last:_Naruto_the_Movie" title="The Last: Naruto the Movie">The Last: Naruto the Movie</a></i>, Naruto grew again to be one of the tallest of his graduating class, cut his hair short, and wore a black elastic forehead protector. Over his pants and sandals, he wears a black uniform jacket with an orange zipper and buttons on the waist and sleeves, which can be folded up at times. He has a red armband with an Uzumaki crest on his left arm. After becoming Hokage, Naruto dons a garment similar to his father's: a white cape that has a red flame pattern around the hem, is held together by a red rope, and has the kanji for "Seventh Hokage" (<span lang="ja">七代目火影</span>&#44; <i>Nanadaime Hokage</i>) written vertically down the back. Underneath this, he wears an orange sweatshirt with black stripes (reverse in the manga version of <i><a href="/wiki/Boruto:_Naruto_Next_Generations" title="Boruto: Naruto Next Generations">Boruto: Naruto Next Generations</a></i>), black pants and sandals. He occasionally wears the traditional <a href="/wiki/Hokage" title="Hokage">Hokage</a> headpiece, but has stopped wearing a forehead protector.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities">Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0a/Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png/revision/latest?cb=20160825112853" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Vs Kaguya" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Vs Kaguya.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0a/Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825112853" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0a/Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png/revision/latest?cb=20160825112853" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Vs Kaguya" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0a/Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825112853" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Vs Kaguya.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0a/Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825112853" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Vs_Kaguya.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's combined senjutsu and tailed beast influence over his trademark techniques.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Originally, Naruto was a rather inept ninja, failing to graduate from the <a href="/wiki/Academy" title="Academy">Academy</a> three times. Through sheer determination and training however, his skills rapidly improved to defeat strong <a href="/wiki/Genin" title="Genin">genin</a> like <a href="/wiki/Neji_Hy%C5%ABga" title="Neji Hyūga">Neji Hyūga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kabuto_Yakushi" title="Kabuto Yakushi">Kabuto Yakushi</a>, earning acknowledgement from all the <a href="/wiki/Sannin" title="Sannin">Sannin</a> for his potential.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Under various tutelage, Naruto was able to <a href="/wiki/Kakuzu" title="Kakuzu">defeat</a> <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">various members</a> of <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a>, ultimately earning praise from Konohagakure as a Hokage-material hero.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's personally defeated various reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Kage" title="Kage">Kage</a><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a> during the Fourth Shinobi World War,<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> with many believing he was the central key to winning the battle.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> By adulthood, his prowess made him the Seventh Hokage, regarded as the strongest shinobi in history<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> and having command of overwhelming <a href="/wiki/Jutsu" title="Jutsu">jutsu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> With the combined might of <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Uchiha" title="Sasuke Uchiha">Sasuke Uchiha</a>, noted as his only rival in power,<sup id="cite_ref-BorutoMovie_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorutoMovie-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> they are said to be able to destroy the world.<sup id="cite_ref-SS_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SS-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Together, they overpowered <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki">Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki</a> who <a href="/wiki/Chakra_Edible_Creation" title="Chakra Edible Creation">absorbed</a> <a href="/wiki/Kinshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki">Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki</a>, and pushed <a href="/wiki/Jigen" title="Jigen">Jigen</a>'s body to its limit. Overall, he could compete against if not defeat world-threatening opponents, such as <a href="/wiki/Obito_Uchiha" title="Obito Uchiha">Obito Uchiha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Madara_Uchiha" title="Madara Uchiha">Madara Uchiha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kaguya_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kaguya Ōtsutsuki">Kaguya Ōtsutsuki</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toneri_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Toneri Ōtsutsuki">Toneri Ōtsutsuki</a>, as well as fighting at his <a href="/wiki/Baryon_Mode" title="Baryon Mode">absolute peak</a> managed to overwhelm <a href="/wiki/Isshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Isshiki Ōtsutsuki">Isshiki Ōtsutsuki</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chakra_and_Physical_Prowess">Chakra and Physical Prowess</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png/revision/latest?cb=20140605131235" class="image"><img alt="Naruto gives Hinata power" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto gives Hinata power.png" data-image-key="Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140605131235" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png/revision/latest?cb=20140605131235" class="image"><img alt="Naruto gives Hinata power" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140605131235" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto gives Hinata power.png" data-image-key="Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140605131235" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_gives_Hinata_power.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto sharing Kurama's chakra through physical contact.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As an Uzumaki and a <a href="/wiki/Reincarnation" title="Reincarnation">reincarnation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Asura_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Asura Ōtsutsuki">Asura Ōtsutsuki</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-ch671_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch671-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Naruto has massive reserves of strong <a href="/wiki/Chakra" title="Chakra">chakra</a>. Even as a child, he had at least four times the amount of a seasoned <a href="/wiki/J%C5%8Dnin" title="Jōnin">Jōnin</a> like <a href="/wiki/Kakashi_Hatake" title="Kakashi Hatake">Kakashi Hatake</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-ch315_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch315-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> and described by <a href="/wiki/Karin" title="Karin">Karin</a> as "bright and warm".<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> His initial poor control of it was offset by his sheer reserves,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> which were large enough to endure three and a half days of constant battle against several powerful opponents. Only by the end of his battle against Sasuke did he show exhaustion, and even then could still fight to a standstill and eventual victory.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's control improved greatly over time; able to <a href="/wiki/Chakra_Transfer_Technique" title="Chakra Transfer Technique">transfer his chakra</a> to others,<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> and perform one-handed hand seals.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's powerful life-force grants him an extreme longevity, healing power, stamina, and vitality;<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> this allowed him to survive the extraction of a tailed beast, though he required aid from <a href="/wiki/Sakura_Haruno" title="Sakura Haruno">Sakura Haruno</a> to stay alive.<sup id="cite_ref-ch661_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch661-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Naruto also learned how to counter <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu" title="Genjutsu">genjutsu</a> from <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>, but his ability to do so is limited.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> In adulthood, Naruto's chakra is powerful enough to intimidate Kawaki into submission<sup id="cite_ref-BC26_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BC26-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> and destroy high-level barriers simply by releasing a burst of it.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He could repel <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru_Nara" title="Shikamaru Nara">Shikamaru Nara</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Imitation_Technique" title="Shadow Imitation Technique">Shadow Imitation Technique</a>, a feat that no one else could do.<sup id="cite_ref-SS_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SS-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> His chakra, when he combined it with his <a href="/wiki/Boruto_Uzumaki" title="Boruto Uzumaki">son's</a> <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Rasengan" title="Vanishing Rasengan">Vanishing Rasengan</a>, turned it into a gigantic <a href="/wiki/Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan">Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan</a> able to kill the <a href="/wiki/Chakra_Edible_Creation" title="Chakra Edible Creation">empowered</a> <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki">Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki</a> who tried to use a <a href="/wiki/Deep_Crimson_Spiral" title="Deep Crimson Spiral">copy</a> of the technique to defeat his.<sup id="cite_ref-BE65_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BE65-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> His chakra reserves were also so vast that he was able to overload <a href="/wiki/Delta" title="Delta">Delta</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Absorbing_Eye" title="Absorbing Eye">Absorbing Eye</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Super-Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Super-Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan">continuous</a> Rasengan-assault and still primed to defeat her.<sup id="cite_ref-BC33_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BC33-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c1/Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221063055" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s clones vs Gaara" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s clones vs Gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c1/Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221063055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c1/Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221063055" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s clones vs Gaara" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c1/Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221063055" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s clones vs Gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c1/Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221063055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_clones_vs_Gaara.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto attacking Gaara with his Naruto Uzumaki Two Thousand Combo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While naturally a short-range fighter, Naruto originally was inept at <a href="/wiki/Taijutsu" title="Taijutsu">taijutsu</a>, requiring unpredictable attacks to surprise combat experts like <a href="/wiki/Kiba_Inuzuka" title="Kiba Inuzuka">Kiba Inuzuka</a> and Neji Hyūga.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> He often utilised shadow clones in large if not massive numbers to simply overwhelm his foes.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Although these tactics resumed later, Naruto becomes much more adept at taijutsu due to Jiraiya's training.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Fukasaku" title="Fukasaku">Fukasaku</a>'s tutelage, he could fend off a pair of expert kenjutsu users.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Two years after the war, Naruto's taijutsu prowess could best dozens of opponents without shadow clones or enhancements.<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> As Hokage, his taijutsu could pressure Momoshiki after he had absorbed <a href="/wiki/Kinshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki">Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BE65_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BE65-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Naruto could even hold off Delta despite her <a href="/wiki/Shinobi-Ware" title="Shinobi-Ware">extreme body modifications</a>, ultimately controlling the pace of the battle to tire her out and gradually overwhelm her<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> to win despite being in the defensive.<sup id="cite_ref-BC33_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BC33-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> His speed had also increased to the point where he could effortlessly catch up with <a href="/wiki/Kawaki" title="Kawaki">Kawaki</a> after he tried to escape from Naruto.<sup id="cite_ref-BC26_76-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BC26-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Likewise, in the anime, he is proven very resilient, able to take a point-blank blast from Kawaki's modifications unfazed.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Body_Modifications">Body Modifications</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png/revision/latest?cb=20210111023937" class="image"><img alt="Shinobi Ware Absorption" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shinobi Ware Absorption.png" data-image-key="Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210111023937" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png/revision/latest?cb=20210111023937" class="image"><img alt="Shinobi Ware Absorption" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210111023937" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shinobi Ware Absorption.png" data-image-key="Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210111023937" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shinobi_Ware_Absorption.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's prototype Absorbing Hand.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After losing his right arm during his final battle with Sasuke, <a href="/wiki/Tsunade" title="Tsunade">Tsunade</a> cultured an artificial prosthesis for him using the cells of <a href="/wiki/Hashirama_Senju" title="Hashirama Senju">Hashirama Senju</a>. As his body and the prosthesis arms are only connected through his chakra itself he can easily remove and replace them.<sup id="cite_ref-B16P37_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-B16P37-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> After Momoshiki's defeat, Naruto took inspiration from his <a href="/wiki/Chakra_absorption_technique" class="mw-redirect" title="Chakra absorption technique">chakra absorption technique</a> and had <a href="/wiki/Katasuke_T%C5%8Dno" title="Katasuke Tōno">Katasuke Tōno</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Scientific_Ninja_Weapons_Team" title="Scientific Ninja Weapons Team">Scientific Ninja Weapons Team</a> modifiy the arm further with mechanical features. With it, Naruto is able to <a href="/wiki/Absorbing_Hand" title="Absorbing Hand">neutralise and even absorb</a> enemy techniques, though they have yet to replicate Momoshiki's ability to discharge them as a counterattack.<sup id="cite_ref-B16P37_89-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-B16P37-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Jinch.C5.ABriki_Transformations"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinchūriki_Transformations">Jinchūriki Transformations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms" title="Jinchūriki Forms">Jinchūriki Forms</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails_Chakra_Mode" title="Nine-Tails Chakra Mode">Nine-Tails Chakra Mode</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baryon_Mode" title="Baryon Mode">Baryon Mode</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/87/Version_1_form.png/revision/latest?cb=20150223122400" class="image"><img alt="Version 1 form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Version 1 form.png" data-image-key="Version_1_form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/87/Version_1_form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223122400" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/87/Version_1_form.png/revision/latest?cb=20150223122400" class="image"><img alt="Version 1 form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/87/Version_1_form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223122400" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Version 1 form.png" data-image-key="Version_1_form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/87/Version_1_form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223122400" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Version_1_form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Version 1 form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Originally as the <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kurama" title="Kurama">Kurama</a>'s Yang half, Naruto had access to massive reserves of exceptionally powerful chakra, which was at least a hundredfold greater than Kakashi's.<sup id="cite_ref-ch315_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch315-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> These chakra levels were increased even further when the Yin half of Kurama was reunited with the Yang half inside of Naruto. Due to his inheriting his <a href="/wiki/Kushina_Uzumaki" title="Kushina Uzumaki">mother</a>'s unique chakra capacities and being Kurama's jinchūriki for essentially his entire life, Naruto's chakra has properly mixed with the fox's,<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> allowing him to perform several chakra-taxing techniques unhindered. Originally, he could only access Kurama's chakra in times of great anger. It enhanced Naruto's abilities, but the fox's negative influence made Naruto more aggressive. While essentially remaining himself when accessing a <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms#Version_1" title="Jinchūriki Forms">Version 1</a> state, manifesting four tails would trigger <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms#Version_2" title="Jinchūriki Forms">Version 2</a> state, which made him lose control and would gradually turn into even more <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Control" title="Tailed Beast Control">feral</a> forms, requiring outside assistance to suppress Kurama's power and regain control, prompting him to avoid relying on the fox's power whenever possible. By the end of the Fourth Great Shinobi War, he could access his Version 1 form without any loss in his mentality.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_transforming.png/revision/latest?cb=20141026161814" class="image"><img alt="Naruto transforming" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto transforming.png" data-image-key="Naruto_transforming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_transforming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141026161814" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_transforming.png/revision/latest?cb=20141026161814" class="image"><img alt="Naruto transforming" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_transforming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141026161814" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto transforming.png" data-image-key="Naruto_transforming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_transforming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141026161814" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_transforming.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto transforming from his Nine-Tails Chakra Mode into his Kurama Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Realising he could not avoid using Kurama's power, Naruto sought to control it with help from <a href="/wiki/Killer_B" title="Killer B">Killer B</a>, a jinchūriki who had fully mastered the power of <a href="/wiki/Gy%C5%ABki" title="Gyūki">Gyūki</a>. Upon succeeding and taking most of Kurama's chakra, Naruto attained the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails_Chakra_Mode" title="Nine-Tails Chakra Mode">Nine-Tails Chakra Mode</a>, which greatly increased his physical parameters. Naruto can also detect <a href="/wiki/Negative_Emotions_Sensing" title="Negative Emotions Sensing">negative emotions</a> in this mode, and use <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Chakra_Arms" title="Tailed Beast Chakra Arms">Tailed Beast Chakra Arms</a> from any part of his body as he pleases, as well as form <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Ball" title="Tailed Beast Ball">Tailed Beast Balls</a> from them. As he didn't have Kurama's cooperation, Naruto needed to exercise extreme caution while using the form, as the chakra exchange could cost him his life. Eventually, when Kurama acknowledged Naruto's life-long strength of character and Naruto learned the fox's true name, their new-found friendship granted Naruto access to its <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails_Chakra_Mode#Kurama_Mode" title="Nine-Tails Chakra Mode">full power</a>, which further increased his physical parameters and with no drawbacks. This also increased his resilience to such degrees to the point where he could survive the <a href="/wiki/Ten-Tails" title="Ten-Tails">Ten-Tails</a>' <a href="/wiki/Tenpenchii" title="Tenpenchii">Tenpenchii</a> and endure Toneri's <a href="/wiki/Golden_Wheel_Reincarnation_Explosion" title="Golden Wheel Reincarnation Explosion">Golden Wheel Reincarnation Explosion</a> — which was able to cut the <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">Moon</a> in half — with no visible signs of damage. This cooperation of Kurama also provides Naruto with an immediate resistance from <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu" title="Genjutsu">genjutsu</a>. Two years later, he could <a href="/wiki/Kurama_Arm_Attack" title="Kurama Arm Attack">store</a> Kurama's chakra within his arm to deliver powerful punches capable of creating massive craters on the Moon and depower Toneri from his <a href="/wiki/Tenseigan_Chakra_Mode" title="Tenseigan Chakra Mode">Tenseigan Chakra Mode</a> to his normal state, as well as block the latter's Golden Wheel Reincarnation Explosion.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20150825070824" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s tailed beast mode" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s tailed beast mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150825070824" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20150825070824" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s tailed beast mode" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150825070824" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s tailed beast mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150825070824" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_tailed_beast_mode.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Tailed Beast Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Failing to transform into a replica of Kurama at first, Naruto instead achieved a <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Mode" class="mw-redirect" title="Tailed Beast Mode">Tailed Beast Mode</a> in the unique form of a life-sized transparent avatar of chakra. In it, he could create <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Ball" title="Tailed Beast Ball">Tailed Beast Balls</a> and revitalise the life-forces of any he touches physically or with the avatar,<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> heal nearly any wounds,<sup id="cite_ref-BorutoMovie_38-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorutoMovie-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> or grant them temporarily chakra-cloaks.<sup id="cite_ref-ch651_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch651-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> After he became the jinchūriki of Kurama's complete self, Naruto is able to manifest the demon fox outside himself for a period akin to summoning, allowing both to fight as separate entities. During the endgame of the Fourth Shinobi World War, Naruto received chakra from the other tailed beasts,<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> which greatly increased his chakra reserves even further and allowed him to access their unique abilities himself, such as <a href="/wiki/Shukaku" title="Shukaku">Shukaku</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sand" title="Sand">sand</a> manipulation, <a href="/wiki/Saiken" title="Saiken">Saiken</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Soap_Bubble_Ninjutsu" title="Soap Bubble Ninjutsu">soap bubble ninjutsu</a> and ability to emit <a href="/wiki/Wisdom_Wolf_Decay" title="Wisdom Wolf Decay">corrosive liquids</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dmei" title="Chōmei">Chōmei</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Scale_Powder" title="Scale Powder">scale powder</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Gy%C5%ABki" title="Gyūki">Gyūki</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ink_Creation" title="Ink Creation">ink creation</a>, and infuse them into his own <a href="/wiki/Sage_Art:_Super_Tailed_Beast_Rasenshuriken" title="Sage Art: Super Tailed Beast Rasenshuriken">techniques</a>. With the infusion of all nine of the tailed beasts' respective chakra inside of him, Naruto has become a medium to connect all the tailed beasts to communicate with each other<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> and made him a human pillar for the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Senjutsu" title="Six Paths Senjutsu">power of the Ten-Tails</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/17/Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20210926184438" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Baryon Mode" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Baryon Mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/17/Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210926184438" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/17/Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20210926184438" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Baryon Mode" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/17/Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210926184438" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Baryon Mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/17/Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210926184438" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_Baryon_Mode.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Baryon Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the most dire of situations, Naruto is able to access a deep level of Kurama's power, <a href="/wiki/Baryon_Mode" title="Baryon Mode">Baryon Mode</a>. In this state, his facial features become even more akin to Kurama with nine blazing chakra tails which he can use in a similar manner to Tailed Beast Chakra Arms to catch and bind opponents or objects and <a href="/wiki/Baryon_Tail_Breaker" title="Baryon Tail Breaker">deflect attacks</a>. He also displayed the ability to use these chakra tails to form a protective shield around something or someone.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> In a process similar to <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuclear_fusion" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nuclear fusion">nuclear fusion</a>, Naruto's and <a href="/wiki/Kurama" title="Kurama">Kurama</a>'s chakra are consumed as raw materials to produce a new type of energy. When in use, it dramatically boosts Naruto's reflexes, raw might, and chakra to such extreme levels, able to surpass Isshiki's capabilities. Because all chakra is connected, the same power that is produced from bits of their lives also work to reduce the lifespan of opponents on contact. Due to its extreme energy consumption, Naruto must remain focused and not waste energy on extraneous thoughts and actions, to maximise the amount of time he can maintain Baryon Mode.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> The drawback of this form is the high chance of death for Kurama from the extreme strain of this form. Upon Kurama's death from this form, while Naruto was spared the same fate, he lost access to all of Kurama's chakra and abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ninjutsu">Ninjutsu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6a/Summoning_Technique.png/revision/latest?cb=20150120115239" class="image"><img alt="Summoning Technique" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Summoning Technique.png" data-image-key="Summoning_Technique.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6a/Summoning_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150120115239" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6a/Summoning_Technique.png/revision/latest?cb=20150120115239" class="image"><img alt="Summoning Technique" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6a/Summoning_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150120115239" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Summoning Technique.png" data-image-key="Summoning_Technique.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6a/Summoning_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150120115239" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Summoning_Technique.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto using the Summoning Technique.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the Academy, the <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Technique" title="Sexy Technique">Sexy Technique</a> was the only technique that Naruto could perform successfully, which had no practical use other than to shock people. Later, he learned more advanced and useful ninjutsu from <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>. This included <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Technique" title="Summoning Technique">summoning</a> <a href="/wiki/Toads" class="mw-redirect" title="Toads">toads</a> from Mount Myōboku to assist him, and use them to <a href="/wiki/Summoning:_Food_Cart_Destroyer_Technique" title="Summoning: Food Cart Destroyer Technique">crush</a> enemies from above. He became skilled in <a href="/wiki/Shurikenjutsu" title="Shurikenjutsu">shurikenjutsu</a>, able to throw weapons quickly and with precision.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's repertoire expanded to <a href="/wiki/F%C5%ABinjutsu" title="Fūinjutsu">fūinjutsu</a>, where he could <a href="/wiki/Enclosing_Technique" title="Enclosing Technique">store</a> his weapons within scrolls. His fūinjutsu was further increased upon receiving <a href="/wiki/Gerotora" title="Gerotora">Gerotora</a> near the start of the Fourth Shinobi World War.<sup id="cite_ref-ch499_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch499-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, Jiraiya taught Naruto <a href="/wiki/Cooperation_ninjutsu" class="mw-redirect" title="Cooperation ninjutsu">cooperation ninjutsu</a>, combining his techniques with others to create an even more powerful one.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> The collaboration techniques he performed with other individuals typically utilised his own elemental affinity, such as the <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Water_Vortex_Technique" title="Typhoon Water Vortex Technique">Typhoon Water Vortex Technique</a> with <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Toad_Gun" title="Wind Release: Toad Gun">Wind Release: Toad Gun</a> with <a href="/wiki/Gamatatsu" title="Gamatatsu">Gamatatsu</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Scorch_Release:_Halo_Hurricane_Jet_Black_Arrow_Style_Zero" title="Scorch Release: Halo Hurricane Jet Black Arrow Style Zero">Scorch Release: Halo Hurricane Jet Black Arrow Style Zero</a> with Sasuke. He also learned from <a href="/wiki/Asuma_Sarutobi" title="Asuma Sarutobi">Asuma Sarutobi</a> to <a href="/wiki/Chakra_Flow" title="Chakra Flow">flow</a> chakra into his weapons to increase their offensive might.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, by adulthood, Naruto became able to use the <a href="/wiki/Shuriken_Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Shuriken Shadow Clone Technique">Shuriken Shadow Clone Technique</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> and also showed some proficiency with bōjutsu.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shadow_Clone_Technique">Shadow Clone Technique</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221104302" class="image"><img alt="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique.png" data-image-key="Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221104302" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221104302" class="image"><img alt="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221104302" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique.png" data-image-key="Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221104302" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto using the Multiple Shadow Clone Technique.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><span class="box headnote ultisup-image-popup"><i>See also: <a href="/wiki/Special:RunQuery/Image_query?Image_query%5Bcharacters%5D=Naruto&amp;Image_query%5Bjutsu%5D=Shadow%20Clone%20Technique&amp;wpRunQuery=true" title="Images of Naruto using Shadow Clone Technique" target="_self">Images of Naruto using Shadow Clone Technique</a></i></span>
Naruto's first trademark technique was the <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Shadow Clone Technique">Shadow Clone Technique</a>. While originally failing constantly with a basic illusionary clone, after briefly studying the <a href="/wiki/Scroll_of_Seals" title="Scroll of Seals">Scroll of Seals</a>, he learned to create shadow clones on a <a href="/wiki/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique">mass scale</a>. From then on, Naruto's skill with shadow clones blossomed to great heights. Having unusually high chakra reserves, Naruto could use this technique to create hundreds of shadow clones and retain large amounts of chakra in each one with relative ease.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> He could use them to outnumber or deceive his enemies, manoeuvre himself in mid-air, transform into weapons, scout areas, or test an opponent's abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> During his elemental-affinity training, learning that the original will gain all the knowledge and conditioning of a shadow clone right after it dispersed. From this, Naruto can use his mass scale of clones to drastically speed up his training to gain years worth of experience in just days. By the time he became Hokage, Naruto's usage of this technique on mass-scale and prolonged-periods allowed him to constantly perform multiple simultaneous tasks throughout the village daily, although he does have a tendency to overexert himself, leaving him exhausted afterwards.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rasengan">Rasengan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d6/Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png/revision/latest?cb=20191003092311" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Rasengan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Rasengan.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d6/Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191003092311" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d6/Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png/revision/latest?cb=20191003092311" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Rasengan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d6/Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191003092311" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Rasengan.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d6/Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191003092311" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_Rasengan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto using the Rasengan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto's second trademark technique is the <a href="/wiki/Rasengan" title="Rasengan">Rasengan</a>. Originally, due to his poor chakra control, Naruto had to use a shadow clone to form the spherical shape while he provided the chakra. Over time, Naruto developed <a href="/wiki/Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Big Ball Rasengan">larger</a> <a href="/wiki/Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan">versions</a> of the Rasengan and learned how to perform it faster.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> During the Fourth Shinobi World War, he learned to use the Rasengan and its variants unaided with a single hand, or even form one in both hands simultaneously.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> He also increased the size of his standard Rasengan.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Naruto had also shown the ability to release the Rasengan as an energy wave,<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> or as a projectile in the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Using senjutsu or Kurama's chakra, Naruto can create <a href="/wiki/Sage_Technique:_Spiralling_Serial_Spheres" class="mw-redirect" title="Sage Technique: Spiralling Serial Spheres">more</a> <a href="/wiki/Spiralling_Strife_Spheres" title="Spiralling Strife Spheres">powerful</a> and <a href="/wiki/Spiralling_Absorption_Sphere" title="Spiralling Absorption Sphere">elaborate</a> <a href="/wiki/Planetary_Rasengan" title="Planetary Rasengan">variations</a> of the Rasengan; using the latter, he even developed the <a href="/wiki/Super_Mini-Tailed_Beast_Ball" title="Super Mini-Tailed Beast Ball">Super Mini-Tailed Beast Ball</a>, performing it in a similar manner to the Rasengan. In the anime, usage of his tailed beast chakra also allows him to instantly perform massive Rasengan without the aid of his hands and launch in quick successions, similar to a <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Ball" title="Tailed Beast Ball">Tailed Beast Ball</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nature_Transformation">Nature Transformation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png/revision/latest?cb=20150813115318" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Creating Lava Rasenshuriken" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Creating Lava Rasenshuriken.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813115318" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png/revision/latest?cb=20150813115318" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Creating Lava Rasenshuriken" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813115318" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Creating Lava Rasenshuriken.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813115318" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Creating_Lava_Rasenshuriken.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto simultaneously using Wind and Lava Release.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto's natural affinity is <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release" title="Wind Release">Wind Release</a>. Using shadow clones, one to form the Rasengan while another infuses the Wind chakra, Naruto could complete difficult task of producing a Rasengan that is the pinnacle of shape and nature transformation, something no one before him could accomplish, including Kakashi and his father. Once adjusting to using the <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Rasengan" title="Wind Release: Rasengan">Wind Release: Rasengan</a> he could expand upon it to produce the <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Rasenshuriken" title="Wind Release: Rasenshuriken">Wind Release: Rasenshuriken</a>. He also created <a href="/wiki/Mini-Rasenshuriken" title="Mini-Rasenshuriken">different</a>-<a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasenshuriken" title="Wind Release: Ultra-Big Ball Rasenshuriken">sized</a> <a href="/wiki/Big_Ball_Rasenshuriken" title="Big Ball Rasenshuriken">variations</a>, and could even use <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Repeated_Rasenshuriken" title="Wind Release: Repeated Rasenshuriken">two Rasenshuriken</a> simultaneously. Two years after its creation, he became skilled enough to form a Rasenshuriken without any shadow clones and throw it in his base form,<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> a feat which he previously could only do while using his enhanced modes. 
</p><p>After gaining the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Senjutsu" title="Six Paths Senjutsu">Six Paths Senjutsu</a>, Naruto can utilise all basic five nature transformations, as well as <a href="/wiki/Yin%E2%80%93Yang_Release" title="Yin–Yang Release">Yin–Yang Release</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> He could make perfect use of the latter to revitalise life-forces, heal whomever he touches, and restore missing organs.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> After gaining chakra from the respective tailed beasts, Naruto can also use <a href="/wiki/Shukaku" title="Shukaku">Shukaku</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Magnet_Release" title="Magnet Release">Magnet Release</a>, <a href="/wiki/Son_Gok%C5%AB" title="Son Gokū">Son Gokū</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lava_Release" title="Lava Release">Lava Release</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Koku%C5%8D" title="Kokuō">Kokuō</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Boil_Release" title="Boil Release">Boil Release</a>, able to infuse any of the other elements into is normal techniques as seamlessly as with Wind chakra. Having an arm made from Hashirama's cells, Naruto has a possibility to use <a href="/wiki/Wood_Release" title="Wood Release">Wood Release</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senjutsu">Senjutsu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/dc/Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20150124180545" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Sage Mode" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Sage Mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/dc/Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150124180545" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/dc/Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20150124180545" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Sage Mode" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/dc/Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150124180545" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Sage Mode.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/dc/Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150124180545" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_Sage_Mode.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Sage Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto later trained in <a href="/wiki/Senjutsu" title="Senjutsu">senjutsu</a> at Mount Myōboku, which was only possible due to his high chakra reserves. Unlike <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>, he was able to perfectly balance <a href="/wiki/Natural_energy" class="mw-redirect" title="Natural energy">natural energy</a> with his chakra, and enter a complete <a href="/wiki/Sage_Mode" title="Sage Mode">Sage Mode</a>, symbolised by the orange pigmentation around his yellow eyes, his toad-like pupils, and no other alterations to his appearance. Using Sage Mode made Naruto's techniques stronger, enhanced his physical parameters,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> utilise the <a href="/wiki/Frog_Kata" title="Frog Kata">Frog Kata</a> taijutsu style,<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Sensing_Technique" title="Sensing Technique">sense</a> chakra through advanced enough to identify different signatures from vast distances.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Since <a href="/wiki/Fukasaku" title="Fukasaku">Fukasaku</a> was unable to <a href="/wiki/Sage_Art:_Amphibian_Technique" title="Sage Art: Amphibian Technique">fuse</a> with Naruto and gather natural energy for him due to Kurama's interference, Naruto had to employ shadow clones instead to maintain the technique, taking advantage of the clones' own buildup of natural energy being transferred to the original and let him use <a href="/wiki/Sage_Mode" title="Sage Mode">Sage Mode</a> a number of times. However, creating more than five shadow clones overall would disrupt the focus of the clones gathering natural energy. The need for this method diminishes over time as Naruto became capable of entering Sage Mode much faster.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> However, after finding unity with <a href="/wiki/Kurama" title="Kurama">Kurama</a>, Naruto overcame this problem and learned to combine Sage Mode with Kurama's chakra to further enhance his abilities, such that he could resist <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">Nagato</a>'s control and shatter <a href="/wiki/Truth-Seeking_Ball" title="Truth-Seeking Ball">Truth-Seeking Balls</a>. In later years, having drawn experience from his various events, Naruto became able to maintain Sage Mode for much longer durations unaided.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Six_Paths_Senjutsu">Six Paths Senjutsu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Senjutsu" title="Six Paths Senjutsu">Six Paths Senjutsu</a></span>
Naruto also gained access to the <b>Six Paths Senjutsu</b> (<span lang="ja">六道仙術</span>&#44; <i>Rikudō Senjutsu</i>), which allows him to fly and also manifest up to nine <a href="/wiki/Truth-Seeking_Ball" title="Truth-Seeking Ball">Truth-Seeking Balls</a>, composed of all five basic <a href="/wiki/Nature" class="mw-redirect" title="Nature">natures</a>, use Yin–Yang Release, and imbue them with the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Chakra" class="mw-redirect" title="Six Paths Chakra">Six Paths Chakra</a>. He can mould the balls into a myriad of shapes, fire them as projectiles and still control them from distance, or convert them into Tailed Beast Balls and use them to create <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Ball_Rasenshuriken" title="Tailed Beast Ball Rasenshuriken">Tailed Beast Ball Rasenshurikens</a> capable of destroying the planetoids generated from <a href="/wiki/Chibaku_Tensei" title="Chibaku Tensei">Chibaku Tensei</a>. While his shadow clones are unable to produce Truth-Seeking Balls of their own, Naruto is able to transfer control of his own to any of his shadow clones.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Six_Paths_Sage_Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Sage_Mode" title="Six Paths Sage Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/22/Naruto%27s_SPSM.png/revision/latest?cb=20150730222303" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s SPSM" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s SPSM.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_SPSM.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/22/Naruto%27s_SPSM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150730222303" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/22/Naruto%27s_SPSM.png/revision/latest?cb=20150730222303" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s SPSM" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/22/Naruto%27s_SPSM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150730222303" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s SPSM.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_SPSM.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/22/Naruto%27s_SPSM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150730222303" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_SPSM.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Six Paths Sage Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With the power given to him by <a href="/wiki/Hagoromo_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki">Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki</a>, Naruto gained access to the <b><a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Sage_Mode" title="Six Paths Sage Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</a></b> (<span lang="ja">六道仙人モード</span>&#44; <i>Rikudō Sennin Mōdo</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-d4_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-d4-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In this mode, his pupils take on a cross-like shape — without manifesting the orange pigmentation around his eyes present in Sage Mode. Going further, Naruto donned a new Nine-Tails Chakra Mode cloak, which he could access instantly and maintain much longer than his standard Sage Mode.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Naruto's physical attributes and techniques are further augmented,<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> to the point where he could dodge <a href="/wiki/Sage_Art:_Storm_Release_Light_Fang" title="Sage Art: Storm Release Light Fang">attacks</a> that moved at the speed of light and deflect Truth-Seeking Balls. It also empowers his sensory abilities to the highest possible level,<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> which allowed him to sense the <a href="/wiki/Limbo:_Border_Jail" title="Limbo: Border Jail">invisible shadows</a> of Limbo.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Asura_Kurama_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20160929122359" class="image"><img alt="Asura Kurama Mode" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Asura Kurama Mode.png" data-image-key="Asura_Kurama_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Asura_Kurama_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929122359" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Asura_Kurama_Mode.png/revision/latest?cb=20160929122359" class="image"><img alt="Asura Kurama Mode" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Asura_Kurama_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929122359" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Asura Kurama Mode.png" data-image-key="Asura_Kurama_Mode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Asura_Kurama_Mode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929122359" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Asura_Kurama_Mode.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's Asura Kurama Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto also retained use of his Tailed Beast Mode avatar of Kurama, which rivalled Sasuke's Rinnegan-empowered <a href="/wiki/Susanoo" title="Susanoo">Complete Body — Susanoo</a> in size and power.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> Using two shadow clones, he could create and combine three Kurama avatars into a single construct with three faces and six arms, which is largely reminiscent of Asura's <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths:_Kunitsukami" title="Six Paths: Kunitsukami">Six Paths: Kunitsukami</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> This state allowed Naruto to infuse <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths:_Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasenshuriken" title="Six Paths: Ultra-Big Ball Rasenshuriken">two massive Rasenshuriken</a> with natural energy whose destructive capabilities rivalled that of Sasuke's most powerful jutsu, <a href="/wiki/Indra%27s_Arrow" title="Indra&#39;s Arrow">Indra's Arrow</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths:_Shinra_Tenky%C5%8D" title="Six Paths: Shinra Tenkyō">resulting explosion</a> from the two techniques colliding created an enormous cyclone that was visible from outer space.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Intelligence">Intelligence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Naruto%27s_intelligence.png/revision/latest?cb=20150220083928" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s intelligence" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s intelligence.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_intelligence.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Naruto%27s_intelligence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083928" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Naruto%27s_intelligence.png/revision/latest?cb=20150220083928" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s intelligence" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Naruto%27s_intelligence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083928" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s intelligence.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_intelligence.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Naruto%27s_intelligence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083928" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_intelligence.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto reveals himself after disguising as a Wind Release: Rasenshuriken.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While headstrong and often acting without thinking, Naruto's years as a prankster had given him a cunning imagination that was useful in split-second decision making, which has repeatedly proved invaluable in battle. He is a remarkable <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kinesthetic_learning" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kinesthetic learning">tactile learner</a>, able to learn better through executing a task rather than understanding the theory of it.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ch409_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch409-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Jiraiya also considered him to have a good gambling instinct.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> Once seen in action, even the likes of the Second Hokage revise their thoughts about Naruto's intellect and instinct in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> After meeting Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki, Naruto gained the innate ability to grasp the nature of chakra and comprehend all universal things,<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> allowing him to quickly master the new powers he received. By adulthood he had become a capable teacher, instructing students at Konoha's <a href="/wiki/Ninja_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Ninja Academy">Ninja Academy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> During his fight with <a href="/wiki/Delta" title="Delta">Delta</a>, Naruto showed his ability to think ahead by hiding his power and faking defeat in order to make Delta drop her guard and reveal her plans, although Delta was perceptive enough to see through his attempts. Naruto ultimately was able to find out the weakness of Delta's <a href="/wiki/Shinobi-Ware" title="Shinobi-Ware">Shinobi-Ware</a> absorbing eye and overtax it after seeing it in action repeatedly.<sup id="cite_ref-BC33_79-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BC33-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Naruto's most famous mental skill is to deceive his opponents, as he made effective use of even the most <a href="/wiki/Transformation_Technique" title="Transformation Technique">simple techniques</a> to trick the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_of_Pain" title="Six Paths of Pain">deadliest of opponents</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> He could formulate multi-step plans or backup plans in the thick of battle,<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> and act quickly even when given new information.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> He can also seemingly make himself predictable by creating a pattern, only to throw off his opponent by breaking it. He has even thrown in what others would call <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Reverse_Harem_Technique" title="Sexy Reverse Harem Technique">completely useless techniques</a> at <a href="/wiki/Kaguya_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kaguya Ōtsutsuki">powerful opponents</a> to create an opening for a counterattack.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> Naruto is rather observant, able to notice details others may overlook and subsequently take advantage of them to overcome his opponents.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> As an adult, Naruto proved to be a capable teacher in ninjutsu, quickly teaching the basics to <a href="/wiki/Kawaki" title="Kawaki">Kawaki</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Part_I">Part I</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span class="box headnote"><i>See also: <a href="/wiki/Plot_of_Naruto" title="Plot of Naruto">Plot of Naruto</a></i></span>
</p>
<h3><span id="Prologue_.E2.80.94_Land_of_Waves"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Prologue_—_Land_of_Waves">Prologue — Land of Waves</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Prologue_%E2%80%94_Land_of_Waves" title="Prologue — Land of Waves">Prologue — Land of Waves</a></span>
</p>
