<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Iruka_protects_naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150504035704" class="image"><img alt="Iruka protects naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Iruka protects naruto.png" data-image-key="Iruka_protects_naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Iruka_protects_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150504035704" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Iruka_protects_naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150504035704" class="image"><img alt="Iruka protects naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Iruka_protects_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150504035704" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Iruka protects naruto.png" data-image-key="Iruka_protects_naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d8/Iruka_protects_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150504035704" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Iruka_protects_naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto is protected by Iruka.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Failing once again to graduate from the <a href="/wiki/Academy" title="Academy">Academy</a>, a disappointed Naruto is advised by one of his instructors, <a href="/wiki/Mizuki" title="Mizuki">Mizuki</a>, to steal the <a href="/wiki/Scroll_of_Seals" title="Scroll of Seals">Scroll of Seals</a> and learn a technique from it in order to graduate. As Naruto struggled to learn the <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Shadow Clone Technique">Shadow Clone Technique</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iruka_Umino" title="Iruka Umino">Iruka Umino</a> tracked him down and realised that Naruto was tricked by Mizuki into stealing the scroll. Mizuki attacked them and told Naruto about the Nine-Tails sealed within him, claiming that Iruka hated him because of it. When Iruka risked his life to protect Naruto, however, he saw through Mizuki's lies and used the <a href="/wiki/Multiple_Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Multiple Shadow Clone Technique">Multiple Shadow Clone Technique</a> to defeat him, prompting Iruka to happily grant Naruto his graduation from the Academy. Naruto would later befriend <a href="/wiki/Konohamaru_Sarutobi" title="Konohamaru Sarutobi">Konohamaru Sarutobi</a>, grandson of the <a href="/wiki/Third_Hokage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Hokage">Third Hokage</a>, and teach him several perverted or useful techniques.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/50/Team_Kakashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20161219035928" class="image"><img alt="Team Kakashi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="148" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Team Kakashi.png" data-image-key="Team_Kakashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/50/Team_Kakashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161219035928" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/50/Team_Kakashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20161219035928" class="image"><img alt="Team Kakashi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/50/Team_Kakashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161219035928" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="148" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Team Kakashi.png" data-image-key="Team_Kakashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/50/Team_Kakashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161219035928" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Team_Kakashi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Team 7's group photo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto was eventually assigned to <a href="/wiki/Team_Kakashi" class="mw-redirect" title="Team Kakashi">Team 7</a>, partnered with <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Uchiha" title="Sasuke Uchiha">Sasuke Uchiha</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sakura_Haruno" title="Sakura Haruno">Sakura Haruno</a> under the leadership of <a href="/wiki/Kakashi_Hatake" title="Kakashi Hatake">Kakashi Hatake</a>. During their first meeting, Naruto shared his love of ramen, his hobbies, and his dream to become Hokage. To test their qualifications, Kakashi gave the team a <a href="/wiki/Bell_test" class="mw-redirect" title="Bell test">bell test</a>, stating that whichever of the three takes one of the two bells on his person will officially become <a href="/wiki/Genin" title="Genin">genin</a>. Instead of hiding like Sakura and Sasuke, Naruto tried to take the bells from Kakashi by force, only to be easily defeated, hung upside-down from a tree and tied to a wooden post in an attempt to steal lunch. After Sakura and Sasuke fail as well, Kakashi explains that the goal of the test was to use teamwork, to do together what none of them could do by themselves. He is persuaded to allow them to try again after lunch, but instructs Sasuke and Sakura not to feed Naruto. They feed him anyway, needing him in top-form if they're to work together. Kakashi sees this and, because they care more about the team than listening to his instructions, allows them all to pass.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png/revision/latest?cb=20151204035743" class="image"><img alt="Zabuza Vs Genin" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zabuza Vs Genin.png" data-image-key="Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151204035743" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png/revision/latest?cb=20151204035743" class="image"><img alt="Zabuza Vs Genin" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151204035743" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zabuza Vs Genin.png" data-image-key="Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151204035743" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zabuza_Vs_Genin.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke team up against Zabuza.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After a series of uneventful <a href="/wiki/D-rank" title="D-rank">D-rank</a> missions, Naruto is able to secure a <a href="/wiki/C-rank" title="C-rank">C-rank</a> mission for Team 7: escorting <a href="/wiki/Tazuna" title="Tazuna">Tazuna</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Waves" title="Land of Waves">Land of Waves</a>. Soon after leaving Konoha, they are attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Demon_Brothers" title="Demon Brothers">Demon Brothers</a>. Naruto is paralysed with fear, forcing Sasuke to step in to disarm them and protect Tazuna until Kakashi can capture them. Tazuna confesses that assassins have been hired to kill him but that he couldn't afford the bodyguard detail he needs. Although the mission is now <a href="/wiki/A-rank" title="A-rank">A-rank</a> in nature - far beyond the skill of genin - Team 7 decides to continue with it. Angered by Sasuke's taunting of him, Naruto cuts his hand to bleed out the poison he received earlier, vowing to never waver again. When they arrive in the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Waves" title="Land of Waves">Land of Waves</a> and are confronted by <a href="/wiki/Zabuza_Momochi" title="Zabuza Momochi">Zabuza Momochi</a>, Naruto is overwhelmed by the battle between Kakashi and Zabuza before he is knocked aside by Zabuza's <a href="/wiki/Water_clone" class="mw-redirect" title="Water clone">water clone</a>. Remembering his vow, Naruto regained his confidence and teamed up with Sasuke to free Kakashi from Zabuza's <a href="/wiki/Water_Prison" class="mw-redirect" title="Water Prison">Water Prison</a>. In the end, Zabuza is seemingly killed by <a href="/wiki/Haku" title="Haku">Haku</a>, allowing Team 7 to escort Tazuna back to his house.
</p><p>Kakashi finds Zabuza's death suspicious and decides to train the team in case he returns. He has them perform the <a href="/wiki/Tree_Climbing_Practice" title="Tree Climbing Practice">Tree Climbing Practice</a> to improve their chakra control, which will help them against Zabuza. Naruto becomes frustrated after several failures and asks for advice from Sakura, who herself mastered it from the start. Now rapidly improving, Naruto competes with Sasuke to finish the training, each determined to outdo the other. One day, Naruto encounters Haku (albeit unaware of his true identity) and they each discussed their dreams and desire to protect those precious to them. After Haku leaves, Naruto finishes the training with Sasuke but is left exhausted, so Team 7 leaves him behind the next morning as they resume their escort duties. Naruto awakens and arrives to assist Team 7 in fighting Zabuza and Haku, but, unaware of how Haku's <a href="/wiki/Demonic_Mirroring_Ice_Crystals" title="Demonic Mirroring Ice Crystals">Demonic Mirroring Ice Crystals</a> work, he joins Sasuke within the prison.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003120339" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Holds Sasuke" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Holds Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120339" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003120339" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Holds Sasuke" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120339" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Holds Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120339" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Holds_Sasuke.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's first use of the Nine-Tails' chakra.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto cannot break free with his shadow clones and Sasuke cannot melt the ice with his fire. As Haku moves in to kill Naruto, Sasuke uses his body as a shield to protect Naruto and seemingly dies. Enraged by Sasuke's apparent death, Naruto unwittingly accesses the <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms#Initial_Jinchūriki_Form" title="Jinchūriki Forms">Nine-Tails' chakra</a> for the first time, allowing him to destroy the ice mirrors and defeat Haku, breaking his mask. Realising his opponent was the boy he met before, Naruto calms himself. He is asked by Haku to kill him, since he feels of no further use to Zabuza. Before Naruto can do so, Haku immediately stops him and goes off to save Zabuza from being killed by Kakashi, sacrificing his own life. When Zabuza refuses to appreciate this, Naruto angrily scolds him, stating that Haku gave up his life to save someone precious to him. Touched by his words, Zabuza, using Naruto's kunai, killed Gatō and many of his henchmen before he himself dies. Sasuke soon awakens, and when their injuries heal, Team 7 leaves for home via Tazuna's newly-constructed <a href="/wiki/Great_Naruto_Bridge" title="Great Naruto Bridge">Great Naruto Bridge</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Ch.C5.ABnin_Exams"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Chūnin_Exams">Chūnin Exams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%ABnin_Exams_(Arc)" title="Chūnin Exams (Arc)">Chūnin Exams</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/34/Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20230223212339" class="image"><img alt="Naruto refuses to give up" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto refuses to give up.png" data-image-key="Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/34/Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223212339" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/34/Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20230223212339" class="image"><img alt="Naruto refuses to give up" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/34/Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223212339" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto refuses to give up.png" data-image-key="Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/34/Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223212339" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_refuses_to_give_up.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto refuses to give up from the Chūnin Exams.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Team 7 resumes its series of unremarkable missions. For their performance in the Land of Waves, however, Kakashi decides to enter them in the <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%ABnin_Exams" title="Chūnin Exams">Chūnin Exams</a> taking place in Konoha, which greatly excites Naruto. Because they've only recently graduated from the Academy, the three feel they must give strong showings to prove themselves. When they enter the exam hall, the team is met by <a href="/wiki/Rock_Lee" title="Rock Lee">Rock Lee</a>, who challenges Sasuke to a fight; Naruto tries to attack Lee in jealousy, but is easily swept aside. The fight is interrupted by <a href="/wiki/Might_Guy" title="Might Guy">Might Guy</a>, after which Naruto notes that the bandages around Lee's arms signify his arduous taijutsu training while also mocking Sasuke for his unability to best Lee.
</p><p>During the exam's first stage, the participating genin are given a written test, the goal of which is to cheat without getting caught. Unaware of this, Naruto struggles to answer the questions, so <a href="/wiki/Hinata_Hy%C5%ABga" title="Hinata Hyūga">Hinata Hyūga</a>, who is seated next to him, offers to let him copy off her paper. Despite the temptation, Naruto declined Hinata's offer, claiming that he isn't the type to cheat and that they might be disqualified if they are caught. Before the tenth question can be given, the genin are presented with the opportunity to forfeit; Naruto refuses to do so, declaring his refusal to give up and his goal to still become Hokage. His determination to face the tenth question despite the potential consequences inspires the rest of the genin to do the same, and so they pass the first stage. It is later noted that he was the only one to hand in a blank sheet, though this did not prevent him from passing.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f4/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20230223221356" class="image"><img alt="Naruto saves Sasuke from Orochimaru" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto saves Sasuke from Orochimaru.png" data-image-key="Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f4/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223221356" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f4/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20230223221356" class="image"><img alt="Naruto saves Sasuke from Orochimaru" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f4/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223221356" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto saves Sasuke from Orochimaru.png" data-image-key="Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f4/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230223221356" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Orochimaru.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto saves Sasuke from Orochimaru's snake.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>For the second phase, teams enter the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Death" class="mw-redirect" title="Forest of Death">Forest of Death</a> with the objective of obtaining a set of two scrolls, one of which they are given at the start. Naruto becomes separated from his team and is attacked and swallowed by a giant snake. He manages to kill it and regroups with his frightened teammates against <a href="/wiki/Orochimaru" title="Orochimaru">Orochimaru</a>. Angered by Sasuke's sudden cowardice and resignation, Naruto engages Orochimaru using the Nine-Tails' chakra, defeats his giant snake, and taunts Sasuke before Orochimaru <a href="/wiki/Five_Element_Seal" class="mw-redirect" title="Five Element Seal">suppresses</a> the Nine-Tails' chakra, rendering Naruto unconscious. After he awakens, Team 7 continues its search for the second scroll, which they eventually gain by defeating <a href="/wiki/Team_Oboro" title="Team Oboro">Team Oboro</a>, allowing them to pass the second stage.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b5/Uzumakirendan.png/revision/latest?cb=20140620064333" class="image"><img alt="Uzumakirendan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Uzumakirendan.png" data-image-key="Uzumakirendan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b5/Uzumakirendan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620064333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b5/Uzumakirendan.png/revision/latest?cb=20140620064333" class="image"><img alt="Uzumakirendan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b5/Uzumakirendan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620064333" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Uzumakirendan.png" data-image-key="Uzumakirendan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b5/Uzumakirendan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620064333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Uzumakirendan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats Kiba.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the preliminary matches of the exam, Naruto was pitted against <a href="/wiki/Kiba_Inuzuka" title="Kiba Inuzuka">Kiba Inuzuka</a> and his dog, <a href="/wiki/Akamaru" title="Akamaru">Akamaru</a>. Believing the match to be an easy victory, Kiba and Akamaru overwhelmed Naruto with many high-speed attacks, so Naruto tricks Kiba into knocking Akamaru out of the fight by using the <a href="/wiki/Transformation_Technique" title="Transformation Technique">Transformation Technique</a>, shocking all spectators. Naruto then disorients Kiba by farting in his face and defeats him with the <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Uzumaki_Combo" title="Naruto Uzumaki Combo">Naruto Uzumaki Combo</a> (which he invented from watching Sasuke's <a href="/wiki/Lion_Combo" title="Lion Combo">Lion Combo</a>). When Neji and Hinata's match begins, Naruto is enraged by Neji's ruthless tirade against Hinata and cheers Hinata on to defeat Neji. Although Hinata is defeated, Naruto wipes up her blood and vows to defeat Neji in the finals.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_meets_Kurama.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222031656" class="image"><img alt="Naruto meets Kurama" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto meets Kurama.png" data-image-key="Naruto_meets_Kurama.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_meets_Kurama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222031656" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_meets_Kurama.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222031656" class="image"><img alt="Naruto meets Kurama" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_meets_Kurama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222031656" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto meets Kurama.png" data-image-key="Naruto_meets_Kurama.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/99/Naruto_meets_Kurama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222031656" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_meets_Kurama.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets the Nine-Tails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the month of training, Naruto first meets <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a> (who knocked out <a href="/wiki/Ebisu" title="Ebisu">Ebisu</a>, Naruto's original teacher) and trains under the <a href="/wiki/Sannin" title="Sannin">Sannin</a> to improve his chakra control. Recognising Naruto as the Nine-Tails' jinchūriki, Jiraiya <a href="/wiki/Five_Elements_Unseal" title="Five Elements Unseal">removes</a> the seal Orochimaru had placed on Naruto to ease his control and begins teaching him how to use the Nine-Tails' power by <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Technique" title="Summoning Technique">summoning</a> <a href="/wiki/Toads" class="mw-redirect" title="Toads">toads</a>. To accelerate Naruto's slow progress, Jiraiya pushes him over a cliff, causing Naruto to enter his subconscious and meet the Nine-Tails. Working past his fear, he bravely demands chakra from it as "rent" for living in his body. The Nine-Tails complies and Naruto summons <a href="/wiki/Gamabunta" title="Gamabunta">Gamabunta</a>, though he exhausts himself and ends up in the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Hospital" title="Konoha Hospital">hospital</a>, where he is visited by <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru_Nara" title="Shikamaru Nara">Shikamaru Nara</a>. After talking, he and Naruto stop <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a> from killing <a href="/wiki/Rock_Lee" title="Rock Lee">Rock Lee</a> in the next room and listen to Gaara's story of his childhood, which Naruto finds very similar to his own. Gaara prepares to kill them, but <a href="/wiki/Might_Guy" title="Might Guy">Might Guy</a> intervenes and forces Gaara to retreat. On the day of the finals, Naruto meets Hinata at the <a href="/wiki/Third_Training_Ground" title="Third Training Ground">Third Training Ground</a> and expresses his doubts about his upcoming match with Neji. Hinata reassures Naruto that he never gave up because he always had the strength to overcome his own failures, admiring him for it. Reinvigorated, Naruto thanks Hinata and tells her even though he first thought she was weird, he now likes her.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ef/Naruto_vs_Neji.png/revision/latest?cb=20150109174006" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs Neji" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs Neji.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_Neji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ef/Naruto_vs_Neji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150109174006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ef/Naruto_vs_Neji.png/revision/latest?cb=20150109174006" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs Neji" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ef/Naruto_vs_Neji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150109174006" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs Neji.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_Neji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ef/Naruto_vs_Neji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150109174006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs_Neji.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto vs. Neji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Facing Neji in the first match of the finals, Naruto began by creating shadow clones to overwhelm Neji's with sheer numbers. Deeming Naruto a failure who could never defeat a genius like himself, Neji easily defeats Naruto's clones and seals his chakra with <a href="/wiki/Eight_Trigrams_Sixty-Four_Palms" title="Eight Trigrams Sixty-Four Palms">Eight Trigrams Sixty-Four Palms</a>. Determined to prove Neji's ideals about fate wrong, Naruto tapped into the Nine-Tails' chakra and, revitalised, clashed with Neji. When the smoke cleared, Neji emerges and Naruto lies defeated. This, however, was only a shadow clone, and the real Naruto burst from the ground beneath Neji, defeating him with an uppercut. Before he is declared the winner, Naruto tells Neji that creating clones was once his shortcoming and that Neji needs to stop believing in inescapable fate. When Sasuke finally arrives for his match with Gaara, Naruto is envious of Sasuke's improvements, but is later <a href="/wiki/Temple_of_Nirvana_Technique" title="Temple of Nirvana Technique">put to sleep</a> along with most of the audience, commencing the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Crush" title="Konoha Crush">Konoha Crush</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Konoha_Crush">Konoha Crush</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Crush_(Arc)" title="Konoha Crush (Arc)">Konoha Crush</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/93/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20221019183433" class="image"><img alt="Naruto saves Sasuke from Gaara" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto saves Sasuke from Gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/93/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221019183433" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/93/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20221019183433" class="image"><img alt="Naruto saves Sasuke from Gaara" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/93/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221019183433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto saves Sasuke from Gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/93/Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221019183433" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_saves_Sasuke_from_Gaara.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto saves Sasuke from Gaara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sakura wakes up Naruto so they can pursue Sasuke, who was pursuing Gaara himself. They arrive in time for Naruto to kick Gaara away before he can kill Sasuke. Partially transformed into <a href="/wiki/Shukaku" title="Shukaku">Shukaku</a>, Gaara knocks Sakura unconscious and binds her to a tree, forcing Naruto to battle him, with little success. Naruto relates to Gaara's painful life as a jinchūriki, but he is not willing to let anything to happen to Sakura and Sasuke. Determined to protect his friends, Naruto creates an army of shadow clones to <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Uzumaki_Two_Thousand_Combo" title="Naruto Uzumaki Two Thousand Combo">relentlessly batter</a> Gaara, forcing him to <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Mode" class="mw-redirect" title="Tailed Beast Mode">fully transform</a> into Shukaku, to which Naruto responds by summoning Gamabunta.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_defeats_gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20140620073538" class="image"><img alt="Naruto defeats gaara" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto defeats gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_defeats_gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_defeats_gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620073538" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_defeats_gaara.png/revision/latest?cb=20140620073538" class="image"><img alt="Naruto defeats gaara" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_defeats_gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620073538" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto defeats gaara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_defeats_gaara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_defeats_gaara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140620073538" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_defeats_gaara.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats Gaara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Gaara <a href="/wiki/Feigning_Sleep_Technique" title="Feigning Sleep Technique">puts himself to sleep</a> to give control of his body to Shukaku, forcing Naruto and Gamabunta to figure out a way to end the jutsu. They do so by <a href="/wiki/Combination_Transformation" title="Combination Transformation">transforming</a> into a giant fox (the Nine-Tails in the anime) to restrain Shukaku, allowing Naruto to awaken Gaara with a solid punch to the face. Shukaku's influence disappears, but Gaara regains control and traps Naruto with his sand. Naruto escapes by tapping into the Nine-Tails' chakra, and headbutts Gaara when he is close enough, destroying Shukaku's form. Exhausted from the fight, the two leap at each other for one final exchange, and Naruto punches Gaara, claiming victory.
</p><p>Naruto and Gaara fell to the ground, unable to move. Slowly crawling towards Gaara, Naruto explained that he also suffered a painful and lonely life, but was later saved by having friends. To that end, he will do anything to protect them, even if it means killing Gaara. Understanding Naruto's true strength, Gaara retreated with <a href="/wiki/Kankur%C5%8D" title="Kankurō">Kankurō</a> and <a href="/wiki/Temari" title="Temari">Temari</a> with a new outlook on life, while Naruto passes out from exhaustion and is returned to Konoha with Sasuke and a rescued Sakura. A few days later, Team 7 attended the <a href="/wiki/Third_Hokage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Hokage">Third Hokage</a>'s funeral.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Search_for_Tsunade">Search for Tsunade</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Search_for_Tsunade" title="Search for Tsunade">Search for Tsunade</a></span>
Jiraiya is tasked with finding <a href="/wiki/Tsunade" title="Tsunade">Tsunade</a>, a candidate for Fifth Hokage, and convinces Naruto to accompany him by promising to teach him a technique stronger than Sasuke's <a href="/wiki/Chidori" title="Chidori">Chidori</a>. Stopping at an inn in <a href="/wiki/Shukuba_Town" title="Shukuba Town">Shukuba Town</a>, Naruto was approached by <a href="/wiki/Kisame_Hoshigaki" title="Kisame Hoshigaki">Kisame Hoshigaki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Itachi_Uchiha" title="Itachi Uchiha">Itachi Uchiha</a> of <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a>, who intend to capture the Nine-Tails. When Sasuke shows up and furiously attacks Itachi, Naruto gathers the Nine-Tails' chakra to help Sasuke, but it is absorbed by Kisame's <a href="/wiki/Samehada" title="Samehada">Samehada</a>. Jiraiya soon arrives and drives off Itachi and Kisame, but Sasuke is left mentally and physically damaged by Itachi. <a href="/wiki/Might_Guy" title="Might Guy">Might Guy</a> appears and takes Sasuke back to Konoha, but not before giving Naruto a spare green jumpsuit.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8d/Tsunade_vs_naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20141015183800" class="image"><img alt="Tsunade vs naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tsunade vs naruto.png" data-image-key="Tsunade_vs_naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8d/Tsunade_vs_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141015183800" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8d/Tsunade_vs_naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20141015183800" class="image"><img alt="Tsunade vs naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8d/Tsunade_vs_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141015183800" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tsunade vs naruto.png" data-image-key="Tsunade_vs_naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8d/Tsunade_vs_naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141015183800" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tsunade_vs_naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Tsunade face-off.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To prepare for the next encounter with Akatsuki, Naruto begins learning the <a href="/wiki/Rasengan" title="Rasengan">Rasengan</a>, completing two of its three learning steps. Taking a break from training, Naruto and Jiraiya eventually found Tsunade and her assistant <a href="/wiki/Shizune" title="Shizune">Shizune</a> at a restaurant. When Tsunade refuses the offer to become Hokage and insults all who held the title, an angry Naruto challenged her to a fight and attacked her with an incomplete Rasengan, only to be easily defeated. Impressed by his progress, however, Tsunade makes a bet with Naruto: if he can master the Rasengan in a week, he gets the <a href="/wiki/First_Hokage%27s_Necklace" title="First Hokage&#39;s Necklace">First Hokage's Necklace</a>; if not, she gets his <a href="/wiki/Gama-chan" title="Gama-chan">wallet</a>. Naruto agreed and spent the week trying to perfect the Rasengan, but has no success and collapses from exhaustion. Once he recovers, Naruto heads out with Jiraiya and Shizune to stop Tsunade from meeting with Orochimaru.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150223120149" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Kabuto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223120149" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150223120149" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223120149" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Kabuto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b0/Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150223120149" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs._Kabuto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats Kabuto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They arrive to see Tsunade, who never intended to aid Orochimaru, in the midst of battle with <a href="/wiki/Kabuto_Yakushi" title="Kabuto Yakushi">Kabuto Yakushi</a>. When Tsunade is incapacitated, Naruto fights Kabuto in her place and eventually defeats him with a perfected Rasengan, which he formed by using a shadow clone. Naruto collapses almost immediately afterwards, his heart muscles torn by Kabuto, but Tsunade successfully manages to heal him, gives him the necklace he wins, and accepts the position of Hokage. After Orochimaru and Kabuto are defeated, Naruto and the others return to Konoha, Tsunade confidently believing Naruto would someday become a great Hokage.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Land_of_Tea_Escort_Mission">Land of Tea Escort Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Tea_Escort_Mission" title="Land of Tea Escort Mission">Land of Tea Escort Mission</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sasuke_Recovery_Mission">Sasuke Recovery Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Recovery_Mission" title="Sasuke Recovery Mission">Sasuke Recovery Mission</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Naruto%27s_Promise.png/revision/latest?cb=20150224121926" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Promise" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Promise.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Promise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Naruto%27s_Promise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150224121926" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Naruto%27s_Promise.png/revision/latest?cb=20150224121926" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s Promise" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Naruto%27s_Promise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150224121926" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s Promise.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_Promise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Naruto%27s_Promise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150224121926" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_Promise.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto promises Sakura to return Sasuke to Konoha.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto visits a recovering Sasuke at the hospital, but is immediately challenged to a fight, to which Naruto eventually agrees. The fight escalates quickly, culminating with Naruto using Rasengan and Sasuke using Chidori. Kakashi arrives and deflects their attacks into opposing water towers before they can clash, Naruto unknowingly doing more damage than Sasuke. Distressed by Sasuke's behaviour, Sakura informs Naruto of the cursed seal Sasuke received from Orochimaru, though Naruto assures Sakura that Sasuke would never abandon Konoha for power. Unfortunately, Sasuke does just that and Naruto joins the <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Recovery_Team" title="Sasuke Recovery Team">Sasuke Recovery Team</a> in order to bring him back; he promises a tearful Sakura to do so before he leaves. En route to Sasuke, the team encounters members of the <a href="/wiki/Sound_Four" title="Sound Four">Sound Four</a>, each of which battles a member of the recovery team, while Naruto engages <a href="/wiki/Kimimaro" title="Kimimaro">Kimimaro</a>. Overwhelmed by Kimimaro's taijutsu skills, Naruto is saved at the last minute by Rock Lee, who volunteers to fight Kimimaro while Naruto heads after Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222045618" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Sasuke clash" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Sasuke clash.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045618" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222045618" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Sasuke clash" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045618" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Sasuke clash.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e6/Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045618" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Sasuke_clash.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto fights Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto finally meets Sasuke at the <a href="/wiki/Valley_of_the_End" title="Valley of the End">Valley of the End</a>. His pleas for Sasuke to come back to Konoha and warns him that Orochimaru will <a href="/wiki/Living_Corpse_Reincarnation" title="Living Corpse Reincarnation">take his body</a>, but his pleadings fall on deaf ears. Naruto starts attacking him, ready to take him back to Konoha by force if necessary. Undeterred, Sasuke responds by tapping into his cursed seal and landing a series of heavy blows on Naruto. It becomes painfully clear to Naruto that Sasuke is fighting with an intent to kill, so Naruto utilises the Nine-Tails' chakra to overpower Sasuke. Naruto says that Sasuke is like a brother to him and that he will do anything to protect that bond. Sasuke vows to sever that bond, but acknowledges Naruto as an equal by putting on his forehead protector. They continue trading blows, with Naruto eventually manifesting a <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms#Version_1" title="Jinchūriki Forms">fox-shaped cloak</a> and Sasuke entering his <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Seal_of_Heaven" title="Cursed Seal of Heaven">cursed seal</a>'s second level. Naruto clashes his Rasengan with Sasuke's Chidori, and within the dome of resulting energy they trade final blows: Sasuke punches Naruto and Naruto scratches Sasuke's forehead protector.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221070005" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke defeats Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sasuke defeats Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221070005" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221070005" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke defeats Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221070005" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sasuke defeats Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221070005" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sasuke_defeats_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeated by Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the energy dissipates, Naruto lies defeated, but Sasuke spares him and continues his way to Orochimaru, leaving his scratched forehead protector behind. Kakashi and <a href="/wiki/Pakkun" title="Pakkun">Pakkun</a> arrive late and failing to retrieve Sasuke, leave with Naruto. In the hospital, Naruto once again promises Sakura to bring Sasuke back one day. Soon after, Jiraiya arrived with an offer to train Naruto for preparation against Orochimaru and Akatsuki in three years and to give up on Sasuke, as he is no different from Orochimaru. Naruto accepts Jiraiya's training, but refuses to give up on Sasuke, satisfying Jiraiya.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Original_Anime_Arcs">Original Anime Arcs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote"><i>See also: <a href="/wiki/Plot_of_Naruto" title="Plot of Naruto">Plot of Naruto</a></i></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png/revision/latest?cb=20230224022502" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Departing Konoha" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Departing Konoha.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022502" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png/revision/latest?cb=20230224022502" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Departing Konoha" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022502" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Departing Konoha.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022502" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Departing_Konoha.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto leaving Konoha.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As in the manga, Naruto later departs with Jiraiya to begin his two and a half years of training, after making a determined gesture at the Fourth Hokage's statue. In the anime, this does not happen until about 3 months later as Jiraiya was occupied with important intel gathering about Akatsuki for Konohagakure. During the waiting period, Tsunade gives Naruto several missions with members of the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_11" title="Konoha 11">Konoha 11</a> to keep him busy.
</p>
<div style="clear: left;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Interlude">Interlude</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/06/Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230224022842" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Improving Resengan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Improving Resengan.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/06/Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022842" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/06/Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230224022842" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Improving Resengan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/06/Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022842" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Improving Resengan.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/06/Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230224022842" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Improving_Resengan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto training with the Big Ball Rasengan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, shortly after leaving Konoha, Jiraiya and Naruto discuss the fact that Naruto will need to learn how to counter genjutsu if he hopes to be a match against Sasuke the next time they meet. Naruto practises with <a href="/wiki/Gamariki" title="Gamariki">Gamariki</a> to dispel genjutsu, but he struggles with it and his chakra keeps hitting Gamariki, who doesn't appreciate it. Naruto follows Jiraiya to the <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu_Tree_Village" title="Genjutsu Tree Village">Genjutsu Tree Village</a> to try a different approach, but they discover the village has been taken over by <a href="/wiki/Kandachi" title="Kandachi">Kandachi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> They free the villagers and then attack Kandachi, who Naruto eventually defeats with his newly-created <a href="/wiki/Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Big Ball Rasengan">Big Ball Rasengan</a>. As they leave afterwards, Jiraiya is pleased by how similar Naruto is to <a href="/wiki/Minato_Namikaze" title="Minato Namikaze">Minato Namikaze</a> and hugs him, which Naruto is bothered by.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="In_Naruto.27s_Footsteps:_The_Friends.27_Paths"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="In_Naruto's_Footsteps:_The_Friends'_Paths">In Naruto's Footsteps: The Friends' Paths</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/In_Naruto%27s_Footsteps:_The_Friends%27_Paths" title="In Naruto&#39;s Footsteps: The Friends&#39; Paths">In Naruto's Footsteps: The Friends' Paths</a></span>
Two years into their training, Naruto's control of the Nine-Tails' chakra has improved significantly. Jiraiya tries to give him more access to the Nine-Tails' power and uses <a href="/wiki/Gerotora" title="Gerotora">Gerotora</a> to weaken Naruto's <a href="/wiki/Eight_Trigrams_Sealing_Style" title="Eight Trigrams Sealing Style">Eight Trigrams Sealing Style</a>. Seizing the opportunity, the Nine-Tails mocked Naruto for his inability to save Sasuke, using Naruto's negative emotions to force him to enter a <a href="/wiki/Version_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 2">version 2</a> form with four tails. Not in control of his body, Naruto attacks Jiraiya and nearly kills him before he manages to suppress the Nine-Tails. Naruto has no memory of what happened and Jiraiya doesn't tell him, instead, shifting Naruto's training to other pursuits, including keeping his anger in check so that the Nine-Tails won't flare up again.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Part_II">Part II</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span class="box headnote"><i>See also: <a href="/wiki/Plot_of_Naruto:_Shipp%C5%ABden" class="mw-redirect" title="Plot of Naruto: Shippūden">Plot of Naruto: Shippūden</a></i></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kazekage_Rescue_Mission">Kazekage Rescue Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kazekage_Rescue_Mission" title="Kazekage Rescue Mission">Kazekage Rescue Mission</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png/revision/latest?cb=20221004113050" class="image"><img alt="Naruto returns to Konoha" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto returns to Konoha.png" data-image-key="Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004113050" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png/revision/latest?cb=20221004113050" class="image"><img alt="Naruto returns to Konoha" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004113050" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto returns to Konoha.png" data-image-key="Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004113050" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_returns_to_Konoha.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto returns to Konohagakure.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto and Jiraiya return to Konoha after two-and-a-half years of training, where Naruto becomes surprised by Tsunade's newly-formed statue on <a href="/wiki/Hokage_Rock" title="Hokage Rock">Hokage Rock</a>. He greets his old friends afterwards: he gives Kakashi a copy of <i><a href="/wiki/Icha_Icha_Tactics" class="mw-redirect" title="Icha Icha Tactics">Icha Icha Tactics</a></i> as a gift; he catches up with Sakura, whom he has become taller than; he gets back into a competition of <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Technique" title="Sexy Technique">Sexy Techniques</a> with <a href="/wiki/Konohamaru_Sarutobi" title="Konohamaru Sarutobi">Konohamaru Sarutobi</a>, only to be violently reprimanded by Sakura. Kakashi reforms Team 7 with them and gives them another <a href="/wiki/Bell_test" class="mw-redirect" title="Bell test">bell test</a>, but unlike last time, taking the bells from him is the real objective. As with last time, Naruto launches a first attack before the test officially begins, but this time it nearly succeeds. Despite their improved abilities, Naruto and Sakura were still unable to get a bell through conventional means, and it was only by Naruto's threat to spoil the latest <i><a href="/wiki/Icha_Icha" title="Icha Icha">Icha Icha</a></i> novel that they distracted Kakashi long enough to take the bells.
</p><p>While Team 7 tries without success to find a mission to go on that Naruto won't complain about, word reaches Konoha that <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a> has kidnapped <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Kazekage" title="Kazekage">Kazekage</a>. Team 7 is sent to Sunagakure to assist in rescuing Gaara. On their way to Suna, Naruto explains that Gaara was kidnapped because he is the <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a> of the <a href="/wiki/One-Tail" class="mw-redirect" title="One-Tail">One-Tail</a>, just as Naruto is the jinchūriki of the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails" class="mw-redirect" title="Nine-Tails">Nine-Tails</a>. Upon arrival in Suna, Naruto defends Kakashi from <a href="/wiki/Chiyo" title="Chiyo">Chiyo</a>'s assault when she mistakes him for his father. Team 7 gathers what intel they can on Gaara's kidnappers and leave to go after them; Chiyo volunteers to escort them since they aren't familiar with the country around Suna. Naruto promises a recovering <a href="/wiki/Kankur%C5%8D" title="Kankurō">Kankurō</a> to rescue Gaara before they leave.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png/revision/latest?cb=20230423165954" class="image"><img alt="Naruto pummels Deidara" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto pummels Deidara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230423165954" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png/revision/latest?cb=20230423165954" class="image"><img alt="Naruto pummels Deidara" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230423165954" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto pummels Deidara.png" data-image-key="Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230423165954" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_pummels_Deidara.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto pummels Deidara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While en route to an Akatsuki lair, they are confronted by <a href="/wiki/Itachi_Uchiha" title="Itachi Uchiha">Itachi Uchiha</a>, who traps Naruto in a genjutsu. Sakura and Chiyo release him, allowing Naruto to team up with Kakashi and defeat Itachi with a <a href="/wiki/Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Big Ball Rasengan">Big Ball Rasengan</a>. The Itachi is discovered to be an <a href="/wiki/Shapeshifting_Technique" title="Shapeshifting Technique">impostor</a>, so they continue to the Akatsuki lair, meeting up with <a href="/wiki/Team_Guy" title="Team Guy">Team Guy</a>, who takes down the barrier over the entrance so that Team 7 can get in. They find Gaara's body finds with his kidnappers, <a href="/wiki/Deidara" title="Deidara">Deidara</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sasori" title="Sasori">Sasori</a>. Deidara flies off with Gaara's body with Naruto and Kakashi in pursuit, leaving Sasori to Chiyo and Sakura. Naruto, enraged, makes repeated failed attempts to rescue Gaara before he is calmed by Kakashi, who uses his new <a href="/wiki/Mangeky%C5%8D_Sharingan" title="Mangekyō Sharingan">Mangekyō Sharingan</a> to distract Deidara with <a href="/wiki/Kamui" title="Kamui">Kamui</a>. Naruto retrieves Gaara's body, but seeing it drives him over the edge: he furiously attacks Deidara and beats him mercilessly into the ground. Discovering that it was a <a href="/wiki/Clay_Clone" title="Clay Clone">Clay Clone</a>, Naruto slips into his <a href="/wiki/Version_1" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 1">two-tailed</a> form in rage, but is restored to normal by Kakashi via the <a href="/wiki/Chakra-Suppressing_Seal" title="Chakra-Suppressing Seal">Chakra-Suppressing Seal</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Gaara_awakens.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103627" class="image"><img alt="Gaara awakens" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gaara awakens.png" data-image-key="Gaara_awakens.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Gaara_awakens.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103627" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Gaara_awakens.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103627" class="image"><img alt="Gaara awakens" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Gaara_awakens.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103627" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gaara awakens.png" data-image-key="Gaara_awakens.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Gaara_awakens.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103627" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gaara_awakens.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Gaara awakens, with Naruto by his side.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Deidara escapes, while Naruto and Kakashi regroup with Sakura, Chiyo, and Team Guy. Sakura attempts to revive Gaara, but the <a href="/wiki/Sealing_Technique:_Phantom_Dragons_Nine_Consuming_Seals" title="Sealing Technique: Phantom Dragons Nine Consuming Seals">removal</a> of Shukaku has caused him to die. Naruto breaks down in tears and angrily lashes out at Chiyo, saying she had no right to make Gaara not only a jinchūriki, but also lose his life because of it. As atonement and with Naruto's aid, Chiyo sacrifices her life to revive Gaara; as the jutsu nears completion, Chiyo voices her faith in Naruto's ability to save Gaara and to become Hokage. Naruto greets Gaara when he awakens, and a few days later, Teams 7 and Guy attend Chiyo's funeral in Suna. Before returning home, Naruto and Gaara shake hands (Gaara using his sand) as a sign of their close relationship.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tenchi_Bridge_Reconnaissance_Mission">Tenchi Bridge Reconnaissance Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tenchi_Bridge_Reconnaissance_Mission" title="Tenchi Bridge Reconnaissance Mission">Tenchi Bridge Reconnaissance Mission</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003164058" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Sai&#39;s first meeting" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Sai&#39;s first meeting.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003164058" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003164058" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Sai&#39;s first meeting" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003164058" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Sai&#39;s first meeting.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003164058" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Sai%27s_first_meeting.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sai's first encounter.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During her fight with Sasori, Sakura learned of an opportunity to meet with a spy in Orochimaru's ranks in a few days' time, hoping it will lead them to Sasuke. Kakashi is left bedridden from his fight with Deidara, so <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a> leads Team 7 as his replacement. Replacing Sasuke on the team is <a href="/wiki/Sai" title="Sai">Sai</a>, whom Naruto actually encounters earlier and dislikes, declaring him an inferior version of Sasuke. Sai is happy for this distinction and proceeds to degrade Sasuke for defecting from Konoha, forcing Yamato to use his <a href="/wiki/Wood_Release" title="Wood Release">Wood Release</a> to break up their fight. Naruto is constantly exasperated by Sai's lack of empathy and his ridicule of Sasuke, but resolves to work with Sai if it means saving Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/04/Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003120655" class="image"><img alt="Team Yamato at Tenchi Bridge" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Team Yamato at Tenchi Bridge.png" data-image-key="Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/04/Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120655" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/04/Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003120655" class="image"><img alt="Team Yamato at Tenchi Bridge" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/04/Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120655" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Team Yamato at Tenchi Bridge.png" data-image-key="Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/04/Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221003120655" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Team_Yamato_at_Tenchi_Bridge.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Team 7 confronts Orochimaru and Kabuto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Yamato disguises himself as Sasori and goes to the <a href="/wiki/Tenchi_Bridge" title="Tenchi Bridge">Tenchi Bridge</a> to meet the spy while Naruto, Sakura, and Sai hide nearby. The spy, <a href="/wiki/Kabuto_Yakushi" title="Kabuto Yakushi">Kabuto Yakushi</a>, begins telling Yamato about Orochimaru's organisation, but they are interrupted by the arrival of Orochimaru, who teams up with Kabuto to fight Yamato, having intended to kill Sasori. Team 7 comes to his aid and Orochimaru, recognising them, taunts Naruto about Sasuke. Naruto is enraged and strikes him, using his <a href="/wiki/Version_1" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 1">version 1</a> form to make his attacks more devastating. Naruto's rage intensifies as he submits to the Nine-Tails' influence: he destroys the Tenchi Bridge and eventually advances to his <a href="/wiki/Version_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 2">version 2</a> form while fighting Orochimaru. Naruto is soon forced back to the destroyed bridge, where, unable to tell friend from foe, he unknowingly attacks Sakura when she approaches him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0b/Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125032008" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Orochimaru.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0b/Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032008" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0b/Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125032008" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0b/Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032008" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Orochimaru.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0b/Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032008" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs._Orochimaru.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A four-tailed Naruto attacks Orochimaru with Tailed Beast Ball.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Yamato restrains Naruto with his Wood Release and suppresses the Nine-Tails' influence, but its chakra leaves Naruto's body badly damaged. After Sakura heals him, Naruto wakes up unable to remember what happened, but is surprised by the devastated landscape. When they realise that Sai is missing, Yamato reports that he has joined with Orochimaru and Kabuto. On the way, Yamato secretly takes Naruto aside and tells him that he is the one who attacked Sakura. He encourages Naruto to use his own strength instead of the Nine-Tails in order to protect his loved ones. The team locates Sai, whom Yamato has placed a <a href="/wiki/Transmission_Wood" title="Transmission Wood">trace</a> on, at Orochimaru's lair and capture him. Restrained, Sai asks why Naruto is determined to save him; Naruto replies that his bond with Sasuke is too precious to be broken and that he will do anything to protect it. Intrigued, Sai switches sides, helping them capture Kabuto and then searching the base for Sasuke on Naruto's behalf.
