While he's gone, Yamato goes through his belongings and finds evidence that Sai has been assigned to assassinate Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/59/Sasuke_draws_sword.png/revision/latest?cb=20150202074839" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke draws sword" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sasuke draws sword.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_draws_sword.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/59/Sasuke_draws_sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150202074839" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/59/Sasuke_draws_sword.png/revision/latest?cb=20150202074839" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke draws sword" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/59/Sasuke_draws_sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150202074839" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sasuke draws sword.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_draws_sword.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/59/Sasuke_draws_sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150202074839" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sasuke_draws_sword.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto encounters Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When they find Sai, he explains that he truly does want to help retrieve Sasuke, and in fact has already found him: Naruto and Sakura are speechless to see Sasuke again. Sasuke reacts with indifference to them, but Naruto remarks he can't become Hokage without saving his friend. To demonstrate that they mean nothing to him, Sasuke quickly neutralises them all. As Naruto struggles to avoid the temptation of using the Nine-Tails, Sasuke suddenly appears in Naruto's subconscious using his Sharingan and suppresses the Nine-Tails. He then prepares to kill them, but is persuaded not to by Orochimaru and leaves without further comment. Naruto is upset at having failed once more to bring Sasuke home, but is reminded by Sakura that they need to become stronger and Team 7 returns to Konoha.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Twelve_Guardian_Ninja">Twelve Guardian Ninja</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Twelve_Guardian_Ninja_(Arc)" title="Twelve Guardian Ninja (Arc)">Twelve Guardian Ninja (Arc)</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Akatsuki_Suppression_Mission">Akatsuki Suppression Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki_Suppression_Mission" title="Akatsuki Suppression Mission">Akatsuki Suppression Mission</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_training.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125032148" class="image"><img alt="Naruto training" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto training.png" data-image-key="Naruto_training.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_training.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032148" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_training.png/revision/latest?cb=20231125032148" class="image"><img alt="Naruto training" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_training.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032148" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto training.png" data-image-key="Naruto_training.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_training.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231125032148" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_training.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto training with his clones.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once Kakashi is done recuperating in the hospital, he assembles Naruto, Sakura, and Sai to discuss their failed mission to retrieve Sasuke. Kakashi believes the best way to match Sasuke is for Naruto to create a new <a href="/wiki/Jutsu" title="Jutsu">jutsu</a>. As the training began, Naruto discovers that his <a href="/wiki/Nature" class="mw-redirect" title="Nature">nature</a> is <a href="/wiki/Wind" class="mw-redirect" title="Wind">wind</a> and learns to use the wind nature. Ordinarily, such training would take months or years, but Kakashi advises that Naruto, by training alongside hundreds of <a href="/wiki/Shadow_clones" class="mw-redirect" title="Shadow clones">shadow clones</a> can do the same training in a mere fraction of the time. With Kakashi's instructions and the training grounds created by Yamato, Naruto quickly masters how to use the wind nature. The next step is more difficult for him: combining that nature with the <a href="/wiki/Rasengan" title="Rasengan">Rasengan</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png/revision/latest?cb=20151004005728" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs Kakuzu " src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs Kakuzu .png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151004005728" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png/revision/latest?cb=20151004005728" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs Kakuzu " src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151004005728" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs Kakuzu .png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ee/Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151004005728" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs_Kakuzu_.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats Kakuzu.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like Kakashi and <a href="/wiki/Minato_Namikaze" title="Minato Namikaze">Minato Namikaze</a> before him, Naruto fails several times in trying to combine his nature with the Rasengan; his frustration evokes the Nine-Tails' chakra at times, which Yamato suppresses. With further advice from Kakashi, Naruto finds his solution using two shadow clones: one helps him form the Rasengan and the other adds his wind nature. When they receive news that Asuma died in battle with members of <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a>, they take a break to attend Asuma's funeral. Kakashi leaves Yamato in charge of overseeing Naruto's training so he could help <a href="/wiki/Team_Asuma" class="mw-redirect" title="Team Asuma">Team 10</a> avenge Asuma. Having finished his jutsu, Naruto and Team Yamato went to provide assistance, arriving in time to save Kakashi and Team 10 from <a href="/wiki/Kakuzu" title="Kakuzu">Kakuzu</a>. Naruto engages Kakuzu alone with his newly-created <a href="/wiki/Wind_Release:_Rasenshuriken" title="Wind Release: Rasenshuriken">Wind Release: Rasenshuriken</a>, though it dissipates on its first use and Naruto is rescued by Kakashi and Yamato. The technique succeeds the second time, destroying two of Kakuzu's hearts and putting the last one on the brink of failure. Kakashi finishes off Kakuzu and they return to Konoha.
</p><p>The Rasenshuriken injures Naruto's arm after use and he is forbidden to use the technique ever again. When they visit Ichiraku Ramen, Naruto has a hard time eating while his arm mends, so Sakura opts to help, before the responsibility falls to Sai, then to Kakashi. As they leave afterwards, they are met by Konohamaru, who demonstrates his <a href="/wiki/Sexy:_Girl_on_Girl_Technique" title="Sexy: Girl on Girl Technique">Sexy: Girl on Girl Technique</a>; Naruto approves but Sakura is disgusted and violently reprimands him. In the manga, Konohamaru responds with <a href="/wiki/Sexy:_Boy_on_Boy_Technique" title="Sexy: Boy on Boy Technique">Sexy: Boy on Boy Technique</a>; Sakura approves but Naruto is disgusted and violently reprimands him.
</p>
<h3><span id="Three-Tails.27_Appearance"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Three-Tails'_Appearance">Three-Tails' Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Three-Tails%27_Appearance" title="Three-Tails&#39; Appearance">Three-Tails' Appearance</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Itachi_Pursuit_Mission">Itachi Pursuit Mission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Itachi_Pursuit_Mission" title="Itachi Pursuit Mission">Itachi Pursuit Mission</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/75/Eight_Man_Squad.png/revision/latest?cb=20210806023638" class="image"><img alt="Eight Man Squad" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Eight Man Squad.png" data-image-key="Eight_Man_Squad.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/75/Eight_Man_Squad.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210806023638" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/75/Eight_Man_Squad.png/revision/latest?cb=20210806023638" class="image"><img alt="Eight Man Squad" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/75/Eight_Man_Squad.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210806023638" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Eight Man Squad.png" data-image-key="Eight_Man_Squad.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/75/Eight_Man_Squad.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210806023638" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Eight_Man_Squad.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Eight Man Squad formed to pursue Itachi and Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>News reaches Konoha that Sasuke has killed Orochimaru. Realising that this is a good opportunity to try once again to reunite with Sasuke, Kakashi combines Teams 7 and 8 into an <a href="/wiki/Eight_Man_Squad" title="Eight Man Squad">Eight Man Squad</a> with the mission to find either Sasuke or his assumed target, Itachi. When they split up to search, Naruto, because he's a target of Akatsuki, is given a protective escort in the form of Hinata, Yamato, and <a href="/wiki/Bull" title="Bull">Bull</a>. Their group encounters Kabuto, who offers them intel on Akatsuki and its members, his thanks to Naruto "inspiring" him to overcome Orochimaru after absorbing his remains. Kabuto then escapes.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tale_of_Jiraiya_the_Gallant">Tale of Jiraiya the Gallant</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tale_of_Jiraiya_the_Gallant" title="Tale of Jiraiya the Gallant">Tale of Jiraiya the Gallant</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a0/Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103240" class="image"><img alt="Itachi&#39;s Genjutsu" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Itachi&#39;s Genjutsu.png" data-image-key="Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a0/Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103240" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a0/Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103240" class="image"><img alt="Itachi&#39;s Genjutsu" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a0/Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103240" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Itachi&#39;s Genjutsu.png" data-image-key="Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a0/Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103240" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Itachi%27s_Genjutsu.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Itachi converse.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After regrouping and <a href="/wiki/Kiba_Inuzuka" title="Kiba Inuzuka">Kiba Inuzuka</a> detects Sasuke's trail, Naruto creates shadow clones to search the area faster, one of which encounters Itachi. Itachi repels Naruto's attacks and insists he only wants to talk. He asks Naruto what Sasuke means to him and what he will do if Sasuke ever moves against Konoha. Naruto replies that he is Sasuke's brother – a better brother than Itachi is – and that if Sasuke ever attacks the village he will defend it without killing Sasuke. Itachi is happy with this answer and gives Naruto some assistance for this purpose: a <a href="/wiki/Itachi%27s_Crow" title="Itachi&#39;s Crow">special crow</a> that he stores within Naruto's body. Itachi left, and Naruto continued his search, eventually finding Sasuke.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As they near Sasuke's location they are intercepted by <a href="/wiki/Tobi" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobi">Tobi</a> of Akatsuki, who prevents them from progressing and who is invulnerable to their attacks.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fated_Battle_Between_Brothers">Fated Battle Between Brothers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fated_Battle_Between_Brothers" title="Fated Battle Between Brothers">Fated Battle Between Brothers</a></span>
As the group continually tries to attack Tobi, he dodges the attacks with ease. Naruto tries several times to attack him with his Rasengan, but without success. Tobi attempts to use a hidden jutsu to attack the teams, but fails at it. Eventually, Zetsu comes to tell him about Sasuke and Itachi's fight. Tobi leaves when he receives news that Sasuke has killed Itachi, and Teams 7 and 8 try to reach Sasuke before he does. Unable to find where Tobi has taken Sasuke, they are forced to return to Konoha.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Six-Tails_Unleashed">Six-Tails Unleashed</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Six-Tails_Unleashed" title="Six-Tails Unleashed">Six-Tails Unleashed</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span id="Pain.27s_Assault"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Pain's_Assault">Pain's Assault</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Pain%27s_Assault_(Arc)" title="Pain&#39;s Assault (Arc)">Pain's Assault</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/da/Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png/revision/latest?cb=20141201100739" class="image"><img alt="Naruto after Jiraiya&#39;s death" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto after Jiraiya&#39;s death.png" data-image-key="Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/da/Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141201100739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/da/Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png/revision/latest?cb=20141201100739" class="image"><img alt="Naruto after Jiraiya&#39;s death" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/da/Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141201100739" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto after Jiraiya&#39;s death.png" data-image-key="Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/da/Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141201100739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_after_Jiraiya%27s_death.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto mourns Jiraiya's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Naruto contemplated his meeting with Itachi, he was called to the <a href="/wiki/Hokage_Residence" title="Hokage Residence">Hokage Residence</a> to hear sombre news: his master Jiraiya was killed by <a href="/wiki/Pain" class="mw-redirect" title="Pain">Pain</a>, the leader of Akatsuki. Grief-stricken, Naruto blamed Tsunade and spent the day mourning his teacher's death, depressed that Jiraiya cannot see him become Hokage. After being comforted by <a href="/wiki/Iruka" class="mw-redirect" title="Iruka">Iruka</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru" class="mw-redirect" title="Shikamaru">Shikamaru</a>, Naruto helped to decipher Jiraiya's dying message and eventually they succeed. Understanding that Jiraiya had bought him time for his own fight with Pain, Naruto went to train with the toads of <a href="/wiki/Mount_My%C5%8Dboku" title="Mount Myōboku">Mount Myōboku</a> to learn <a href="/wiki/Senjutsu" title="Senjutsu">senjutsu</a>. Naruto trained to harmonise with nature, a process he sped up by using a limited number of shadow clones. He rapidly progressed through the training stages and attained a perfect <a href="/wiki/Sage_Mode" title="Sage Mode">Sage Mode</a>, which Jiraiya was unable to do. News of <a href="/wiki/Pain%27s_Assault" title="Pain&#39;s Assault">Pain's Assault</a> on Konoha reached them, they began to mobilise for battle.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/af/Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png/revision/latest?cb=20150125203535" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Fukasaku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Fukasaku.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/af/Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150125203535" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/af/Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png/revision/latest?cb=20150125203535" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Fukasaku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/af/Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150125203535" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Fukasaku.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/af/Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150125203535" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Fukasaku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto arrives to fight Pain.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Naruto, <a href="/wiki/Fukasaku" title="Fukasaku">Fukasaku</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gamaken" title="Gamaken">Gamaken</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gamahiro" title="Gamahiro">Gamahiro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gamabunta" title="Gamabunta">Gamabunta</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Gamakichi" title="Gamakichi">Gamakichi</a> were summoned to the centre of Konoha, the group was confronted by the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_of_Pain" title="Six Paths of Pain">Six Paths of Pain</a>, who had just destroyed the village. After destroying the <a href="/wiki/Asura_Path" title="Asura Path">Asura Path</a> before it could attack Tsunade, Naruto told her to make sure everyone left the battle to him. After a brief skirmish with <a href="/wiki/Animal_Path" title="Animal Path">Animal Path</a>, Naruto and the toads defeated the Animal, <a href="/wiki/Preta" class="mw-redirect" title="Preta">Preta</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Human_Path" title="Human Path">Human Paths</a> before running out of senjutsu chakra. Naruto revealed that he had two shadow clones waiting back at <a href="/wiki/Mount_My%C5%8Dboku" title="Mount Myōboku">Mount Myōboku</a> to revitalise him with natural energy. Naruto went back on the offensive, dispatching the healed Preta and Naraka Path before the Deva Path regained its full power. Pain killed Fukasaku and used the opportunity to capture Naruto, pinning him down to the ground.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Naruto_influenced.png/revision/latest?cb=20230413161548" class="image"><img alt="Naruto influenced" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto influenced.png" data-image-key="Naruto_influenced.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Naruto_influenced.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230413161548" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Naruto_influenced.png/revision/latest?cb=20230413161548" class="image"><img alt="Naruto influenced" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Naruto_influenced.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230413161548" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto influenced.png" data-image-key="Naruto_influenced.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Naruto_influenced.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230413161548" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_influenced.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto succumbs completely to the Nine-Tails' influence.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Naruto restrained, Pain opened up his reasons for Akatsuki, their plan for the tailed beasts, and the peaceful world he wanted to create. Though Naruto rejected his notion that using a weapon to force peace, he could offer no alternative. Before Pain could depart with Naruto, he was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Hinata_Hy%C5%ABga" title="Hinata Hyūga">Hinata Hyūga</a>. Declaring her love for Naruto and vowing to protect him, she continued to fight against Pain before she was subdued and critically wounded. Believing Hinata to had been killed, an enraged Naruto erupted into his <a href="/wiki/Version_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 2">six-tailed form</a>. Resisting the <a href="/wiki/First_Hokage%27s_Necklace" title="First Hokage&#39;s Necklace">First Hokage's Necklace</a>'s attempted to quell the transformation and destroying it, the Nine-Tails attacked Pain, forcing him out of the village to get close enough to his actual body to use the <a href="/wiki/Chibaku_Tensei" title="Chibaku Tensei">Chibaku Tensei</a>, trapping Naruto within the small satellite. The technique was not enough to stop the Nine-Tails, however, as it simply progressed to <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms#Partial_Transformation" title="Jinchūriki Forms">eight-tailed form</a> to force its way out of the satellite. Meanwhile within his subconscious, Naruto was tempted by the Nine-Tails to open its seal to save him from the pain of not having Pain's answer for peace. However, before Naruto could, <a href="/wiki/Minato" class="mw-redirect" title="Minato">Minato</a> appeared, having left some of his chakra within the seal in case of an emergency to protect his son. Overjoyed at meeting his father, but angered that he would condemn him to life as a jinchūriki, Naruto listened to his father encouraging him, confident that he would find a way to break the cycle of hatred. After repairing the seal, Minato disappeared and the newly-inspired Naruto prepared to resume his battle with Pain.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/79/Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222045336" class="image"><img alt="Naruto defeating Deva path" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto defeating Deva path.png" data-image-key="Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/79/Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045336" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/79/Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222045336" class="image"><img alt="Naruto defeating Deva path" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/79/Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045336" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto defeating Deva path.png" data-image-key="Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/79/Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222045336" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_defeating_Deva_path.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats Pain.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Confidence restored, Naruto was greatly relieved to learn that not only had Hinata survived, but nobody was injured during his rampage. After clever use of shadow clones, Naruto destroyed the Deva Path with a Rasengan, defeating the last of Pain's Six Paths. Using one of Pain's <a href="/wiki/Black_Receiver" title="Black Receiver">Black Receivers</a>, Naruto followed the chakra signal to <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">Nagato</a> and <a href="/wiki/Konan" title="Konan">Konan</a>'s position. Confronting Nagato, Naruto listened to Nagato's story that turned him into Pain and came to understand why he made the actions he did. Despite not forgiving him, he told Nagato he would not kill him and would instead try to create the better world that their teacher wished for. Moved by Naruto's determination to create a better world, Nagato decided to put his trust in Naruto and sacrificed his own life to <a href="/wiki/Outer_Path:_Samsara_of_Heavenly_Life_Technique" class="mw-redirect" title="Outer Path: Samsara of Heavenly Life Technique">revive</a> all the people he had killed in Konoha. Naruto helped Konan retrieve Nagato and <a href="/wiki/Yahiko" title="Yahiko">Yahiko</a>'s bodies for burial in <a href="/wiki/Amegakure" title="Amegakure">Amegakure</a>, and Konan left Naruto a bouquet of paper flowers for him, symbolising their new alliance.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20150222030908" class="image"><img alt="Hero of the Hidden Leaf" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hero of the Hidden Leaf.PNG" data-image-key="Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222030908" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20150222030908" class="image"><img alt="Hero of the Hidden Leaf" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222030908" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hero of the Hidden Leaf.PNG" data-image-key="Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222030908" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hero_of_the_Hidden_Leaf.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The village greets Naruto upon his return.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto then created a <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya%27s_Memorial" title="Jiraiya&#39;s Memorial">memorial</a> for <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a> and left the flowers and a copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tale_of_the_Utterly_Gutsy_Shinobi" title="The Tale of the Utterly Gutsy Shinobi">The Tale of the Utterly Gutsy Shinobi</a></i> by a rock with the kanji for <i>teacher</i> (<span lang="ja">師</span>&#44; <i>shi</i>). While the exhausted Naruto walked back to the village, he was found by Kakashi who carried him the rest of the way. Upon arrival, Naruto was greeted as a hero by the villagers, his dream of acknowledgement being realised at last.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past_Arc:_The_Locus_of_Konoha">Past Arc: The Locus of Konoha</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Past_Arc:_The_Locus_of_Konoha" title="Past Arc: The Locus of Konoha">Past Arc: The Locus of Konoha</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Five_Kage_Summit">Five Kage Summit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Five_Kage_Summit_(Arc)" title="Five Kage Summit (Arc)">Five Kage Summit</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fa/Karui_Beating_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20180428081333" class="image"><img alt="Karui Beating Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Karui Beating Naruto.png" data-image-key="Karui_Beating_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fa/Karui_Beating_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180428081333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fa/Karui_Beating_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20180428081333" class="image"><img alt="Karui Beating Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fa/Karui_Beating_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180428081333" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Karui Beating Naruto.png" data-image-key="Karui_Beating_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fa/Karui_Beating_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180428081333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Karui_Beating_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto willingly gets beaten by Karui.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sakura informs Naruto that Tsunade fell into a coma and that there's nothing that can be done to bring her out of it. While they talk, they are approached by <a href="/wiki/Tazuna" title="Tazuna">Tazuna</a> and <a href="/wiki/Inari" title="Inari">Inari</a>, who have come to help rebuild Konoha. They ask about Sasuke, which Naruto avoids going into detail about so as to spare them and Sakura a discussion about Sasuke's defection. After Tazuna and Inari leave, they receive news that <a href="/wiki/Danz%C5%8D_Shimura" title="Danzō Shimura">Danzō Shimura</a> has become the next <a href="/wiki/Hokage" title="Hokage">Hokage</a> and that he has ordered Sasuke be killed as a traitor. Naruto and Sakura approach Sai to ask him how they can convince Danzō to change his mind, but Sai is unable to help. <a href="/wiki/Omoi" title="Omoi">Omoi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Karui" title="Karui">Karui</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kumogakure" title="Kumogakure">Kumogakure</a> overhear them talking about Sasuke and they ask for information about Sasuke, wishing to kill him for his role in Akatsuki's capture of <a href="/wiki/Killer_B" title="Killer B">Killer B</a>. Naruto leads Omoi and Karui away to spare Sakura pain, but refuses to reveal anything about Sasuke. Instead, Naruto allows the Kumo-nin vent their anger by beating him, to which <a href="/wiki/Karui" title="Karui">Karui</a> obliges until Sai stops her and the Kumo-nin retreat.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png/revision/latest?cb=20230322222828" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s failed plea to Raikage" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s failed plea to Raikage.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230322222828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png/revision/latest?cb=20230322222828" class="image"><img alt="Naruto&#39;s failed plea to Raikage" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230322222828" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto&#39;s failed plea to Raikage.png" data-image-key="Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230322222828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto%27s_failed_plea_to_Raikage.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto unsuccessfully pleas the Raikage to forgive Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Recovering later, Naruto asked Yamato and Kakashi to take him to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Iron" title="Land of Iron">Land of Iron</a>, so that he could ask <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Raikage" class="mw-redirect" title="Fourth Raikage">Fourth Raikage</a> to pardon Sasuke. Upon arrival, the Raikage rejected Naruto's request even with Kakashi and Yamato's assistance and berated him for defending a criminal. Naruto went to a local inn to ponder his next course of action, but was soon confronted by <a href="/wiki/Tobi" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobi">Tobi</a>, who wanted to understand Nagato's change of heart. Naruto ignored the question and demanded to know about his plans with Sasuke. Tobi told him about the <a href="/wiki/Sage_of_the_Six_Paths" class="mw-redirect" title="Sage of the Six Paths">Sage of the Six Paths</a>, the Uchiha clan, and the truth about the <a href="/wiki/Uchiha_Clan_Downfall" title="Uchiha Clan Downfall">Uchiha Clan Downfall</a>, all of which now drove Sasuke along <a href="/wiki/Curse_of_Hatred" title="Curse of Hatred">a path of vengeance</a> against Konoha and anyone else who would dare cross his path. Naruto insisted that he could still get through to Sasuke, but Tobi laughed and left, saying that Naruto and Sasuke were fated to fight again.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/85/As_one%27s_friend.png/revision/latest?cb=20150209080724" class="image"><img alt="As one&#39;s friend" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="As one&#39;s friend.png" data-image-key="As_one%27s_friend.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/85/As_one%27s_friend.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150209080724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/85/As_one%27s_friend.png/revision/latest?cb=20150209080724" class="image"><img alt="As one&#39;s friend" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/85/As_one%27s_friend.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150209080724" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="As one&#39;s friend.png" data-image-key="As_one%27s_friend.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/85/As_one%27s_friend.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150209080724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:As_one%27s_friend.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto talks with Gaara about Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Naruto was practising his Sage Mode's sensory abilities to locate Sasuke, he was interrupted by the arrival of Sakura, <a href="/wiki/Rock_Lee" title="Rock Lee">Rock Lee</a>, Kiba and Sai. Sakura attempted to dissuade Naruto in his attempts to bring Sasuke back to Konoha by falsely telling him that she loved him. However, Naruto knew she was lying and he rejected her confession and her proposal to abandon Sasuke, stating it had nothing to do with his promise to her. After Sakura's party left, Sai's <a href="/wiki/Ink_clone" class="mw-redirect" title="Ink clone">ink clone</a> revealed that the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_11" title="Konoha 11">Konoha 11</a> had decided to kill Sasuke themselves to prevent another war, while Sakura planned to kill Sasuke herself, at Sai's unintended insistence. <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a>, who attended the <a href="/wiki/Five_Kage_Summit" title="Five Kage Summit">Five Kage Summit</a> that Sasuke attacked, arrived and revealed Tobi's declaration of the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>, telling Naruto how they would be fighting Sasuke to protect Naruto, but he did advise Naruto to consider for himself what was the right thing to do. After hearing that most of his friends have turned against Sasuke, who now wanted to unleash his vengeance on just about everyone, Naruto hyperventilated and passed out. When he awoke, he was told by Yamato that Kakashi went to stop Sakura from dealing with Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222112017" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222112017" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222112017" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222112017" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f7/Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222112017" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs._Sasuke.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke clash.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Using a shadow clone as a decoy, Naruto escaped from the inn and followed Kakashi, arriving just in time to save Sakura from being killed by Sasuke. He tried once more to reason with Sasuke, sympathising with his pain and acknowledging Itachi's sacrifice. However, Sasuke was unmoved and declared his resolve to destroy Konoha and sever the Uchiha's connection to the shinobi world. Naruto then clashed his Rasengan with Sasuke's Chidori, realising that everything in his life he could have easily gone down the same path of Sasuke. Despite his jealousy of him, he had come to like Sasuke and was glad to have met him. Undeterred, Sasuke gave Naruto two options: kill or be killed; Naruto chose neither. Tobi and <a href="/wiki/Zetsu" title="Zetsu">Zetsu</a> arrived and prepared to depart with Sasuke. Naruto resolved that if he and Sasuke were to battle again, they would kill each other, but he was willing to accept it as he would shoulder Sasuke's hatred alone. Sasuke vowed to kill Naruto first and left with Tobi and Zetsu, while Naruto and his teammates returned to Konoha, with the captive <a href="/wiki/Karin" title="Karin">Karin</a>. Naruto explained the situation to his friends and asked to fight Sasuke alone, determined to get stronger for their upcoming battle.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Power">Power</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paradise_Life_on_a_Boat">Paradise Life on a Boat</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Paradise_Life_on_a_Boat" title="Paradise Life on a Boat">Paradise Life on a Boat</a></span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Countdown">Fourth Shinobi World War: Countdown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Countdown" title="Fourth Shinobi World War: Countdown">Fourth Shinobi World War: Countdown</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a2/The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png/revision/latest?cb=20150506011736" class="image"><img alt="The Great Toad&#39;s Prediction" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Great Toad&#39;s Prediction.png" data-image-key="The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a2/The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150506011736" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a2/The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png/revision/latest?cb=20150506011736" class="image"><img alt="The Great Toad&#39;s Prediction" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a2/The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150506011736" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Great Toad&#39;s Prediction.png" data-image-key="The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a2/The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150506011736" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Great_Toad%27s_Prediction.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets with the Great Toad Sage.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Naruto was about to eat at Ichiraku, he was suddenly summoned back to Mount Myōboku by <a href="/wiki/Fukasaku" title="Fukasaku">Fukasaku</a>. He learns from the <a href="/wiki/Great_Toad_Sage" class="mw-redirect" title="Great Toad Sage">Great Toad Sage</a>'s fortune that he would meet an "<a href="/wiki/Gy%C5%ABki" title="Gyūki">octopus</a>" and would battle a "<a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Uchiha" title="Sasuke Uchiha">young man with powerful eyes</a>." When <a href="/wiki/Gerotora" title="Gerotora">Gerotora</a> was summoned to give Naruto the "key" to the <a href="/wiki/Eight_Trigrams_Seal" class="mw-redirect" title="Eight Trigrams Seal">Eight Trigrams Seal</a>, Naruto knew he would need the Nine-Tails' power for the battles to come and accepted the key. Naruto was sent back to Ichiraku, where some of the villagers asked for his autograph. Naruto was unaware that the five Kage were planning to keep him from participating in the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>. For his safety, Tsunade gave Naruto an "S-rank mission" on a <a href="/wiki/Genbu" title="Genbu">remote island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Lightning" title="Land of Lightning">Land of Lightning</a> with <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>, <a href="/wiki/Might_Guy" title="Might Guy">Might Guy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aoba_Yamashiro" title="Aoba Yamashiro">Aoba Yamashiro</a>, and other Konoha-nin as security.
</p><p>Once at the island, Naruto met <a href="/wiki/Killer_B" title="Killer B">Killer B</a>, the jinchūriki of <a href="/wiki/Eight-Tails" class="mw-redirect" title="Eight-Tails">Eight-Tails</a>, and requested to train under him after marvelling at B's mastery of his tailed beast. B refused as he was on vacation, despite Naruto's best efforts to impress him. However, when <a href="/wiki/Motoi" title="Motoi">Motoi</a> heard Naruto bumped fists with B, he took Naruto was taken to <a href="/wiki/Falls_of_Truth" title="Falls of Truth">Falls of Truth</a>, where B trained to control the Eight-Tails. Following Motoi's instructions, Naruto sat on the platform in front of the waterfall and closed his eyes to see his true self: Dark Naruto, who berated Naruto on how quickly the Konoha villagers changed their opinions of him and exclaimed that the Nine-Tails liked him better. Inside his mind, Naruto fought his dark self, but found that they were evenly matched. Breaking out of meditation, Naruto questioned Motoi about B's history in order to learn how to conquer his inner darkness.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/49/Cho-odama.png/revision/latest?cb=20210805005445" class="image"><img alt="Cho-odama" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Cho-odama.png" data-image-key="Cho-odama.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/49/Cho-odama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210805005445" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/49/Cho-odama.png/revision/latest?cb=20210805005445" class="image"><img alt="Cho-odama" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/49/Cho-odama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210805005445" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Cho-odama.png" data-image-key="Cho-odama.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/49/Cho-odama.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210805005445" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cho-odama.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto fights the Nine-Tails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto reminisced about how B and Gaara changed everyone's opinions about them and began to doubt if the Konoha villagers sincerely trusted him. After witnessing B save Motoi from a <a href="/wiki/Giant_squid" class="mw-redirect" title="Giant squid">giant squid</a> and resume their friendship, an inspired Naruto returned to the Falls of Truth and confronted Dark Naruto again. With Naruto now having faith in himself, Dark Naruto began to weaken as he asked what his reason for existing was. Naruto answered by hugging him, accepted Dark Naruto as a part of him while thanking him for pushing him to become a better person. Dark Naruto finally relented and faded. B led Naruto and Yamato to a special room in the <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Temple" title="Tailed Beast Temple">secret temple</a> behind the waterfall, where Naruto was prepared to fight the Nine-Tails for its chakra. Within his subconscious, Naruto unlocked the seal and engaged the Nine-Tails in battle using <a href="/wiki/Sage_Mode" title="Sage Mode">Sage Mode</a>. Though he appeared to have the upper hand and drain the Nine-Tails' chakra, the fox instantly planted its own hatred within its absorbed chakra, consuming Naruto.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ab/Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20141024185050" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Kushina meet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Kushina meet.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ab/Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141024185050" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ab/Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20141024185050" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Kushina meet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ab/Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141024185050" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Kushina meet.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ab/Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141024185050" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Kushina_meet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets his mother.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Just before Naruto was completely consumed, the spirit of his mother, <a href="/wiki/Kushina_Uzumaki" title="Kushina Uzumaki">Kushina Uzumaki</a>, appeared. Naruto believed that Kushina was the Nine-Tails in disguise, earning a hit on the head and an immediate apology from her, who hoped that he did not inherit her short-temper. Realising Kushina was his mother, he tearfully hugged her and the love-filled reunion purged the Nine-Tails' hatred within its drained chakra. With renewed confidence from hearing the story of his parents, Naruto battled the Nine-Tails once more. With his mother's assistance, Naruto successfully weakens the fox long enough to separate it from its chakra. Attaining the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails_Chakra_Mode" title="Nine-Tails Chakra Mode">Nine-Tails Chakra Mode</a>, Naruto imprisons the emaciated and infuriated Nine-Tails within a <a href="/wiki/Torii_Seal" title="Torii Seal">new, stronger seal</a>, apologising to it as it faded into darkness. Afterwards, Naruto learned from Kushina about his <a href="/wiki/Uzumaki_Clan" title="Uzumaki Clan">heritage</a>, the truth behind the <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tailed_Demon_Fox%27s_Attack" title="Nine-Tailed Demon Fox&#39;s Attack">Nine-Tails' attack on Konoha</a>, and how his parents gave their lives to protect him. Naruto told his mother that he could finally understand what a parent's love felt like and that he didn't blame them for what happened, instead feeling glad to be their son. As she fades away, Kushina tearfully hugged Naruto, thanking him for letting her and Minato be his parents.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png/revision/latest?cb=20120218213914" class="image"><img alt="Naruto crashes into Kisame" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto crashes into Kisame.png" data-image-key="Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120218213914" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png/revision/latest?cb=20120218213914" class="image"><img alt="Naruto crashes into Kisame" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120218213914" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto crashes into Kisame.png" data-image-key="Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b6/Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120218213914" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_crashes_into_Kisame.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto attacks Kisame.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the real world, Naruto demonstrated his Nine-Tails Chakra Mode to B and Yamato before sensing <a href="/wiki/Kisame_Hoshigaki" title="Kisame Hoshigaki">Kisame Hoshigaki</a> of <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a> hidden inside his <a href="/wiki/Samehada" title="Samehada">Samehada</a> via <a href="/wiki/Negative_Emotions_Sensing" title="Negative Emotions Sensing">his negative emotions</a>. When Kisame attempted to escape, Naruto used his blinding speed to quickly smash Kisame into the wall, though his foot gets stuck. Yamato helps Naruto out while B pursues Kisame and they regroup to see Kisame's defeat by Guy. Kisame is restrained for interrogation, though he breaks free of his confinements through sheer will and summons sharks inside a <a href="/wiki/Water_prison" class="mw-redirect" title="Water prison">water prison</a> to eat him alive. Shocked by Kisame's suicide, Naruto observes that even those in Akatsuki fight for their comrades. They examine the intel that Kisame was trying to send, which turns out to be booby-trapped: they are each caught in a water prison and are trapped alongside a shark. Another shark, meanwhile, is able to escape with Kisame's intel. After they escape, Naruto is tasked with evacuating the giant animals into the <a href="/wiki/Island_Turtle" class="mw-redirect" title="Island Turtle">Island Turtle</a>'s shell and logging the island's ecology as part of his "official" <a href="/wiki/S-rank" title="S-rank">S-rank</a> mission. He remains unaware that it is a ploy to keep him away from the war.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Confrontation">Fourth Shinobi World War: Confrontation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Confrontation" title="Fourth Shinobi World War: Confrontation">Fourth Shinobi World War: Confrontation</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto_senses_the_war.png/revision/latest?cb=20230207041812" class="image"><img alt="Naruto senses the war" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto senses the war.png" data-image-key="Naruto_senses_the_war.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto_senses_the_war.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230207041812" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto_senses_the_war.png/revision/latest?cb=20230207041812" class="image"><img alt="Naruto senses the war" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto_senses_the_war.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230207041812" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto senses the war.png" data-image-key="Naruto_senses_the_war.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6e/Naruto_senses_the_war.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230207041812" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_senses_the_war.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto senses the war with Sage Mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto returned to the Falls of Truth with B to start practising his <a href="/wiki/Nine-Tails_Chakra_Mode" title="Nine-Tails Chakra Mode">Nine-Tails Chakra Mode</a>, specifically learning how to use <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Ball" title="Tailed Beast Ball">Tailed Beast Balls</a>. Since Tailed Beast Balls couldn't be made without the Nine-Tails' cooperation, Naruto tried to create the <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Rasengan" title="Tailed Beast Rasengan">Tailed Beast Rasengan</a> as a workaround. While struggling to balance the jutsu's composition, he sensed a <a href="/wiki/Kinkaku" title="Kinkaku">distant source</a> of the Nine-Tails' chakra. Naruto left the Falls of Truth to investigate and was met by a contingent of Konoha-nin, amongst them <a href="/wiki/Iruka_Umino" title="Iruka Umino">Iruka Umino</a>. Iruka tried to convince him to go back to his training, but Naruto bypassed them and, from entering Sage Mode, sensed the ongoing <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>. Naruto became angry that they would try to keep the war a secret from him and that they wouldn't let him help. Iruka apologised, yet still made an effort to <a href="/wiki/String_Light_Formation" title="String Light Formation">restrain</a> him. Naruto escaped and found a <a href="/wiki/Self-Repairing_Barrier" title="Self-Repairing Barrier">Self-Repairing Barrier</a>, preventing him from leaving by himself. B, at Iruka's request, decided to join him, and together they broke through the barrier.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png/revision/latest?cb=20120830133809" class="image"><img alt="Naruto in Kyubi&#39;s eye" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto in Kyubi&#39;s eye.png" data-image-key="Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120830133809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png/revision/latest?cb=20120830133809" class="image"><img alt="Naruto in Kyubi&#39;s eye" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120830133809" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto in Kyubi&#39;s eye.png" data-image-key="Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/de/Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120830133809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_in_Kyubi%27s_eye.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto states his resolve to the Nine-Tails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after, the Nine-Tails pulled Naruto into his subconscious, berating him for squandering its chakra and calling him naive for thinking he could stop the war by himself. When the Nine-Tails failed to once again tempt Naruto with power, the fox went off to claim that his attempt to put an end to hatred was futile, using his history with Sasuke as proof. Naruto responded by <a href="/wiki/Torii_Seal" title="Torii Seal">pinning</a> the fox down, refuting that it was the one who was being naive and confidently exclaiming he would find a way to deal with Sasuke and end the war. Before he leaves, Naruto also promises to resolve the Nine-Tails' own hatred someday, unnerving the fox.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Naruto_bypasses_A.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214203904" class="image"><img alt="Naruto bypasses A" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto bypasses A.png" data-image-key="Naruto_bypasses_A.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Naruto_bypasses_A.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150214203904" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Naruto_bypasses_A.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214203904" class="image"><img alt="Naruto bypasses A" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Naruto_bypasses_A.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150214203904" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto bypasses A.png" data-image-key="Naruto_bypasses_A.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a5/Naruto_bypasses_A.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150214203904" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_bypasses_A.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto outpaces A.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On their way to the battlefield, Naruto and B were met by the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Raikage" class="mw-redirect" title="Fourth Raikage">Fourth Raikage</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tsunade" title="Tsunade">Tsunade</a>, both intent on stopping the jinchūriki. B tried to convince the Raikage to let them go, and when that failed, Naruto tried to get around them, but the Raikage's <a href="/wiki/Lightning_Release_Chakra_Mode" title="Lightning Release Chakra Mode">Lightning Release Chakra Mode</a> was too fast for that. The Raikage became increasingly aggressive in his determination to stop Naruto and B from joining the war effort, going so far as to threaten to kill Naruto if it would keep Akatsuki from capturing the Nine-Tails. First B and then Tsunade joined Naruto in arguing to allow them to fight, which the Raikage relented to once Naruto dodges his maximum speed. On Tsunade's orders, <a href="/wiki/Shikaku_Nara" title="Shikaku Nara">Shikaku Nara</a> contacted Naruto and informed him about Akatsuki's <a href="/wiki/White_Zetsu_Army" title="White Zetsu Army">White Zetsu Army</a> and the accompanying <a href="/wiki/Impure_World_Reincarnation" class="mw-redirect" title="Impure World Reincarnation">Impure World Reincarnations</a>. Naruto and B soon afterwards encountered a squad of seeming Allied forces, but with his Nine-Tails Chakra Mode's <a href="/wiki/Negative_Emotions_Sensing" title="Negative Emotions Sensing">ability</a>, it allowed him to detect them as disguised Zetsu. He quickly defeated them and sent shadow clones to various other battlefields to lend assistance.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f9/Naruto_kills_dog.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222111845" class="image"><img alt="Naruto kills dog" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto kills dog.png" data-image-key="Naruto_kills_dog.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f9/Naruto_kills_dog.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222111845" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f9/Naruto_kills_dog.png/revision/latest?cb=20150222111845" class="image"><img alt="Naruto kills dog" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f9/Naruto_kills_dog.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222111845" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto kills dog.png" data-image-key="Naruto_kills_dog.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/f9/Naruto_kills_dog.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150222111845" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_kills_dog.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto fights Nagato.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto and B soon ran into the reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Itachi_Uchiha" title="Itachi Uchiha">Itachi Uchiha</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">Nagato</a>. They greeted Naruto and briefly caught up on what had happened since their deaths, but were quickly forced to attack by their summoner, <a href="/wiki/Kabuto_Yakushi" title="Kabuto Yakushi">Kabuto Yakushi</a>. Nagato advised Naruto and B on how to counter his jutsu while Itachi, between his own attacks, recalled the crow he planted in Naruto during their last meeting. Itachi activated the <a href="/wiki/Kotoamatsukami" title="Kotoamatsukami">Kotoamatsukami</a> of the crow's <a href="/wiki/Mangeky%C5%8D_Sharingan" title="Mangekyō Sharingan">Mangekyō Sharingan</a> to release himself from Kabuto's influence. Itachi joined Naruto and B in fighting Nagato, first by neutralising the <a href="/wiki/Rinnegan_Summoning" class="mw-redirect" title="Rinnegan Summoning">Rinnegan Summoning</a> and then saving them from being killed by Nagato. Nagato, his personality now suppressed, tried capturing them with <a href="/wiki/Chibaku_Tensei" title="Chibaku Tensei">Chibaku Tensei</a>, which the three combined efforts to destroy. While Nagato was distracted by their attack, Itachi sealed him with <a href="/wiki/Susanoo" title="Susanoo">Susanoo</a>. His personality restored, Nagato used his last moments to apologise and put his faith in Naruto. Afterwards, Itachi destroyed the crow, its Kotoamatsukami too valuable to let fall into the wrong hands. He left to find Kabuto so that he could end the Impure World Reincarnation, but not before telling Naruto to let his friends support him and leaving Sasuke's reform to him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e1/Mujun.png/revision/latest?cb=20150220083855" class="image"><img alt="Mujun" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mujun.png" data-image-key="Mujun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e1/Mujun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083855" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e1/Mujun.png/revision/latest?cb=20150220083855" class="image"><img alt="Mujun" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e1/Mujun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083855" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mujun.png" data-image-key="Mujun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e1/Mujun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150220083855" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mujun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto defeats the Third Raikage.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A shadow clone arrived at the site of the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Division" title="Fourth Division">Fourth Division</a>'s battle with various reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Kage" title="Kage">Kage</a>. Naruto was able to land a sneak attack on <a href="/wiki/M%C5%AB" title="Mū">Mū</a>, allowing the <a href="/wiki/Third_Tsuchikage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Tsuchikage">Third Tsuchikage</a> to seal him before he could say anything. The Tsuchikage went to help <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a> fight the <a href="/wiki/Second_Mizukage" class="mw-redirect" title="Second Mizukage">Second Mizukage</a>, leaving Naruto to fight the <a href="/wiki/Third_Raikage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Raikage">Third Raikage</a> along with the other members of the Fourth Division. Like the Fourth Raikage, the Third was very fast, easily dodging most attacks. The few attacks that did land had almost no effect, his body's natural defence was too high, and the Raikage's offences allowed him to break through every attempt to contain him. When Naruto noticed that the Raikage had a scar from his fight with the Eight-Tails years earlier, he contacted it via B to ask how the Raikage received the scar.
