Upon hearing the Eight-Tails' answer, Naruto surmises the scar was self-inflicted, confirming it as he manipulates the Third into piercing his own body. The Third is sealed and Naruto regroups with the Tsuchikage and Gaara, who already defeated the Second Mizukage.
</p><p>As Naruto and B continued onwards, Naruto's shadow clones started arriving at various locations. In the anime, shadow clones were able to: save the members of the <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Recovery_Team" title="Sasuke Recovery Team">Sasuke Recovery Team</a> from the reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Sound_Four" title="Sound Four">Sound Four</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Space%E2%80%93Time_Technique_Formula:_Underworld_Turnover" title="Space–Time Technique Formula: Underworld Turnover">Space–Time Technique Formula: Underworld Turnover</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> update <a href="/wiki/Tatewaki" title="Tatewaki">Tatewaki</a> about the fates of the children he was responsible for during life, granting him peace and allowing him to return to the afterlife;<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> run in to <a href="/wiki/Yota" title="Yota">Yota</a>, a childhood friend, and giving Yota a chance to play with him again before releasing himself from the Impure World Reincarnation;<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NS314_149-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NS314-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NS315_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NS315-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> assist <a href="/wiki/Omoi" title="Omoi">Omoi</a> in saving the <a href="/wiki/Thundercloud_Unit" title="Thundercloud Unit">Thundercloud Unit</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Climax">Fourth Shinobi World War: Climax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War:_Climax" title="Fourth Shinobi World War: Climax">Fourth Shinobi World War: Climax</a></span>
Shadow clones arrived at all the remaining battlefields, securing Impure World Reincarnations, weeding out the Zetsu that had infiltrated the Alliance's ranks, and defeating any other remaining Zetsu. Victory seemed near when the <a href="/wiki/Sensor_Division" title="Sensor Division">Sensor Division</a> detected a new threat near the Fourth Division: Mu, who <a href="/wiki/Fission_Technique" title="Fission Technique">split</a> himself before his sealing, and the reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Madara_Uchiha" title="Madara Uchiha">Madara Uchiha</a>. Shocked by this revelation, they all wondered who the masked man, <a href="/wiki/Tobi" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobi">Tobi</a>, really was. Madara gave them little time to discuss it and attacked them immediately. He cut swaths through the Fourth Division's ranks and used his Rinnegan to avoid the clone's, the Tsuchikage's, and Gaara's counterattack. Wishing to eliminate them all at once, Madara <a href="/wiki/Tengai_Shinsei" title="Tengai Shinsei">dropped a meteorite</a> on them.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/cc/Kurama_helps_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20130801133607" class="image"><img alt="Kurama helps Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama helps Naruto.png" data-image-key="Kurama_helps_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/cc/Kurama_helps_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130801133607" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/cc/Kurama_helps_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20130801133607" class="image"><img alt="Kurama helps Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/cc/Kurama_helps_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130801133607" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama helps Naruto.png" data-image-key="Kurama_helps_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/cc/Kurama_helps_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130801133607" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama_helps_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto receives help from the Nine-Tails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While the survivors regroup, Madara tried to <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Technique" title="Summoning Technique">summon</a> the Nine-Tails. Although it failed, the fox sensed the attempt and offered some <a href="/wiki/Chakra" title="Chakra">chakra</a> to help fight Madara, preferring Naruto over the Uchiha. The shadow clone used the Nine-Tails' chakra to counter Madara's <a href="/wiki/Nativity_of_a_World_of_Trees" class="mw-redirect" title="Nativity of a World of Trees">Nativity of a World of Trees</a> with <a href="/wiki/Big_Ball_Spiralling_Serial_Zone_Spheres" title="Big Ball Spiralling Serial Zone Spheres">Big Ball Spiralling Serial Zone Spheres</a>, though the extended fighting left the clone exhausted afterwards. Madara moved in to capture it, but was parried by the arrival of Tsunade, the Fourth Raikage, and the <a href="/wiki/Fifth_Mizukage" class="mw-redirect" title="Fifth Mizukage">Fifth Mizukage</a>. The Five Kage vowed to deal with Madara themselves and asked that Naruto should instead focus on defeating Tobi. The clone dispersed just as the real Naruto converged on Tobi. Naruto and B clashed with Tobi's reincarnated <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a>, styled like a <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_of_Pain" title="Six Paths of Pain">Six Paths of Pain</a>. During the fighting, Naruto referenced another Madara and asked who Tobi really was. Realising his lie was exposed, Tobi refused to accept any particular identity, believing it to be irrelevant. Naruto was not satisfied with this answer and vowed to break Tobi's mask.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7a/Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103933" class="image"><img alt="Jinchūriki clashes" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jinchūriki clashes.png" data-image-key="Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7a/Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103933" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7a/Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png/revision/latest?cb=20150221103933" class="image"><img alt="Jinchūriki clashes" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7a/Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103933" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jinchūriki clashes.png" data-image-key="Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7a/Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150221103933" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jinch%C5%ABriki_clashes.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and B clash with the reincarnated jinchūriki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>B entered <a href="/wiki/Tailed_Beast_Mode" class="mw-redirect" title="Tailed Beast Mode">Tailed Beast Mode</a> to clear the surrounding forest that was giving him and Naruto a disadvantage against the reincarnated jinchūriki. He then tried to <a href="/wiki/Sealing_Technique:_Octopus_Hold" title="Sealing Technique: Octopus Hold">seal</a> the jinchūriki, but Tobi had them enter <a href="/wiki/Version_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Version 2">Version 2</a> forms to escape at the last second. The increased strength of the jinchūriki caused difficulties for Naruto and B. Tobi, taking advantage of the situation, nearly captured Naruto, but was blocked by the arrival of Kakashi and Guy. Their arrival balanced out the two sides, so Tobi had the <a href="/wiki/Four-Tails" class="mw-redirect" title="Four-Tails">Four-Tails</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Six-Tails" class="mw-redirect" title="Six-Tails">Six-Tails</a> enter Tailed Beast Modes as well. The Four-Tails captured Naruto in its mouth, allowing it to communicate with him. The Four-Tails, introducing itself with the name Son Gokū, was angered to be controlled by Tobi, but it doubted Naruto would be any better since humans had always sought to control it and its fellow tailed beasts. Naruto insisted he was different and Son Gokū, touched by his desire to help it, told him how to release it from Tobi's control. Naruto managed to break out of its mouth, locate the <a href="/wiki/Black_receiver" class="mw-redirect" title="Black receiver">black receiver</a>, and remove it.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/08/Kurama_teams_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20130905155937" class="image"><img alt="Kurama teams up" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama teams up.png" data-image-key="Kurama_teams_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/08/Kurama_teams_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905155937" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/08/Kurama_teams_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20130905155937" class="image"><img alt="Kurama teams up" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/08/Kurama_teams_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905155937" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama teams up.png" data-image-key="Kurama_teams_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/08/Kurama_teams_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905155937" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama_teams_up.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Kurama unite.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Son Gokū thanked Naruto for his help, but explained that it couldn't actually be saved, as it was still bound to the <a href="/wiki/Demonic_Statue_of_the_Outer_Path" title="Demonic Statue of the Outer Path">Demonic Statue of the Outer Path</a>. Before it was pulled back into the Demonic Statue, Son Gokū gave some of its chakra to Naruto and wished him luck. Tobi, having lost the use of one tailed beast, forced the others to enter Tailed Beast Modes so that the battle could be brought to an end. The Nine-Tails remarked that Naruto couldn't possibly win without its help. Naruto stated that he was not up for taking its chakra by force at the moment and that he would figure something out. However, Naruto's earlier determination to help Son Gokū moved the Nine-Tails, reminding it of the many selfless things Naruto had done during his life and the perseverance he always displayed. The Nine-Tails no longer wanted to oppose Naruto and instead offered to join him as a partner, asking only that Naruto call it by name: Kurama.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6b/Seishin_Sekai.png/revision/latest?cb=20130905162801" class="image"><img alt="Seishin Sekai" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Seishin Sekai.png" data-image-key="Seishin_Sekai.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6b/Seishin_Sekai.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905162801" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6b/Seishin_Sekai.png/revision/latest?cb=20130905162801" class="image"><img alt="Seishin Sekai" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6b/Seishin_Sekai.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905162801" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Seishin Sekai.png" data-image-key="Seishin_Sekai.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6b/Seishin_Sekai.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130905162801" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Seishin_Sekai.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets the tailed beasts.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto entered his own Tailed Beast Mode and went to save Kakashi and Guy, deflecting the other five beasts' Tailed Beast Balls. The Kurama avatar fought the beasts in close combat, forcing them to combine their Tailed Beast Balls into one against it. Kurama countered theirs with a single one of its own Tailed Beast Balls and Naruto then used the avatar's tails to grab and remove the beasts' black receivers. From the contact, Naruto was able to interface with the other beasts, who introduced themselves and, like Son Gokū, gave him portions of their chakra. Tobi recalled the beasts back into the Demonic Statue and, though irritated, remained confident in his eventual victory as he faced off with Naruto, B, Kakashi, and Guy. By the time night fell, however, Tobi was still unable to defeat them. A light eventually descended on the reincarnated jinchūriki that B had kept restrained, returning them to the afterlife and signalling that Itachi had finally defeated Kabuto.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/46/Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20221102145109" class="image"><img alt="Naruto destroys the mask of Tobi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto destroys the mask of Tobi.png" data-image-key="Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/46/Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221102145109" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/46/Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20221102145109" class="image"><img alt="Naruto destroys the mask of Tobi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/46/Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221102145109" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto destroys the mask of Tobi.png" data-image-key="Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/46/Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221102145109" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_destroys_the_mask_of_Tobi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto destroys Tobi's mask.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With his options running out, Tobi deposited the <a href="/wiki/Benihisago" title="Benihisago">Benihisago</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Kohaku_no_J%C5%8Dhei" title="Kohaku no Jōhei">Kohaku no Jōhei</a> (which contained <a href="/wiki/Gold_and_Silver_Brothers" title="Gold and Silver Brothers">portions of Kurama's chakra</a>) into the Demonic Statue which, combined with a fragment of the Eight-Tails, <a href="/wiki/Gy%C5%ABki" title="Gyūki">Gyūki</a>'s, chakra he acquired previously, was enough to start the revival of the <a href="/wiki/Ten-Tails" title="Ten-Tails">Ten-Tails</a>. Naruto, B, Kakashi, and Guy started focusing on destroying it, but were constantly stopped by Tobi and his peculiar teleportation and intangibility abilities. From the fighting, however, Kakashi noticed that Tobi's abilities were seemingly linked to his own <a href="/wiki/Kamui" title="Kamui">Kamui</a>. To take advantage of this, Kakashi had one of Naruto's shadow clones attack Tobi and, just as the clone was about to be destroyed by one of Tobi's attacks, Kakashi used Kamui on it without Tobi noticing. Naruto then attacked with a Tailed Beast Ball, which Tobi escaped by retreating to <a href="/wiki/Kamui%27s_dimension" class="mw-redirect" title="Kamui&#39;s dimension">Kamui's dimension</a>. He found the clone waiting for him there and it destroyed his mask with a Rasengan.
</p><p>When they saw his face, Guy and Kakashi recognised Tobi as their childhood friend, <a href="/wiki/Obito_Uchiha" title="Obito Uchiha">Obito Uchiha</a>, whom they'd long thought dead. Obito declined to explain his actions to them and instead attacked, which attracted Madara, who escaped the release of the Impure World Reincarnation, to their location. Seeing Madara, Naruto asked what happened to the Kage, to which the elder Uchiha replied that they were in bad condition when he left them. From that and the conversation he overheard between Madara and Obito, particularly their manipulation of Nagato, Naruto attacked in a rage. Madara reflected him and then tried to capture him and B so that the Ten-Tails could be revived in its complete form. Naruto split his attention, he and B fighting Madara's <a href="/wiki/Wood_dragon" class="mw-redirect" title="Wood dragon">wood dragon</a> with their Tailed Beast Modes and one of his shadow clones trying to help Kakashi get over the revelation that Obito was alive.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/67/Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png/revision/latest?cb=20150915092614" class="image"><img alt="Allied Forces Jutsu" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Allied Forces Jutsu.png" data-image-key="Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/67/Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150915092614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/67/Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png/revision/latest?cb=20150915092614" class="image"><img alt="Allied Forces Jutsu" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/67/Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150915092614" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Allied Forces Jutsu.png" data-image-key="Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/67/Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150915092614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Allied_Forces_Jutsu.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto with the Allied Shinobi Forces.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Obito tried to convince Naruto of the futility of resistance. Naruto insisted that protecting his comrades was always worthwhile, no matter how hopeless things may seem. His words brought Kakashi out of his slump, enabling him to start fighting Obito on his own, and energised Guy, who created an opening for Naruto and B to attack the Demonic Statue with a combined Tailed Beast Ball. The attack came too late, however, and the Ten-Tails was revived. Naruto, B, Kakashi, and Guy regrouped and coordinated an attack, but the Ten-Tails was too powerful and Madara and Obito, once they linked themselves to it, were able to deploy its powers effectively. Just before they could kill Naruto and the others, the combined remaining Allied Shinobi Forces arrived to help. Shikaku Nara, communicating to all of them from the Alliance's headquarters, staged an offensive to restrain the Ten-Tails. Although it failed, it was effective enough that Madara and Obito had the Ten-Tails destroy the distant headquarters, killing Shikaku and everyone else stationed there.
</p><p>The Allies made individual attacks against the Ten-Tails, but none had any effect. At the same time, the Ten-Tails started raining wooden skewers all over the battlefield, killing many. When one was about to hit Naruto, <a href="/wiki/Hinata" class="mw-redirect" title="Hinata">Hinata</a> shielded him with her body and <a href="/wiki/Neji" class="mw-redirect" title="Neji">Neji</a> shielded her with his own. Dying, Neji collapsed on Naruto's shoulder, asking him to be more careful in the future since many lives, Hinata's particularly, now depend on his. With his last breath, he thanked Naruto for calling him a genius all those years ago. Naruto was deeply distraught by Neji's death, which Obito tried to use as an example of the needless death that resistance caused and that could be solved in the new world he wanted to create. Hinata brought Naruto back to his senses by reminding him of all the people who had given their lives to protect him and whose memories he would be insulting if he had given up now. As Naruto thanked her, he took her hand and coated her with some of Kurama's chakra.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8a/Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20140612131231" class="image"><img alt="Naruto powered the Alliance up" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto powered the Alliance up.png" data-image-key="Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8a/Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140612131231" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8a/Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png/revision/latest?cb=20140612131231" class="image"><img alt="Naruto powered the Alliance up" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8a/Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140612131231" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto powered the Alliance up.png" data-image-key="Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8a/Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140612131231" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_powered_the_Alliance_up.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto gives chakra to the Allied Shinobi Forces.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto shared Kurama's chakra throughout the Allied Forces, increasing their strength and protecting them from harm. They all manoeuvred into a formation that Shikaku was able to communicate to them before he died and, taking the form of a bird in memory of Neji, successfully removed the Ten-Tails from Obito and Madara's control. Forced to fend for themselves, Obito sought out Naruto, criticising him for wasting his energy protecting others. Naruto replied that protecting them actually gave him strength, motivating everyone within earshot. They then sensed the Ten-Tails was about to attack, which Kakashi tried to stop with Kamui. Obito intercepted him and they teleported away, leaving the others to endure the Ten-Tails' <a href="/wiki/Tenpenchii" title="Tenpenchii">Tenpenchii</a>. Kurama's chakra protected everyone, but it faded in the aftermath; Naruto was left quite beaten up, requiring Sakura to heal him. When the Ten-Tails attacked with another Tailed Beast Ball, the Allies mustered what little defence they could. Before it could reach them, however, the Tailed Beast Ball was suddenly teleported away and Naruto's reincarnated father, <a href="/wiki/Minato_Namikaze" title="Minato Namikaze">Minato Namikaze</a>, appeared at Naruto's side.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/00/Team_7_Reunited.png/revision/latest?cb=20170321021257" class="image"><img alt="Team 7 Reunited" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Team 7 Reunited.png" data-image-key="Team_7_Reunited.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/00/Team_7_Reunited.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170321021257" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/00/Team_7_Reunited.png/revision/latest?cb=20170321021257" class="image"><img alt="Team 7 Reunited" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/00/Team_7_Reunited.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170321021257" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Team 7 Reunited.png" data-image-key="Team_7_Reunited.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/00/Team_7_Reunited.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170321021257" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Team_7_Reunited.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Team 7 reunites.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Hashirama" class="mw-redirect" title="Hashirama">First</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tobirama" class="mw-redirect" title="Tobirama">Second</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Third_Hokage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Hokage">Third Hokage</a> arrived soon afterward and, along with Minato, erected a barrier around the Ten-Tails to confine it. Sasuke arrived shortly too, at whose request the previous Hokage were reincarnated by <a href="/wiki/Orochimaru" title="Orochimaru">Orochimaru</a> and who now opposed Obito and Madara. Their fellow <a href="/wiki/Rookie_Nine" class="mw-redirect" title="Rookie Nine">Rookie Nine</a> had set aside their differences with Sasuke for the time being and joined forces in launching an attack against the Ten-Tails' <a href="/wiki/Ten-Tails_Fission" title="Ten-Tails Fission">cruft</a>. On Sai's advice, Naruto, Sasuke, and Sakura all summoned their signature animals (Naruto calling on <a href="/wiki/Gamakichi" title="Gamakichi">Gamakichi</a>) in order to focus directly on the Ten-Tails itself. Naruto and Sasuke successfully damaged the Ten-Tails' arm with a combined <a href="/wiki/Scorch_Release:_Halo_Hurricane_Jet_Black_Arrow_Style_Zero" title="Scorch Release: Halo Hurricane Jet Black Arrow Style Zero">Scorch Release: Halo Hurricane Jet Black Arrow Style Zero</a>, but it merely removed the arm to prevent the flames of Sasuke's <a href="/wiki/Amaterasu" title="Amaterasu">Amaterasu</a> from spreading.
</p><p>Before they could attack again, Obito returned, landing on top of the Ten-Tails head and seemingly about to use the <a href="/wiki/Samsara_of_Heavenly_Life_Technique" class="mw-redirect" title="Samsara of Heavenly Life Technique">Samsara of Heavenly Life Technique</a> to restore Madara to life. While everyone focused on stopping Obito, Naruto couldn't help but notice that the <a href="/wiki/Hand_seals" class="mw-redirect" title="Hand seals">hand seals</a> he was using were different from what Nagato used. Minato tried to cut Obito down, but discovered that it was too late as he sealed the Ten-Tails into his body, becoming its jinchūriki.
</p>
<h3><span id="Birth_of_the_Ten-Tails.27_Jinch.C5.ABriki"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Birth_of_the_Ten-Tails'_Jinchūriki">Birth of the Ten-Tails' Jinchūriki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Birth_of_the_Ten-Tails%27_Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Birth of the Ten-Tails&#39; Jinchūriki">Birth of the Ten-Tails' Jinchūriki</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Shuriken_hits_Obito.png/revision/latest?cb=20140925140812" class="image"><img alt="Shuriken hits Obito" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shuriken hits Obito.png" data-image-key="Shuriken_hits_Obito.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Shuriken_hits_Obito.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140812" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Shuriken_hits_Obito.png/revision/latest?cb=20140925140812" class="image"><img alt="Shuriken hits Obito" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Shuriken_hits_Obito.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140812" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shuriken hits Obito.png" data-image-key="Shuriken_hits_Obito.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Shuriken_hits_Obito.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140812" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shuriken_hits_Obito.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke attack Obito.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Obito used his new power to destroy the barrier, forcing the Hokage to put the energy they were using toward the barrier into the fight instead. Because they had immortal bodies, they launched the first attack so that the others could learn what they could about Obito's new abilities, but they were quickly defeated. Naruto and Sasuke engaged him as well, but were nearly killed, saved only by Naruto using his <a href="/wiki/Chakra_arm" class="mw-redirect" title="Chakra arm">chakra arms</a> to link to Minato so he could teleport them to safety. Just as before, Naruto and Sasuke combined their attacks, having Minato and the Second Hokage coordinate teleports so that the attack would connect. Obito's <a href="/wiki/Truth-Seeking_Ball" title="Truth-Seeking Ball">Truth-Seeking Balls</a> dissipated much of the attack and the damage that he did incur was quickly regenerated.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/72/Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20140925140701" class="image"><img alt="Naruto attacks Obito anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto attacks Obito anime.png" data-image-key="Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/72/Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140701" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/72/Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20140925140701" class="image"><img alt="Naruto attacks Obito anime" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/72/Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140701" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto attacks Obito anime.png" data-image-key="Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/72/Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140925140701" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_attacks_Obito_anime.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto attacks Obito after discovering his weakness.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>From the development and some of the previous exchanges, Minato concluded that Obito was able to neutralise <a href="/wiki/Ninjutsu" title="Ninjutsu">ninjutsu</a>. Gamakichi, wanting to make some final contribution to the fight before he was forced to return to <a href="/wiki/Mount_My%C5%8Dboku" title="Mount Myōboku">Mount Myōboku</a>, attacked with his <a href="/wiki/Starch_Syrup_Gun" title="Starch Syrup Gun">Starch Syrup Gun</a>. Minato took this opportunity to try and reason with Obito, reminding him of his former dream to become Hokage. Obito berated the title and those who had held it, as he had surpassed them. Naruto was insulted not only because that was a slight against his father, but also because he hadn't abandoned his dream of being Hokage like Obito had. The Second Hokage teleported him to Obito and he attacked with a Rasengan, which successfully damaged Obito; Naruto noticed that Gamakichi's attack wasn't neutralised and realised Obito was vulnerable to <a href="/wiki/Senjutsu" title="Senjutsu">senjutsu</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e7/Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png/revision/latest?cb=20141002132605" class="image"><img alt="Minato and Naruto bump fists" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minato and Naruto bump fists.png" data-image-key="Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e7/Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141002132605" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e7/Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png/revision/latest?cb=20141002132605" class="image"><img alt="Minato and Naruto bump fists" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e7/Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141002132605" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minato and Naruto bump fists.png" data-image-key="Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e7/Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141002132605" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minato_and_Naruto_bump_fists.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kurama and its jinchūriki join forces.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With a weakness discovered, Obito trapped the Alliance in a <a href="/wiki/Six_Red_Yang_Formation" title="Six Red Yang Formation">barrier</a> and began charging multiple Tailed Beast Balls that he would use to wipe out everyone within its confines. Minato noted that he wouldn't be able to teleport them all away in time, so Naruto came up with a different approach: he linked his chakra with Minato and remotely restored the Alliance's chakra cloaks, networking everyone in with Minato's <a href="/wiki/Flying_Thunder_God_Technique" title="Flying Thunder God Technique">Flying Thunder God Technique</a>, allowing him to teleport everyone out of the barrier. Minato did so and was afterwards very proud of his son, saying he wished they had more time to talk. Naruto replied that it was not necessary since he already met <a href="/wiki/Kushina" class="mw-redirect" title="Kushina">his mother</a> and that she explained everything. Naruto and Minato each entered Tailed Beast Modes, with Naruto merging his with Sage Mode in order to imbue their shared Rasengan with senjutsu. The Second teleported them to Obito and they attacked, but he blocked it with his Truth-Seeking Balls.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fe/Obito_vs_Titans.png/revision/latest?cb=20150901144314" class="image"><img alt="Obito vs Titans" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Obito vs Titans.png" data-image-key="Obito_vs_Titans.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fe/Obito_vs_Titans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150901144314" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fe/Obito_vs_Titans.png/revision/latest?cb=20150901144314" class="image"><img alt="Obito vs Titans" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fe/Obito_vs_Titans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150901144314" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Obito vs Titans.png" data-image-key="Obito_vs_Titans.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/f/fe/Obito_vs_Titans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150901144314" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Obito_vs_Titans.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A senjutsu-enhanced Naruto and Sasuke attack Obito.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To move ahead with his plans, Obito created a replica of the <a href="/wiki/God_Tree" title="God Tree">God Tree</a>, the first step in performing the <a href="/wiki/Infinite_Tsukuyomi" title="Infinite Tsukuyomi">Infinite Tsukuyomi</a>. The tree started absorbing chakra from those nearby until they die, a fate that Naruto nearly succumbed to until he was saved by the Third Hokage. Obito pointed to the growing number of casualties as further evidence that Naruto should stop resisting, an argument that Naruto was increasingly having trouble ignoring. Sasuke, unmoved by Obito's words, used Susanoo to hack through the tree and then mocked Naruto for giving up. Naruto was reminded of his desire to not lose Sasuke or anyone else for that matter and, reinvigorated, joined Sasuke in the offensive. Although their senjutsu-enhanced Tailed Beast Mode and Susanoo could compete with Obito, they were individually unable to defeat him. Obito continued trying to convince Naruto to stop, but he ignored him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/37/Obito_is_taken_down.png/revision/latest?cb=20141030115428" class="image"><img alt="Obito is taken down" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Obito is taken down.png" data-image-key="Obito_is_taken_down.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/37/Obito_is_taken_down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141030115428" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/37/Obito_is_taken_down.png/revision/latest?cb=20141030115428" class="image"><img alt="Obito is taken down" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/37/Obito_is_taken_down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141030115428" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Obito is taken down.png" data-image-key="Obito_is_taken_down.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/37/Obito_is_taken_down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141030115428" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Obito_is_taken_down.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke slash through Obito.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sasuke then coated his Susanoo around Naruto's Tailed Beast Mode, granting the Kurama-avatar a sword and armour. Sensing that it was the final exchange, Obito created a <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Nunoboko" title="Sword of Nunoboko">sword and shield</a> of his own out of Truth-Seeking Balls. Naruto created a Rasengan in each of the Kurama-avatar's tails, which his friends from Konoha guide in a coordinated assault to Obito's shield, destroying it. As soon as Naruto and Sasuke sliced through Obito with their sword, the tailed beasts then began to emerge from the Uchiha's body, giving Naruto and the combined Allied Shinobi Forces the opportunity to pull them out. The tug-of-war for the tailed beasts linked Naruto's consciousness with Obito's. Naruto reminded Obito of his earlier claim that he was nobody and set out to prove to him that he was Obito Uchiha, specifically the Obito Uchiha that Kakashi used to know. Naruto pointed out their similarities, how both were orphans and that, because of that, they wanted to be Hokage. Obito agreed that they were similar, but that was the reason why he has been trying so hard to convince Naruto that he was right, and insisted that the world he wanted to create was a better one because his vision of the future was clear, whereas the future of the current world was ambiguous. Naruto argued that was the point and that uncertainty, when faced with comrades, was worthwhile, and offered Obito his hand so that they might see what happened together.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20141225125851" class="image"><img alt="Kurama extracted from Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama extracted from Naruto.png" data-image-key="Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141225125851" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20141225125851" class="image"><img alt="Kurama extracted from Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141225125851" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama extracted from Naruto.png" data-image-key="Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141225125851" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama_extracted_from_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kurama is extracted from Naruto by Madara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Allies successfully removed the tailed beasts from Obito and he fell to the ground, defeated. Minato and Kakashi insisted that Obito be left to them while Naruto and the rest of the Alliance should focus on Madara. They did so, joining forces with the First Hokage against him, but right before he could seal him, Madara put one final fail-safe into effect: he had <a href="/wiki/Black_Zetsu" title="Black Zetsu">Black Zetsu</a> force Obito to revive him. Madara quickly neutralised the First, fended off Naruto, Sasuke, and Sai, and then went after the freed tailed beasts. Naruto entered Tailed Beast Mode and assisted them with fighting him off. They were initially successful, but when Madara reacquired one of his <a href="/wiki/Rinnegan" title="Rinnegan">Rinnegan</a>, he easily defeated them with <a href="/wiki/Limbo:_Border_Jail" title="Limbo: Border Jail">Limbo: Border Jail</a>, sealing them all back into the Demonic Statue, including B's Gyūki and Naruto's Kurama.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Obito_Saving_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150625113652" class="image"><img alt="Obito Saving Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Obito Saving Naruto.png" data-image-key="Obito_Saving_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Obito_Saving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150625113652" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Obito_Saving_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20150625113652" class="image"><img alt="Obito Saving Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Obito_Saving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150625113652" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Obito Saving Naruto.png" data-image-key="Obito_Saving_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/42/Obito_Saving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150625113652" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Obito_Saving_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Obito transfers his tailed beasts' chakra into Naruto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The removal of Kurama from his body caused Naruto to pass out and placed his life in immediate danger. His <a href="/wiki/Uzumaki" class="mw-redirect" title="Uzumaki">Uzumaki</a> heritage prevented him from dying instantly, but he required constant medical attention from Sakura in order to keep him alive. On the advice of Kurama right before it was extracted, Gaara took Naruto to Minato so that Minato's portion of Kurama's chakra could be sealed into him, saving him. Kakashi sent Naruto and Sakura to <a href="/wiki/Kamui%27s_dimension" class="mw-redirect" title="Kamui&#39;s dimension">Kamui's dimension</a> so that she could continue performing life support without interruption. Obito soon arrived to help her, having overcome both Black Zetsu and Madara in order to acquire Minato's half of Kurama and give it to Naruto, as his form of penance.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/3e/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png/revision/latest?cb=20221004212858" class="image"><img alt="Naruto &amp; Sasuke obtain Rikudo Power" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto &amp; Sasuke obtain Rikudo Power.png" data-image-key="Naruto_%26amp%3B_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/3e/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004212858" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/3e/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png/revision/latest?cb=20221004212858" class="image"><img alt="Naruto &amp; Sasuke obtain Rikudo Power" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/3e/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004212858" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto &amp; Sasuke obtain Rikudo Power.png" data-image-key="Naruto_%26amp%3B_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/3e/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221004212858" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_%26_Sasuke_obtain_Rikudo_Power.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke accept Hagoromo's power.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While on the border of life and death, Naruto was met by the Sage of Six Paths, <a href="/wiki/Hagoromo_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki">Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki</a>. He explained his past conflicts with his mother, <a href="/wiki/Kaguya_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kaguya Ōtsutsuki">Kaguya Ōtsutsuki</a>, and the conflicts that emerged between his sons, <a href="/wiki/Asura" class="mw-redirect" title="Asura">Asura</a> and <a href="/wiki/Indra" class="mw-redirect" title="Indra">Indra</a>. His sons' conflict had continued through the centuries, with their chakra reincarnated every generation in new individuals to fight anew; Naruto was the current reincarnation of Asura, while Sasuke was the reincarnation of Indra. Naruto was not greatly surprised, having sensed something like that when he met Sasuke during the <a href="/wiki/Five_Kage_Summit" title="Five Kage Summit">Five Kage Summit</a>. Because of Madara's aims for the world, Hagoromo asked that he and Sasuke join forces to stop him, a task he was only encouraged by from the tailed beasts' positive words concerning Naruto. He gave Naruto the <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Yang_Power" title="Six Paths Yang Power">Six Paths Yang Power</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chakra#Six_Paths_Chakra" title="Chakra">half his chakra</a> and <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Sage_Mode" title="Six Paths Sage Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</a> to help him in this goal.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bc/Madara_Attacked.png/revision/latest?cb=20150813125145" class="image"><img alt="Madara Attacked" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Madara Attacked.png" data-image-key="Madara_Attacked.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bc/Madara_Attacked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813125145" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bc/Madara_Attacked.png/revision/latest?cb=20150813125145" class="image"><img alt="Madara Attacked" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bc/Madara_Attacked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813125145" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Madara Attacked.png" data-image-key="Madara_Attacked.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bc/Madara_Attacked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150813125145" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Madara_Attacked.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke strike Madara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Naruto woke up, he had Obito send him back to the real world. There, he stopped Madara from killing Might Guy and used Hagoromo's power to stabilise Guy's life force from using the <a href="/wiki/Eight_Gates_Released_Formation" title="Eight Gates Released Formation">Eight Gates Released Formation</a>. Surprised by Naruto's sudden increase in power, Madara was hit by Naruto's <a href="/wiki/Sage_Art:_Lava_Release_Rasenshuriken" title="Sage Art: Lava Release Rasenshuriken">Sage Art: Lava Release Rasenshuriken</a>, which was fueled by Son Gokū's chakra and instantly cut down the giant tree Obito created earlier. When Sasuke arrived, Naruto entered <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Sage_Mode" title="Six Paths Sage Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</a> and they started overwhelming Madara. Realising his window was closing, Madara went after Kakashi and took his Mangekyō Sharingan, using it to follow Obito. Sakura appeared shortly afterward, sent by Obito so Madara wouldn't kill her. She could do nothing about Kakashi's eye, so Naruto used Hagoromo's power to restore the one he lost years ago.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/03/Clones_vs_Shadows.png/revision/latest?cb=20150820123333" class="image"><img alt="Clones vs Shadows" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Clones vs Shadows.png" data-image-key="Clones_vs_Shadows.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/03/Clones_vs_Shadows.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150820123333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/03/Clones_vs_Shadows.png/revision/latest?cb=20150820123333" class="image"><img alt="Clones vs Shadows" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/03/Clones_vs_Shadows.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150820123333" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Clones vs Shadows.png" data-image-key="Clones_vs_Shadows.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/03/Clones_vs_Shadows.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150820123333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Clones_vs_Shadows.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's clones facing Madara's clones.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Madara soon returned, now having both his Rinnegan and Black Zetsu in control of Obito's body. Naruto and Sasuke immediately resumed their attack, but Madara had an easier time with them. He rose into the sky, raining <a href="/wiki/Chibaku_Tensei" title="Chibaku Tensei">Chibaku Tensei</a> on them to keep them busy while he projected the <a href="/wiki/Infinite_Tsukuyomi" title="Infinite Tsukuyomi">Infinite Tsukuyomi</a> on the world. While Naruto destroyed the remaining satellite-like constructs, Sasuke shielded him, Sakura, and Kakashi with Susanoo from the Infinite Tsukuyomi's gaze. He let them out once the illusion was finished casting and they emerged to find themselves alone, with the rest of the world being wrapped into Madara's <a href="/wiki/God:_Nativity_of_a_World_of_Trees" title="God: Nativity of a World of Trees">God: Nativity of a World of Trees</a>. As Madara confronted them and started explaining how he had saved the world, he was stabbed in the back by Black Zetsu. Black Zetsu then transferred to Madara's body from Obito's and forced him to absorb the world's chakra, converting him into a woman that Naruto and Sasuke recognised as Kaguya Ōtsutsuki.
</p>
<h3><span id="Kaguya_.C5.8Ctsutsuki_Strikes"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaguya_Ōtsutsuki_Strikes">Kaguya Ōtsutsuki Strikes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kaguya_%C5%8Ctsutsuki_Strikes" title="Kaguya Ōtsutsuki Strikes">Kaguya Ōtsutsuki Strikes</a></span>
Kaguya detected that Naruto and Sasuke as the reincarnations of Asura and Indra, and also that her son Hagoromo had given them the power to defeat her. Not wanting to further the damage the world that their fighting would cause, she <a href="/wiki/Amenominaka" title="Amenominaka">shifted</a> them all to one of <a href="/wiki/Kaguya%27s_Dimension" class="mw-redirect" title="Kaguya&#39;s Dimension">her dimensions</a>, placing them above a sea of lava. Sasuke summoned his <a href="/wiki/Hawk" title="Hawk">hawk</a> <a href="/wiki/Garuda" title="Garuda">Garuda</a> to save himself and Naruto, but ignored Naruto's pleas to save Sakura, Kakashi, and Obito too since only he and Naruto were vital to the fight. Kakashi was able to briefly stop their fall, but the heat burned the scroll he used to save them and it was only Naruto's sudden discovery that he was able to levitate that saved them from the lava. He left a shadow clone to hold onto them and engaged Kaguya, creating an opening for Sasuke to attack.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/83/Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png/revision/latest?cb=20160602115905" class="image"><img alt="Kaguya Freezes Boys" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaguya Freezes Boys.png" data-image-key="Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/83/Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160602115905" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/83/Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png/revision/latest?cb=20160602115905" class="image"><img alt="Kaguya Freezes Boys" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/83/Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160602115905" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaguya Freezes Boys.png" data-image-key="Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/83/Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160602115905" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaguya_Freezes_Boys.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaguya thwarts Naruto and Sasuke's sealing attempt.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sasuke's attack failed and Naruto must save him from the lava. With their attacks ineffective and the environment such a hazard, Naruto and Sasuke discussed what to do. Kaguya appeared behind them and paralysed them, binding them with Black Zetsu while she started absorbing their chakra. Black Zetsu took the opportunity to expand on the history earlier given by Hagoromo, painting Kaguya as the victim of her sons, Hagoromo and <a href="/wiki/Hamura" class="mw-redirect" title="Hamura">Hamura</a>. Black Zetsu had for centuries been manipulating others toward the outcome of reviving her, and only then had it finally succeeded. It encouraged them to bask in the embrace of their oblivion, but Naruto refused, breaking himself and Sasuke free. Needing to take drastic action, Naruto used his "ultimate" jutsu: <a href="/wiki/Sexy:_Reverse_Harem_Technique" class="mw-redirect" title="Sexy: Reverse Harem Technique">Sexy: Reverse Harem Technique</a>. Kaguya was so distracted that she was nearly sealed, but she recomposed herself in time to shift dimensions again, freezing Naruto and Sasuke in place.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/88/Naruto_Region_Combo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160804114947" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Region Combo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Region Combo.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Region_Combo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/88/Naruto_Region_Combo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160804114947" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/88/Naruto_Region_Combo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160804114947" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Region Combo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/88/Naruto_Region_Combo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160804114947" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Region Combo.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Region_Combo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/88/Naruto_Region_Combo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160804114947" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Region_Combo.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto overwhelms Kaguya with shadow clones.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Because Naruto and Sasuke were only a threat to her when together, Kaguya <a href="/wiki/Yomotsu_Hirasaka" title="Yomotsu Hirasaka">sent</a> Sasuke to a different dimension while she focused on Naruto. While Kaguya manipulated the ice dimension against him, his shadow clone explained to Kakashi, Sakura, and the now-awake Obito that his and Sasuke's powers were both necessary to defeat her. Obito offered to use his Kamui to try and explore Kaguya's dimensions to find Sasuke. To give Obito an opening, Naruto used <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Region_Combo" title="Naruto Region Combo">Naruto Region Combo</a> to overwhelm Kaguya, forcing her to retreat to another dimension to get her bearings. When she did so, Obito infiltrated the dimension Kaguya went to with Sakura and the shadow clone. The shadow clone faced her so that she wouldn't notice them while they look for Sasuke. Kaguya returned to the ice dimension and resumed her fight with the army of Naruto's clones. He kept her preoccupied until Obito returned with Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ed/Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png/revision/latest?cb=20160818114419" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Attacks Kaguya" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Attacks Kaguya.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ed/Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160818114419" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ed/Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png/revision/latest?cb=20160818114419" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Attacks Kaguya" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ed/Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160818114419" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Attacks Kaguya.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/ed/Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160818114419" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Attacks_Kaguya.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto separates Black Zetsu from Kaguya.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Increasingly frustrated, Kaguya shifted them to another dimension with powerful gravity to immobilise Naruto and Sasuke while she attacked with her <a href="/wiki/All-Killing_Ash_Bones" title="All-Killing Ash Bones">All-Killing Ash Bones</a>. Kakashi and Obito used themselves to shield the attack, with Obito then using Kamui to protect Kakashi, leaving Obito unable to defend himself. Naruto tried to heal the damage to his body, but even Hagoromo's power couldn't save him. While Sasuke fought Kaguya, Obito thanked Naruto for reminding him of who he was and made him promise to become Hokage for both their sakes. Naruto agreed and Obito's body crumbled. Black Zetsu ridiculed Obito for living an insignificant life and dying an insignificant death. Enraged, Naruto severed Kaguya's arm, in the sleeve of which Black Zetsu had been hiding, and then pinned it to the ground with his Truth-Seeking Balls.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7c/Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png/revision/latest?cb=20160825114025" class="image"><img alt="Kaguya&#39;s Defeat" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaguya&#39;s Defeat.png" data-image-key="Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7c/Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825114025" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7c/Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png/revision/latest?cb=20160825114025" class="image"><img alt="Kaguya&#39;s Defeat" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7c/Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825114025" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaguya&#39;s Defeat.png" data-image-key="Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7c/Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160825114025" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaguya%27s_Defeat.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Team 7 defeats Kaguya.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto and his shadow clones attacked Kaguya with <a href="/wiki/Sage_Art:_Super_Tailed_Beast_Rasenshuriken" title="Sage Art: Super Tailed Beast Rasenshuriken">Sage Art: Super Tailed Beast Rasenshuriken</a>. On impact, the tailed beasts' chakra within her began reacting and Kaguya started losing control of her form. She was able to reconfigure herself and prepared an <a href="/wiki/Expansive_Truth-Seeking_Ball" title="Expansive Truth-Seeking Ball">Expansive Truth-Seeking Ball</a> to destroy them. Kakashi interfered, using Susanoo (a last gift from Obito) to make an opening for Naruto and Sasuke. She tried to escape, but Sakura punched her to keep her in place, allowing Naruto and Sasuke to trigger <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_%E2%80%94_Chibaku_Tensei" title="Six Paths — Chibaku Tensei">Six Paths — Chibaku Tensei</a>. The tailed beasts were removed from her, Madara was spat out, and she was entombed in her own dimension. Not wanting Black Zetsu to scheme for her release again, Naruto made a point to trap it with her but not before telling it that a spoiled brat like it has no right to compare itself with the men and women who truly shaped shinobi history.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0c/Minato_leaving_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20160901115517" class="image"><img alt="Minato leaving Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minato leaving Naruto.png" data-image-key="Minato_leaving_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0c/Minato_leaving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160901115517" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0c/Minato_leaving_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20160901115517" class="image"><img alt="Minato leaving Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0c/Minato_leaving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160901115517" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minato leaving Naruto.png" data-image-key="Minato_leaving_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/0c/Minato_leaving_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160901115517" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minato_leaving_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minato wishes happy birthday to Naruto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Team 7 wondered how they would return to their world. Sensing their need, Hagoromo combined the efforts of the dead Kage to summon them, the tailed beasts, and Madara back. Hagoromo thanked them for saving the world, as did the tailed beasts for saving them. Naruto happily greeted to his original Kurama, asking if it missed him, to which the flustered fox denied. After Madara died from his ordeal, Naruto met with Minato who, as day broke, wished him a happy seventeenth birthday. As Hagoromo returned Minato's and the souls of the other dead Kage to the <a href="/wiki/Pure_Land" title="Pure Land">Pure Land</a>, Minato voiced his pride in Naruto and promised to tell Kushina everything about him. The other Kage also gave words of parting, which Naruto tearfully accepted.
</p><p>With all threats gone, Hagoromo explained that the Infinite Tsukuyomi could be released if Naruto and Sasuke combine their chakra. Sasuke agreed to this, but first he wanted to kill the Kage and destroy the tailed beasts, believing both were inhibitive to world peace. When he was unwilling to back down from his threat, the tailed beasts moved in to stop Sasuke, but he captured each in their own Chibaku Tensei. Hagoromo recognised that as a continuation of Indra's feud with Asura, but lacked the time and power to do anything about it. Sakura tried to reason with Sasuke, but he knocked her out and left. Naruto followed after him, promising to Hagoromo that he would bring him around and finally end the centuries-long feud.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png/revision/latest?cb=20210623032601" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Sasuke begins.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210623032601" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png/revision/latest?cb=20210623032601" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210623032601" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs. Sasuke begins.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/e/e5/Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210623032601" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs._Sasuke_begins.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke begin their rematch at the Valley of the End.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto and Sasuke ended up at the <a href="/wiki/Valley_of_the_End" title="Valley of the End">Valley of the End</a>, where they fought years ago. Sasuke stated his willingness to bear the world's burdens by himself and live independently of the past, neither of which Naruto believed were possible, or at least wise. He tells Sasuke it's impossible to do everything alone like he plans to, pointing to the missteps Itachi made and their own successful teamwork against Kaguya. Sasuke replies that he only wants to remake a better world, one where he can, like Itachi before, be solely responsible for the difficult decisions that must be made so that nobody else needs to; this is what he believes a true "Hokage" to be. Naruto insists he will be Hokage, not Sasuke, because Sasuke is still going against what Itachi wanted for him and they start fighting.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/40/Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160929112839" class="image"><img alt="Kurama vs Susanoo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama vs Susanoo.png" data-image-key="Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/40/Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929112839" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/40/Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160929112839" class="image"><img alt="Kurama vs Susanoo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/40/Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929112839" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama vs Susanoo.png" data-image-key="Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/40/Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160929112839" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama_vs_Susanoo.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke's attacks collide.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After a brief exchange of blows reminiscent of their fight years ago, Naruto and Sasuke started trading punches with their Tailed Beast Mode and Susanoo respectively. Sasuke chastised Naruto for not attacking with an intent to kill, but Naruto, like last time, was unwilling to do so, not wishing for either of them to go without the other. Naruto then clashed his Tailed Beast Ball with Sasuke's Susanoo-supported Chidori, producing a large explosion that does noticeable but not debilitating damage to their respective avatars. Each therefore powered up the avatars, Sasuke by channelling the captured tailed beasts into his Susanoo and Naruto by merging his avatar with the avatars of two shadow clones. The two met attacks once again, creating a giant explosion that stripped away their avatars and left them with too little chakra to use practically. They instead resorted to <a href="/wiki/Taijutsu" title="Taijutsu">taijutsu</a>, kicking and punching each other into the night.
</p>
