<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001023655" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke Vs Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sasuke Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161001023655" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001023655" class="image"><img alt="Sasuke Vs Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161001023655" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sasuke Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4d/Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161001023655" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sasuke_Vs_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke's final clash.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the two battled near exhaustion, Kurama mustered enough chakra for Naruto to make one last attack, but Sasuke <a href="/wiki/Preta_Path" title="Preta Path">absorbed</a> it. Having expected this, Naruto delivered a solid punch, finally irritating Sasuke over the endless repetition of their fight. Kurama gave the last of its chakra to Naruto, who used it to make a Rasengan to counter Sasuke's Chidori. Both woke up later to find that much of the Valley of the End had been destroyed, that they had each lost an arm, and that neither could move. Sasuke reflected that Naruto had been a constant obstacle to his goals, but that he was also the only person who never given up on him. Naruto's usual response that they were friends didn't convince Sasuke since it obviously went beyond, so Naruto elaborated that he experienced pain if he didn't have Sasuke. Sasuke was awed, knowing full well that Naruto had experienced various misfortunes in his life, smiled through all of them, yet would suffer without Sasuke.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b4/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png/revision/latest?cb=20161006113834" class="image"><img alt="Naruto &amp; Sasuke Wounded" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto &amp; Sasuke Wounded.png" data-image-key="Naruto_%26amp%3B_Sasuke_Wounded.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b4/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161006113834" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b4/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png/revision/latest?cb=20161006113834" class="image"><img alt="Naruto &amp; Sasuke Wounded" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b4/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161006113834" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto &amp; Sasuke Wounded.png" data-image-key="Naruto_%26amp%3B_Sasuke_Wounded.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/b4/Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161006113834" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_%26_Sasuke_Wounded.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke reconnect.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When they woke up the next day, Sasuke admitted defeat for the first time in his life, as he came to accept that Naruto was just as vital to him as he was to Naruto. Kakashi and Sakura eventually tracked them down and Sakura healed them, though she couldn't do anything about their missing arms. Once they were able to walk, they returned to where the Allied Shinobi Forces were all trapped still, dispelled the Infinite Tsukuyomi according to Hagoromo's instructions, and Sasuke released the tailed beasts. With the war over, Naruto returns to the village, where he attends a mass funeral for the participants of the war. In the anime, while recovering from his injuries, Gaara and A approach Naruto and thank him for his effort during the war. Shikamaru later brings Naruto to the Academy to meet with Iruka and Kakashi, who is considering on promoting Naruto as a jōnin. However, because he never got to retake the Chūnin Exams, Naruto has to complete two years worth of studies, much to his dismay. However, Naruto is cheered up as Iruka offers to help him.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Blank_Period">Blank Period</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Parting_Ways.png/revision/latest?cb=20161013121158" class="image"><img alt="Parting Ways" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Parting Ways.png" data-image-key="Parting_Ways.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Parting_Ways.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161013121158" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Parting_Ways.png/revision/latest?cb=20161013121158" class="image"><img alt="Parting Ways" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Parting_Ways.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161013121158" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Parting Ways.png" data-image-key="Parting_Ways.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c4/Parting_Ways.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161013121158" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Parting_Ways.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke part ways.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Months after the war, Sasuke was pardoned for his crimes on the good word of Naruto and Kakashi (who had been selected to become the Sixth Hokage). Just before Sasuke left Konoha to wander the world, he was met by Naruto, who returned to him his <a href="/wiki/Forehead_protector" class="mw-redirect" title="Forehead protector">forehead protector</a>.
</p>
<div style="clear: left;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kakashi_Hiden:_Lightning_in_the_Icy_Sky">Kakashi Hiden: Lightning in the Icy Sky</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kakashi_Hiden:_Lightning_in_the_Icy_Sky" title="Kakashi Hiden: Lightning in the Icy Sky">Kakashi Hiden: Lightning in the Icy Sky</a></span>
Nearly a year after the end of the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Shinobi_World_War" title="Fourth Shinobi World War">Fourth Shinobi World War</a>, Naruto and Sai were sent to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Waves" title="Land of Waves">Land of Waves</a> to capture <a href="/wiki/Gary%C5%8D" title="Garyō">Garyō</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Ry%C5%ABha_Armament_Alliance" title="Ryūha Armament Alliance">Ryūha Armament Alliance</a>. Once they located the Alliance's hideout, Naruto launched an assault with multiple shadow clones; although he was still missing an arm, he had learned how to perform one-handed <a href="/wiki/Hand_seals" class="mw-redirect" title="Hand seals">hand seals</a>. He easily dealt with most of the Alliance's members, but was briefly stalled by the <a href="/wiki/Ice_Release" title="Ice Release">Ice Release</a> of Garyō's <a href="/wiki/Kahy%C5%8D" title="Kahyō">bodyguard</a>. Naruto distracted the bodyguard with a shadow clone for long enough to apprehend Garyō. Garyō tried to convince Naruto that the Alliance was doing good work by releasing the world from money's corruptive influence. Although sympathetic, Naruto couldn't abide their terrorist actions and escaped with Garyō on Sai's <a href="/wiki/Super_Beast_Imitating_Drawing" title="Super Beast Imitating Drawing">bird</a>.
</p><p>At some point within the next two months, Naruto received a prosthetic arm to replace the one he lost during the war. While eating at <a href="/wiki/Ramen_Ichiraku" title="Ramen Ichiraku">Ramen Ichiraku</a> one day, he saw Kakashi walking by and asked him when he would officially take on the responsibilities of Hokage. He tried to convince Kakashi by listing the many shortcomings of Tsunade, unaware that she was standing behind him; she angrily knocked Naruto unconscious. Kakashi finally accepted the Hokage position shortly after the mission involving the Ryūha Armament Alliance and the <a href="/wiki/Blood_Prison" class="mw-redirect" title="Blood Prison">Blood Prison</a>. When Naruto learned about the mission, specifically that he was expressly forbidden from being informed about it at the time, Naruto started spreading rumours about Kakashi's relationship with the Blood Prison's new warden, <a href="/wiki/Kahy%C5%8D" title="Kahyō">Kahyō</a>. Kakashi angrily attacked him and then bought him some ramen to apologise.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shikamaru_Hiden:_A_Cloud_Drifting_in_Silent_Darkness">Shikamaru Hiden: A Cloud Drifting in Silent Darkness</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru_Hiden:_A_Cloud_Drifting_in_Silent_Darkness" title="Shikamaru Hiden: A Cloud Drifting in Silent Darkness">Shikamaru Hiden (novel)</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru_Hiden:_A_Cloud_Drifting_in_Silent_Darkness_(Arc)" title="Shikamaru Hiden: A Cloud Drifting in Silent Darkness (Arc)">Shikamaru Hiden (anime)</a></span>
Naruto ran into <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru" class="mw-redirect" title="Shikamaru">Shikamaru</a> early one morning and they discussed their heavy workloads for the <a href="/wiki/Shinobi_Union" title="Shinobi Union">Shinobi Union</a>. Since Naruto's assignments were given to him by Shikamaru, he took the opportunity to complain. Shikamaru explained that Naruto, a prime candidate for an eventual Hokage position, needed to get used to it. Naruto later discussed what Shikamaru had said with <a href="/wiki/Sakura" class="mw-redirect" title="Sakura">Sakura</a>, having sensed that there was something Shikamaru was keeping from him. Sakura reminded Naruto of all the work Shikamaru did to prepare Naruto for becoming Hokage and that it likely had something to do with that. Naruto was aware of all that Shikamaru did on his behalf, but wondered if he was worth Shikamaru's trouble.
</p><p>A few days later, Naruto was approached by <a href="/wiki/Temari" title="Temari">Temari</a>, who was worried about Shikamaru's recent behaviour and now asked where he was. Naruto didn't know, and was troubled to find that neither did <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dji" class="mw-redirect" title="Chōji">Chōji</a> or <a href="/wiki/Ino" class="mw-redirect" title="Ino">Ino</a>. He finally asked Kakashi, who admitted under pressure that Shikamaru was on a secret assignment to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Silence" title="Land of Silence">Land of Silence</a>. Naruto joined Temari's team of <a href="/wiki/Suna" class="mw-redirect" title="Suna">Suna</a> ninja to go to the Land of Silence to provide assistance to Shikamaru. They interrogated the locals upon arrival and learned that Shikamaru had been captured by the <a href="/wiki/Enlightened_Ones" title="Enlightened Ones">Enlightened Ones</a>. They attacked the prison where Shikamaru was being held and successfully freed him, enabling him to complete his mission by taking the country's leader, <a href="/wiki/Gengo" title="Gengo">Gengo</a>, into custody. Afterwards, Naruto demanded that Shikamaru never keep anything from him again, otherwise their future Hokage—advisor relationship would be very problematic. Shikamaru agreed and apologised. While Shikamaru returned to Konoha, Naruto and several other Konoha and Suna shinobi remain in the Land of Silence to help the country recover from Gengo's control.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Last:_Naruto_the_Movie">The Last: Naruto the Movie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_Last:_Naruto_the_Movie" title="The Last: Naruto the Movie">The Last: Naruto the Movie</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/97/Naruto_vs_puppets.png/revision/latest?cb=20150821105522" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs puppets" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto vs puppets.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_puppets.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/97/Naruto_vs_puppets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821105522" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/97/Naruto_vs_puppets.png/revision/latest?cb=20150821105522" class="image"><img alt="Naruto vs puppets" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/97/Naruto_vs_puppets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821105522" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto vs puppets.png" data-image-key="Naruto_vs_puppets.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/97/Naruto_vs_puppets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150821105522" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_vs_puppets.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto vs. Toneri's puppets.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Rinne_Festival" title="Rinne Festival">Rinne Festival</a>, Naruto, being the hero of the village, was bombarded with gifts from various young Konoha residents. To distract Naruto from all the attention, <a href="/wiki/Konohamaru" class="mw-redirect" title="Konohamaru">Konohamaru</a> invited him over to <a href="/wiki/Hiruzen_Sarutobi" title="Hiruzen Sarutobi">his grandfather</a>'s storage, where Naruto found a scarf that <a href="/wiki/Kushina_Uzumaki" title="Kushina Uzumaki">his mother</a> had knitted for him before she passed. He happily began wearing the scarf around the village, treating it as a precious memento. Naruto attempted to discuss his new-found attention to <a href="/wiki/Hinata" class="mw-redirect" title="Hinata">Hinata</a> over ramen, but it made her uncomfortable and ran away with embarrassment, much to his confusion and leading him to chase after her. While looking for her, Naruto stumbled across a horde of <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Puppet" title="Autonomous Puppet">puppets</a> trying to abduct Hinata. After he rescued her, they were notified that Hinata's sister <a href="/wiki/Hanabi" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanabi">Hanabi</a> was kidnapped by <a href="/wiki/Toneri_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Toneri Ōtsutsuki">Toneri Ōtsutsuki</a>, and were assigned on a <a href="/wiki/Hanabi_Rescue_Team" title="Hanabi Rescue Team">team</a> to rescue her.
</p><p>Kakashi informed the team of the imminent crashing of the <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">moon</a> onto the Earth, and asked that they do what they can to stop it in case Toneri was connected in any way. They followed Hanabi's trail and were led into a cave. While traveling through it, they were caught in <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu_Ball_Trap" title="Genjutsu Ball Trap">genjutsu</a> formed from their own memories. From seeing events of his own past and some of Hinata's, Naruto was reminded of her feelings for him and realised that he felt the same way. Sakura released them from the genjutsu and they continued with the mission. After the team encountered the <a href="/wiki/Gatekeeper" title="Gatekeeper">Gatekeeper</a>, Naruto noticed that Hinata was missing and left to find her, only to discover that she was in a conversation with a <a href="/wiki/Puppet" title="Puppet">disguised</a> Toneri who he quickly defeated. Hinata wouldn't share what she discussed with the puppet, so Naruto vowed not to let her out of his sight again. They continued through the cave and eventually arrived in the moon's interior, which the team then split up to investigate the surrounding <a href="/wiki/%C5%8Ctsutsuki_clan" class="mw-redirect" title="Ōtsutsuki clan">settlement</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1b/Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png/revision/latest?cb=20150815201547" class="image"><img alt="Naruto confesses to Hinata" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto confesses to Hinata.png" data-image-key="Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1b/Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150815201547" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1b/Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png/revision/latest?cb=20150815201547" class="image"><img alt="Naruto confesses to Hinata" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1b/Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150815201547" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto confesses to Hinata.png" data-image-key="Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/1b/Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150815201547" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_confesses_to_Hinata.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto confesses to Hinata.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the team regrouped, Naruto watched Hinata as she repaired her ruined scarf. She expressed her concerns that she wasn't doing enough to save her sister, so Naruto reassured her and also told her how he felt. Toneri appeared before she could respond, prompting Hinata to give Naruto the scarf and departed with Toneri. Naruto chased after them, believing Hinata was being taken against her will. When Hinata did not deny Toneri's statement about them getting married, Naruto became too shocked to react. Toneri attacked him, destroying the scarf and leaving him badly injured. After three days of around-the-clock medical attention from Sakura, he woke up. Naruto was distraught, believing there was no reason to go on if Hinata had chosen Toneri. Sakura reassured him that Hinata couldn't really have feelings for Toneri as she loved Naruto too much, and had a reason for doing what she did. As his strength returned, Naruto vowed he would save Hinata and for her to wait for him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d1/Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711121327" class="image"><img alt="Silver Wheel Reincarnation" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Silver Wheel Reincarnation.png" data-image-key="Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d1/Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711121327" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d1/Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711121327" class="image"><img alt="Silver Wheel Reincarnation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d1/Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711121327" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Silver Wheel Reincarnation.png" data-image-key="Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d1/Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711121327" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Silver_Wheel_Reincarnation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto fighting Toneri.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The team soon infiltrated Toneri's castle and after <a href="/wiki/Sage_Mode" title="Sage Mode">locating</a> Hinata, Naruto went after her while the others rescued Hanabi. He arrived in time to interrupt Toneri's and Hinata's wedding ceremony. Toneri, who was <a href="/wiki/Puppet-Cursing_Sphere" title="Puppet-Cursing Sphere">controlling</a> Hinata, had her attack Naruto, only for him to break his control and escape with her. Hinata led him to the <a href="/wiki/Tenseigan_(Energy_Vessel)" title="Tenseigan (Energy Vessel)">Tenseigan</a> that was controlling the moon's decent, which they individually tried to destroy to no success, but <a href="/wiki/Gentle_Wind_Spiralling_Twin_Lion_Fists:_Snow_White" title="Gentle Wind Spiralling Twin Lion Fists: Snow White">together</a> they succeeded. After regrouping with the others, Hinata gave Naruto a piece of the scarf she knitted for him, which he graciously accepted. The team then attempted to flee the castle, but a furious Toneri appeared and separated the group, which gave him the opportunity to recapture Hinata. During their intense fight, Naruto managed to overcome Toneri's <a href="/wiki/Tenseigan_Chakra_Mode" title="Tenseigan Chakra Mode">new power</a> and overwhelm him by concentrating all his chakra into his fist and defeated him with a single punch, freeing Hinata in the process.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/53/Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711120642" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Hinata kiss" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Hinata kiss.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/53/Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120642" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/53/Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png/revision/latest?cb=20150711120642" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Hinata kiss" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/53/Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120642" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Hinata kiss.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/53/Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150711120642" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Hinata_kiss.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Hinata kiss.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Toneri tried one <a href="/wiki/Puppet_Reincarnation" title="Puppet Reincarnation">final attack</a>, but was unable to control its power, leading to Naruto to intervene and save him from drifting out into space. Afterwards, Hinata informed Toneri of Hamura's actual decree and he, regretful about what he did, allowed the team to return home. As they were returning to Earth, Naruto reaffirmed his feelings for Hinata and stated that he wanted to be with her for the rest of his life, much to her happiness, and the two later shared their first kiss.
</p>
<h3><span id="Sakura_Hiden:_Thoughts_of_Love.2C_Riding_Upon_a_Spring_Breeze"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sakura_Hiden:_Thoughts_of_Love,_Riding_Upon_a_Spring_Breeze">Sakura Hiden: Thoughts of Love, Riding Upon a Spring Breeze</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sakura_Hiden:_Thoughts_of_Love,_Riding_Upon_a_Spring_Breeze" title="Sakura Hiden: Thoughts of Love, Riding Upon a Spring Breeze">Sakura Hiden: Thoughts of Love, Riding Upon a Spring Breeze</a></span>
While Naruto and Hinata were <a href="/wiki/After_The_Last" title="After The Last">out on a date</a> in Konoha, they ran into Sakura. Sensing that Sakura was overworking herself, they invited her to join them, but she declined.
</p><p>One day, while Naruto was teaching a class of <a href="/wiki/Academy_student" class="mw-redirect" title="Academy student">Academy students</a> how to spar, he noticed Sakura, who was wandering around Konoha, looking distressed. Sensing that she needed a distraction, Naruto insisted that she help him, which took her mind off recent events. As thanks, Sakura informed Naruto of something she avoided telling him: there were rumours that Sasuke was trying to destroy Konoha. She didn't believe the rumours were true, but nobody had been able to get in touch with Sasuke to confirm. Naruto pointed out that Sasuke must not be worried by these rumours, otherwise he would respond to the messages he'd been sent. Sakura thought that was a good point and was put at ease.
</p><p>When Naruto and Hinata later learned that Sakura had been kidnapped by <a href="/wiki/Kido_Tsumiki" title="Kido Tsumiki">Kido Tsumiki</a>, they joined with Kakashi in going to rescue her. On finding her, however, they discovered that she had already defeated Kido. They congratulated her on her victory.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Konoha_Hiden:_The_Perfect_Day_for_a_Wedding">Konoha Hiden: The Perfect Day for a Wedding</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Hiden:_The_Perfect_Day_for_a_Wedding" title="Konoha Hiden: The Perfect Day for a Wedding">Konoha Hiden (novel)</a> and <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Hiden:_The_Perfect_Day_for_a_Wedding_(Arc)" title="Konoha Hiden: The Perfect Day for a Wedding (Arc)">Konoha Hiden (anime)</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6c/Hinata_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417154800" class="image"><img alt="Hinata &amp; Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hinata &amp; Naruto.png" data-image-key="Hinata_%26amp%3B_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6c/Hinata_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180417154800" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6c/Hinata_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417154800" class="image"><img alt="Hinata &amp; Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6c/Hinata_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180417154800" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hinata &amp; Naruto.png" data-image-key="Hinata_%26amp%3B_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/6c/Hinata_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180417154800" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hinata_%26_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Hinata preparing to be wed.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto and Hinata decided to get married and invited their friends and family. Because his parents were dead, Naruto asked <a href="/wiki/Iruka" class="mw-redirect" title="Iruka">Iruka</a> to attend as his father, which Iruka happily agreed to. On the day of the wedding, though, Naruto kept his real father in his thoughts, looking upon <a href="/wiki/Minato" class="mw-redirect" title="Minato">Minato</a>'s face on the <a href="/wiki/Hokage_Rock" title="Hokage Rock">Hokage Rock</a> with admiration as he and Hinata were about to walk down the aisle.
</p>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sasuke_Shinden:_Book_of_Sunrise">Sasuke Shinden: Book of Sunrise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Shinden:_Book_of_Sunrise" title="Sasuke Shinden: Book of Sunrise">Sasuke Shinden (novel)</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Shinden:_Book_of_Sunrise_(Arc)" title="Sasuke Shinden: Book of Sunrise (Arc)">Sasuke Shinden (anime)</a></span>
Naruto appears in the novel.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Era:_Part_I">New Era: Part I</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a4/Uzumaki_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20180614114818" class="image"><img alt="Uzumaki Family" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Uzumaki Family.png" data-image-key="Uzumaki_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a4/Uzumaki_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180614114818" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a4/Uzumaki_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20180614114818" class="image"><img alt="Uzumaki Family" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a4/Uzumaki_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180614114818" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Uzumaki Family.png" data-image-key="Uzumaki_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a4/Uzumaki_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180614114818" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Uzumaki_Family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Hinata raising their children.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after their wedding, Naruto and Hinata had <a href="/wiki/Boruto" class="mw-redirect" title="Boruto">a son</a>, and two years later they had <a href="/wiki/Himawari" class="mw-redirect" title="Himawari">a daughter</a>. In the anime, over the years, Naruto was constantly busy, leading to him not taking the Chūnin Exams. Despite being a genin, Naruto was selected to succeed Kakashi and become the Seventh Hokage.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> On the day of his inauguration, Boruto accidentally destroyed Himawari's toy, leading to Naruto stepping in to defend his son from Himawari's <a href="/wiki/Gentle_Fist" title="Gentle Fist">Gentle Fist</a>-strike, but ended up taking the blow instead, rendering him unconscious. He ended up missing his own inauguration, forcing Konohamaru to <a href="/wiki/Transformation_Technique" title="Transformation Technique">impersonate him</a> during the ceremony.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> As Hokage, he hosted a <a href="/wiki/Kage_Summit" class="mw-redirect" title="Kage Summit">Kage Summit</a> in Konoha, in which Sasuke and Sakura attended alongside the four <a href="/wiki/Kage" title="Kage">Kage</a> and their bodyguards. During the meeting, Sasuke reported that a <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Momoshiki Ōtsutsuki">threat</a> greater than Kaguya may still exist somewhere, which Naruto and the other Kage decided to keep the information between themselves to avoid causing a panic.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sasuke_Retsuden:_The_Uchiha_Descendants_and_the_Heavenly_Stardust">Sasuke Retsuden: The Uchiha Descendants and the Heavenly Stardust</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Retsuden" class="mw-redirect" title="Sasuke Retsuden">Sasuke Retsuden</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Retsuden_(manga)" class="mw-redirect" title="Sasuke Retsuden (manga)">Sasuke Retsuden (manga)</a></span>
When Naruto became afflicted with an unknown illness, Sasuke decided to go to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Redaku" title="Land of Redaku">Land of Redaku</a> when learning of stories that the Sage of Six Paths had the same illness and found a cure there. Naruto tried to talk Sasuke out of it, but he ignored his pleas.
</p><p>Ultimately, Sasuke, with the help of Sakura and Kakashi, were able to find the cure, <a href="/wiki/Polar_particles" title="Polar particles">polar particles</a>. Upon recovering, Naruto thanks his friends for their efforts
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Academy_Entrance_Arc">Academy Entrance Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D57&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Academy_Entrance_Arc" title="Academy Entrance Arc">Academy Entrance Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020030556" class="image"><img alt="Naruto welcoming Academy students" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto welcoming Academy students.png" data-image-key="Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030556" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020030556" class="image"><img alt="Naruto welcoming Academy students" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030556" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto welcoming Academy students.png" data-image-key="Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/be/Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030556" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_welcoming_Academy_students.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto welcoming the Academy students.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, Naruto partakes in the entrance ceremony at the Academy, which leads to him being mortified after Boruto arrives and damages the <a href="/wiki/Hokage_Rock" title="Hokage Rock">Hokage Rock</a>. After the incident, Naruto learns from the <a href="/wiki/Denki%27s_Father" class="mw-redirect" title="Denki&#39;s Father">Kaminarimon Company president</a> that Boruto is having a positive impact on his <a href="/wiki/Denki_Kaminarimon" title="Denki Kaminarimon">son</a>, leading to Naruto smiling. Later, as a <a href="/wiki/Nue" title="Nue">mysterious presence</a> continues to cause people in the village to randomly attack the citizens, Naruto decides to begin an investigation, which uncovers that victims are having their chakra severely drained to the point of hospitalisation.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/12/Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020030739" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Hiashi talk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Hiashi talk.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/12/Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/12/Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020030739" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Hiashi talk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/12/Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030739" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Hiashi talk.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/12/Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020030739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Hiashi_talk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Hiashi discuss Boruto's training.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, as the mysterious attack began to happen throughout the village, Naruto's efforts to uncover the truth began to exhaust him and being insisted by Shikamaru to go home and rest. Upon arriving, he learned that Boruto was acting very strange recently. Once confronting his son about his new attitude, Boruto insisted that he had finally manifested his Byakugan, leading them to talk to <a href="/wiki/Hiashi" class="mw-redirect" title="Hiashi">Hiashi</a>. Upon arriving at his household, Hiashi like Naruto had doubts that Boruto awakened the Byakugan. Deciding to test Boruto, Hanabi faces Boruto, which concluded that Boruto hadn't manifested the <a href="/wiki/D%C5%8Djutsu" title="Dōjutsu">dōjutsu</a>. Afterwards, Naruto talked with Hiashi about his grandchildren.
</p><p>After assigning Sai to investigate the attacks in the village, he returned home late, and confided in Hinata about his ineptitude in interacting with his children, believing it to stem from his growing up without parents. Sometime later, Naruto saved civilians at the Konoha Purification Plant. As Boruto decided to check on his hospitalised friends, realising that his son was conducting his own investigation on the attacks, Naruto dragged Boruto to the surgery room, showing his son what was becoming of the victims of prolonged rampages. While hoping to sway Boruto into staying out of this matter, it only strengthened Boruto's resolve. Shino then appeared, encouraging Naruto to have faith in his son as the teacher himself was recently saved by Boruto's efforts. While still weary, Naruto decided to trust Shino's judgement.
</p><p>While having dinner with his family and <a href="/wiki/Mitsuki" title="Mitsuki">Mitsuki</a>, Naruto abruptly departs to handle a matter involving strange chakra spreading across Konoha. Soon after, Sai discovered that the culprit behind these attacks was <a href="/wiki/Sumire_Kakei" title="Sumire Kakei">Sumire Kakei</a>. Naruto learned from Kakashi that Sumire's intention was to unleash the <a href="/wiki/Gozu_Tenn%C5%8D" title="Gozu Tennō">Gozu Tennō</a> on the village. Later, when Sai found Sumire, she unleashed the <a href="/wiki/Nue" title="Nue">Nue</a>. Naruto soon joined the unit to fend off the creature, but Kakashi warned Naruto to not get close, having realised that the endgame of this creature was to amass enough chakra to produce a powerful enough explosion to destroy the village. While the barrier team worked to keep the creature at bay, it suddenly teleported away. As Naruto attempted to find the creature with Sage Mode, Kakashi deduced that the creature worked differently from normal summonings, existing naturally in its own separate dimension.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/28/Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020033620" class="image"><img alt="Naruto meets up with Sasuke" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto meets up with Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/28/Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020033620" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/28/Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020033620" class="image"><img alt="Naruto meets up with Sasuke" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/28/Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020033620" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto meets up with Sasuke.png" data-image-key="Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/28/Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020033620" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_meets_up_with_Sasuke.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets up with Sasuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon Sumire turning herself in, Sai and Shikamaru notified him that it's due to Boruto appealing to Sumire's genuine love of her friends in the Academy, making Naruto relieved that decided to admit her in the first place. Later, he informs Boruto that while he must look to the welfare of the entire village and does not have absolute say, he promises to help Sumire. Ultimately, it was decided to pardon Sumire and let her return to the Academy. Later, Naruto sent a clone to meet up with Sasuke, giving him the research on the <a href="/wiki/Gozu_Tenn%C5%8D" title="Gozu Tennō">Gozu Tennō</a>. Sasuke quickly deduced that this was an attempt on Danzō to recreate Kaguya's technique. Before Sasuke departs, he asks Naruto to apologise to Sakura for his continued absence, leading to Naruto feeling responsible for.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sarada_Uchiha_Arc">Sarada Uchiha Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Gaiden:_The_Seventh_Hokage_and_the_Scarlet_Spring" title="Naruto Gaiden: The Seventh Hokage and the Scarlet Spring">Naruto Gaiden: The Seventh Hokage and the Scarlet Spring</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a7/Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020032053" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Boruto at Ichiraku Ramen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Boruto at Ichiraku Ramen.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a7/Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020032053" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a7/Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png/revision/latest?cb=20221020032053" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Boruto at Ichiraku Ramen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a7/Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020032053" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Boruto at Ichiraku Ramen.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a7/Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221020032053" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Boruto_at_Ichiraku_Ramen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Boruto having dinner at Ichiraku Ramen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, when Himawari became sick due to a fever, Naruto hurried home worried about her in which Boruto pointed out that his Hokage cloak is inside out. When Naruto and Boruto began fighting over what Himawari should eat, Hinata became angry and kicked them both out of the house due to them being noisy. Naruto then invited Boruto to eat with him at Ramen Ichiraku to try to bond with him in which he accepted. As they ate, Naruto told his son about all the precious memories he had in the shop, such as being acknowledged by Iruka, hanging out with Team 7, and going on his first <a href="/wiki/After_The_Last" title="After The Last">date</a> with Hinata.
</p><p>On the day of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Kage_Summit" title="Five Kage Summit">Five Kage Summit</a> in Konoha, <a href="/wiki/Moegi_Kazamatsuri" title="Moegi Kazamatsuri">Moegi Kazamatsuri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Udon_Ise" title="Udon Ise">Udon Ise</a> notify Naruto that Boruto had vandalised the <a href="/wiki/Hokage_Rock" title="Hokage Rock">Hokage Rock</a>. Before Boruto could do any more damage, Naruto catches and stops him. Afterwards, he gives his son a lecture about how the whole village is his family. The ordeal leads to Naruto arriving late to the kage meeting, which he apologies for.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Boruto's graduation exam from the <a href="/wiki/Academy" title="Academy">Academy</a> was approaching, Naruto used a shadow clone to help him train. Meanwhile, the real Naruto received a report from Sasuke about a <a href="/wiki/Shin_Uchiha_(Clones)" title="Shin Uchiha (Clones)">boy</a> with the Sharingan. After he consulted with Kakashi about it, Naruto decided to accompany Sasuke to a meeting with <a href="/wiki/Orochimaru" title="Orochimaru">Orochimaru</a>, leaving behind a shadow clone to manage Konoha in his absence. He made a point to leave the village before Boruto could come to see him off, though he asked Shikamaru to apologise to Boruto on his behalf.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_Protects_Kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20170816102703" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Protects Kids" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Protects Kids.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Protects_Kids.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_Protects_Kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170816102703" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_Protects_Kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20170816102703" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Protects Kids" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_Protects_Kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170816102703" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Protects Kids.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Protects_Kids.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/61/Naruto_Protects_Kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170816102703" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Protects_Kids.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto protecting Sarada and Chōchō from Shin's attack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While on his way to the rendezvous point, Naruto sensed that he was being followed by <a href="/wiki/Sarada_Uchiha" title="Sarada Uchiha">Sarada Uchiha</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dch%C5%8D_Akimichi" title="Chōchō Akimichi">Chōchō Akimichi</a>. He initially tried to ignore them, but eventually decided it would be better to confront them than to let them continue coming after him. When he arrived to speak with them, however, he found them being attacked by the same boy from Sasuke's report. Although he was pleased that they were able to hold their own against their attacker, Naruto decided to get personally involved when he saw the boy had a <a href="/wiki/Mangeky%C5%8D_Sharingan" title="Mangekyō Sharingan">Mangekyō Sharingan</a>. The boy could do nothing against Naruto's Nine-Tails Chakra Mode, so he fled with a <a href="/wiki/Sharingan_Spying_Creature" title="Sharingan Spying Creature">creature</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Shin_Uchiha%27s_Space%E2%80%93Time_D%C5%8Djutsu" title="Shin Uchiha&#39;s Space–Time Dōjutsu">space–time ninjutsu</a>. Because the boy was apparently after Sarada, Naruto allowed them to come with him so that he could keep them safe.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Sarada_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20170830111731" class="image"><img alt="Sarada &amp; Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sarada &amp; Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sarada_%26amp%3B_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Sarada_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170830111731" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Sarada_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20170830111731" class="image"><img alt="Sarada &amp; Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Sarada_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170830111731" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sarada &amp; Naruto.png" data-image-key="Sarada_%26amp%3B_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d3/Sarada_%26_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170830111731" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sarada_%26_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto comforts Sarada.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While having lunch, Naruto told Sarada about what her father was like growing up and then informed both Sarada and Chōchō in what ways they take after their parents. Sarada was not only interested to hear about Sasuke, but also found she got along quite well with Naruto. As they got close to where they were supposed to meet up with Sasuke, Sarada used the bathroom as an excuse to sneek away from Naruto and Chōchō so that she could see him first. Naruto followed, and, on arrival, was reprimanded by Sasuke for bringing children with him. Sarada explained that she came without permission, as she wanted to know if Sakura was her real mother. Sasuke ignored the question, which only upset her and caused her to storm out. Naruto tried to comfort her, but his assurances that Sasuke meant well did not improve her mood. Before he could continue, he sensed the boy's return and defended Sarada as the boy and his father, <a href="/wiki/Shin_Uchiha" title="Shin Uchiha">Shin Uchiha</a>, attack. Sasuke assisted in fighting off Shin and his son, but Shin was able to <a href="/wiki/Object_Manipulation_Technique" title="Object Manipulation Technique">manipulate</a> Sasuke's sword and used it to stab Naruto. Naruto continued attacking Shin despite his injury, though tried to use being impaled by the sword to win sympathy; Kurama ridiculed Naruto for allowing himself to be stabbed at all, but assured him that it wouldn't kill him. Sakura suddenly arrived to lend assistance and landed a fatal blow on Shin, forcing Shin to escape and took Sakura with him. Unable to detect where Shin had taken Sakura, they continued to Orochimaru's lair. Orochimaru informed them that Shin was an old experiment of his that he since lost control of. Naruto noticed Sarada sneaking off with <a href="/wiki/Suigetsu_H%C5%8Dzuki" title="Suigetsu Hōzuki">Suigetsu Hōzuki</a> during Orochimaru's explanation and followed them, listening in as Suigetsu ran a DNA test that suggested Sarada's real mother was actually <a href="/wiki/Karin" title="Karin">Karin</a>.
</p><p>Not knowing what the truth was, Naruto was upset first with Sasuke for the secret he has seemingly been keeping, but also with Suigetsu for getting involved. He approached Sarada to discuss it with her, but she lashed out at him, believing he had been a knowing participant in the lie that Sakura was her mother. When she tried to insist that having no blood relation to Sakura meant they weren't family, Naruto took a firm stance: he wasn't related to most of Konoha's villagers, yet he still considered them his family because they were important to him. In the same way, Sakura and Sarada were family because they were important to each other. Sarada realised how much she loved Sakura and decided she wanted to help rescue her. They reunited with the others and head out for Shin's hideout.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Shin_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20170906101448" class="image"><img alt="Shin Vs Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shin Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Shin_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Shin_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170906101448" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Shin_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20170906101448" class="image"><img alt="Shin Vs Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Shin_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170906101448" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shin Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Shin_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/89/Shin_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170906101448" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shin_Vs_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto facing a Shin clone.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Using Sasuke's <a href="/wiki/Rinnegan" title="Rinnegan">Rinnegan</a>, they were able to reach where Shin took Sakura, only to find Sakura faring fine on her own fighting him. With the numbers against him growing, Shin called in his sons (actually his clones) to assist, but they turned against him and killed him because he always mistreated them. The clones then turned their attention to Naruto and the others, which Naruto engaged with his own shadow clones. Because they were only children, he frightened them into surrendering by manifesting Kurama. After learning that Sakura indeed was her biological mother, Sarada reconciled with her parents, much to Naruto's happiness. Then, they all returned to Konoha, with Shin's clones being delivered to the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_Orphanage" title="Konoha Orphanage">Konoha Orphanage</a>.
</p>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="School_Trip_Arc">School Trip Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/School_Trip_Arc" title="School Trip Arc">School Trip Arc</a></span>
In the anime, to improve relationships with other villages and symbolically show the warring era was over, Naruto set up an official class trip for the Academy to go to Kirigakure. Working out the details with <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dj%C5%ABr%C5%8D" title="Chōjūrō">Chōjūrō</a>, he also got a tour guide for the class.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Graduation_Exams_Arc">Graduation Exams Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Graduation_Exams_Arc" title="Graduation Exams Arc">Graduation Exams Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/02/Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120040251" class="image"><img alt="Naruto training Konoha-nin" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto training Konoha-nin.png" data-image-key="Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/02/Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120040251" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/02/Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120040251" class="image"><img alt="Naruto training Konoha-nin" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/02/Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120040251" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto training Konoha-nin.png" data-image-key="Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/02/Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120040251" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_training_Konoha-nin.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto training with Konoha-nin.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, as Academy classes began preparing for the graduation exams, the various students were interviewed about their future goals alongside a parent. Naruto however was unable to join his son as he was busy discussing matters with Orochimaru about his research on Danzō's old experiments. As Orochimaru delivered promising results to aid Sasuke in his own investigations, while Shikamaru voiced his still limited trust in Orochimaru, Naruto was more relaxed about Orochimaru roaming the village.
</p><p>On Boruto's first day as a genin, Naruto managed to get some time to have breakfast with his family and see Boruto off to be assigned his team. After Boruto left, Shikamaru went to Naruto's house to collect him and inform him of his various duties for the day. Later on, Naruto was in a field testing a number of shinobi's skills in <a href="/wiki/Barrier_Ninjutsu" title="Barrier Ninjutsu">Barrier Ninjutsu</a> to better protect the village with <a href="/wiki/Mirai_Sarutobi" title="Mirai Sarutobi">Mirai Sarutobi</a> as his escort for the day. When Boruto and his teammates came to him, he was thinking that they want to change teams, but was pleasantly surprised when instead they want their team denomination to be changed to Team 7.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Genin_Mission_Arc">Genin Mission Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D61&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Genin_Mission_Arc" title="Genin Mission Arc">Genin Mission Arc</a></span>
In the anime, as the recently promoted genin began to prepare for their first missions, Naruto prepared to present them, as it was customary. While Boruto began bragging about how easy it will, Naruto sternly warned him not to be so cocky. He presented Team 7 with a D-rank mission to aid the Green Banks Village who were being attacked by bandits for their crops. Naruto stressed that the team show team-work to complete the mission.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Byakuya_Gang_Arc">Byakuya Gang Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D62&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Byakuya_Gang_Arc" title="Byakuya Gang Arc">Byakuya Gang Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/44/Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png/revision/latest?cb=20180404012503" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Quelling Crowd" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Quelling Crowd.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/44/Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180404012503" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/44/Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png/revision/latest?cb=20180404012503" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Quelling Crowd" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/44/Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180404012503" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Quelling Crowd.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/44/Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180404012503" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Quelling_Crowd.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto quelling the protest.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, when the <a href="/wiki/Byakuya_Gang" title="Byakuya Gang">Byakuya Gang</a> began conducting heists throughout Konoha, their act of distributing their stolen wealth to the poor began gaining much support from many of the villagers, leading to a protest breaking out after the group fooled the villages into believing the Kaminarimon Company was corrupt. After shinobi determined that the leaders of the protest were being manipulated by <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu_Cursed_Seal" title="Genjutsu Cursed Seal">genjutsu</a> and freed them, Naruto and his clones appeared before the crowds and began quelling them with his speech. Straight after, Naruto headed towards the Land of Fire's border where he apprehended <a href="/wiki/Gekk%C5%8D" title="Gekkō">Gekkō</a>, who had used the riots as a distraction to steal the <a href="/wiki/Magnum_Opus" title="Magnum Opus">Magnum Opus</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Ninjutsu_Research_Centre" title="Ninjutsu Research Centre">Ninjutsu Research Centre</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_Shinden:_Parent_and_Child_Day">Naruto Shinden: Parent and Child Day</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Shinden:_Parent_and_Child_Day" title="Naruto Shinden: Parent and Child Day">Naruto Shinden: Parent and Child Day</a> and <a href="/wiki/Parent_and_Child_Day_Arc" title="Parent and Child Day Arc">Parent and Child Day Arc</a></span>
<span class="box headnote"><b><font color="green">NOTE</font>:</b> In the anime, the events of this arc occur after the <a href="#Mitsuki&#39;s_Disappearance_Arc">Mitsuki's Disappearance Arc</a>.</span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d5/Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png/revision/latest?cb=20190211155811" class="image"><img alt="Hima and Naruto playing" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hima and Naruto playing.png" data-image-key="Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d5/Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190211155811" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d5/Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png/revision/latest?cb=20190211155811" class="image"><img alt="Hima and Naruto playing" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d5/Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190211155811" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hima and Naruto playing.png" data-image-key="Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d5/Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190211155811" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hima_and_Naruto_playing.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Himawari spending Parent and Child Day together.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After announcing <a href="/wiki/Parent_and_Child_Day" title="Parent and Child Day">Parent and Child Day</a>, Shikamaru took care of Naruto's paperwork, allowing him to spend time with Himawari. Despite being sleep deprived, Naruto accepted his daughter's wish and began searching for a Kurama doll with her. After being joined by Kiba during their unsuccessful search, he bought Himawari a Shukaku doll, to which she enjoyed. Later, with Himawari going to bed with Hinata, Naruto approached Boruto and apologised for not having spent any time during the holiday with his son. He gave Boruto a custom shuriken as a present and the two decided to spend the remainder of the evening training together.
</p>
<div style="clear: left;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Versus_Momoshiki_Arc">Versus Momoshiki Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D64&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Boruto:_Naruto_the_Movie" title="Boruto: Naruto the Movie">Boruto: Naruto the Movie</a> and <a href="/wiki/Versus_Momoshiki_Arc" title="Versus Momoshiki Arc">Versus Momoshiki Arc</a></span>
In the anime, on the day of Boruto's birthday, work got in the way, making him unable to attend, instead only arriving home late at night with only a birthday present as an apology. Later, as more investigations to the workings of Kaguya continued, a third Ōtsutsuki clan ruin tied to her was found. Determined to find out all he could, Naruto prepared to investigate it personally. One the way out, Naruto was approached by his son, demanding that his father promised he would show up for Himawari's birthday that was coming up, which he did.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_exhausted.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120034155" class="image"><img alt="Naruto exhausted" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto exhausted.png" data-image-key="Naruto_exhausted.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_exhausted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120034155" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_exhausted.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120034155" class="image"><img alt="Naruto exhausted" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_exhausted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120034155" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto exhausted.png" data-image-key="Naruto_exhausted.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/25/Naruto_exhausted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120034155" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_exhausted.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto exhausted from overusing his clones.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Naruto remained busy with his Hokage duties and continued having a strained relationship with his son, Boruto. Konoha has grown into a large city under Naruto's leadership, although Naruto is overwhelmed with the responsibilities of being Hokage, leading him to create shadow clones to tend to his family and the villagers. When Boruto and his <a href="/wiki/Team_Konohamaru" class="mw-redirect" title="Team Konohamaru">team</a> report to Naruto after a mission, Naruto asked his son to address him as "the Seventh" instead of "Dad," and reminded him of the importance of teamwork, which annoyed his son, as he believed that he could handle anything on his own.
