Boruto warned his father to be home for Himawari's birthday party or else he will never forgive him. <a href="/wiki/Katasuke_T%C5%8Dno" title="Katasuke Tōno">Katasuke Tōno</a> then entered his office, requesting permission from Naruto to allow participants of the upcoming Chūnin Exams to use his new invention, the <a href="/wiki/Kote" class="mw-redirect" title="Kote">Kote</a>. However Naruto refused on the grounds that it did not show one's true abilities as a shinobi. Naruto was unable to make it to his daughter's birthday party and sent a shadow clone instead. However, the clone ended up disappearing and dropping the cake when Naruto became fatigued, which enraged Boruto and caused him to throw Naruto's old, tattered jacket out the window. Naruto felt guilty for letting his family down and Shikamaru told him to go home and rest. The jacket was found by Sasuke, who returned to Konoha to ask for help in deciphering a scroll he found in Kaguya's abandoned castle. They met in Naruto's office where Sasuke mentioned his meeting with Boruto and this leads to them making a bet on whether the nature of a shinobi has changed in regards to Boruto, to which Sasuke says it hasn't and Naruto says it has.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/92/Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120032906" class="image"><img alt="Naruto exposes Boruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto exposes Boruto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/92/Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120032906" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/92/Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120032906" class="image"><img alt="Naruto exposes Boruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/92/Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120032906" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto exposes Boruto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/92/Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230120032906" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_exposes_Boruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto exposes Boruto's cheating at the Chūnin Exams.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto wasn't surprised when Boruto won the first test but after being advised by Shikamaru to reach out to Boruto, Naruto congratulated him via email, much to Boruto's annoyance. While the scroll was being deciphered, Naruto sent a clone to meet up with Sasuke and asked him if it was true that he was training Boruto. Naruto said that perhaps Sasuke was right concerning the nature of shinobi remaining the same, to which Sasuke agrees. Naruto was nervous about the outcome of the second test but after learning Boruto passed, Naruto was overjoyed. Later, he met with Boruto in his bedroom and personally congratulated him and told him not to lose against Shikadai. Naruto offered a fist bump, but Boruto only smiled as he didn't want his father to discover the Kote he was wearing. For the third test, Naruto chose to sit with Hinata and Himawari rather than with the other Kage as they watched Boruto fight in the third round and finally against <a href="/wiki/Shikadai_Nara" title="Shikadai Nara">Shikadai Nara</a>. Near the end, Naruto suspected something was wrong after Boruto won. In the anime, he did not realise anything was amiss until Boruto's next match in the finals when he defeated <a href="/wiki/Shinki" title="Shinki">Shinki</a>. He asked Hinata to use her Byakugan and she noticed Boruto wearing a Kote (in the anime he realised the truth on his own). Realising that Boruto was using the exam-forbidden tool to advance his techniques, a disappointed Naruto confronted him in the arena, ordered that Boruto be disqualified from the exam and took Boruto's forehead protector from him, suspending his ninja status. He told Boruto they would talk about this at home, but Boruto lashed out at him that Naruto doesn't know how to give him a lecture when he's never home.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/5e/Naruto_Captured.png/revision/latest?cb=20180706070938" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Captured" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Captured.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Captured.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/5e/Naruto_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180706070938" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/5e/Naruto_Captured.png/revision/latest?cb=20180706070938" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Captured" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/5e/Naruto_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180706070938" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Captured.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Captured.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/5/5e/Naruto_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180706070938" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Captured.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto captured by Momoshiki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Suddenly, <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki" class="mw-redirect" title="Momoshiki">Momoshiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kinshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki">Kinshiki Ōtsutsuki</a> appear and began attacking the arena. Naruto is knocked out of the arena by Momoshiki but he rushes back to defend his son when he is in danger and is shortly joined by Sasuke and Sarada. Sasuke informed Naruto that the two enemies are the new threat written about in the scroll. Naruto realises he is their target and demands to know what they want. After Momoshiki reveals he wanted Kaguya's chakra, and eventually Kurama's from the Seventh Hokage, Naruto and Sasuke combine Kurama and Susanoo to shield themselves and their children from the enemies' attacks. Naruto also dispatches shadow clones to protect civilians that hadn't managed to flee from the arena. Determined to protect his son and friends, Naruto ultimately decides to allow himself to be captured in Momoshiki's jutsu and asks Sasuke to take care of Boruto for him. Just before Naruto disappears, he looks over his shoulder and offers his son one last smile. Naruto was teleported to another dimension and bound by Momoshiki and Kinshiki to a God Tree. Naruto resisted as Momoshiki extracted half of Kurama's chakra from inside Naruto. The two debated the merits of instant strength and earned strength, causing Naruto to realise his own lack of effort in trying to understand Boruto, which is what drove him to cheat with the Shinobi Gauntlet. During the ordeal, Sasuke, Boruto, and the other Kage arrived to rescue him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Kurama_Vs_Golem.png/revision/latest?cb=20240123231059" class="image"><img alt="Kurama Vs Golem" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama Vs Golem.png" data-image-key="Kurama_Vs_Golem.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Kurama_Vs_Golem.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240123231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Kurama_Vs_Golem.png/revision/latest?cb=20240123231059" class="image"><img alt="Kurama Vs Golem" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Kurama_Vs_Golem.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240123231059" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama Vs Golem.png" data-image-key="Kurama_Vs_Golem.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/d/d2/Kurama_Vs_Golem.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240123231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama_Vs_Golem.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke fighting Momoshiki's techniques.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto, surprised to see Boruto wearing his old jacket, told his son that it was like looking at one of his shadow clones. When he tried to apologise to Boruto for not being there for him, Boruto replied that it was alright and he just wants to hear more about Naruto's past. After the other Kage failed to defeat Kinshiki, and the latter was absorbed by Momoshiki, Naruto and Sasuke joined forces to fight him and initially gained the upper hand until Naruto was briefly imprisoned by boulders and Sasuke was severely burned by Momoshiki's <a href="/wiki/Lava_Release" title="Lava Release">Lava Release</a>. Naruto became enraged upon seeing Sasuke injured but was relieved to find he was all right and still able to fight after being healed by Kurama's chakra. By once again combining Kurama and Susanoo, they managed to defeat Momoshiki and cut his lava creature in half, but Katasuke rushed in and began firing ninjutsu attacks from his Kote at Momoshiki, which he absorbed and used to attack Naruto and the others. Naruto is restrained by black rods while Momoshiki prepares to eliminate the rest of the Kage. When Boruto used his <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Rasengan" title="Vanishing Rasengan">Vanishing Rasengan</a> against Momoshiki to free his father and the other Kage, Naruto was greatly surprised to find that his son was able to use the Rasengan. As they prepare their final assault, Naruto helps Boruto to create a <a href="/wiki/Parent_and_Child_Rasengan" title="Parent and Child Rasengan">Parent and Child Rasengan</a>, which Boruto himself unleashes upon Momoshiki and ultimately kills him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png/revision/latest?cb=20160103035031" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Boruto fist bump" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto and Boruto fist bump.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160103035031" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png/revision/latest?cb=20160103035031" class="image"><img alt="Naruto and Boruto fist bump" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160103035031" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto and Boruto fist bump.png" data-image-key="Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160103035031" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_and_Boruto_fist_bump.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Boruto reconcile.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the battle ends, Naruto sits with Sasuke and Naruto agrees Sasuke won their bet. Naruto proudly looked on at his son and stated that he would always be there to watch Boruto grow as his father. After returning home, Naruto posed for a photograph with Boruto, Sasuke, and the four other Kage. In the anime, Naruto hosted a shared birthday party for Boruto and Himawari as an apology for his actions during Himawari's actual birthday and brought home a cake for the family to eat. After Boruto punched Naruto, thinking it was a shadow clone, Naruto began scolding him, while Himawari asked for a piggy back ride. Hinata maintained order by threatening to throw the cake away. The next morning, as Boruto left to meet with his team and Naruto left to go to work, both wished each other to do their best and bumped fists with each other. While Boruto was giving a live interview on Konoha TV, Naruto watches it proudly from his desk.
</p>
<h3><span id="Ch.C5.8Dch.C5.8D_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Chōchō_Arc">Chōchō Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D65&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%8Dch%C5%8D_Arc" title="Chōchō Arc">Chōchō Arc</a></span>
In the anime, when the two <a href="/wiki/Ashina" title="Ashina">lead</a> <a href="/wiki/Tomaru" title="Tomaru">actors</a> of a popular TV drama received a death threat, Naruto assigned Team 7 and Team 10 to protect them.
</p>
<h3><span id="Mitsuki.27s_Disappearance_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Mitsuki's_Disappearance_Arc">Mitsuki's Disappearance Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D66&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Mitsuki%27s_Disappearance_Arc" title="Mitsuki&#39;s Disappearance Arc">Mitsuki's Disappearance Arc</a></span>
In the anime, when <a href="/wiki/Sa%C5%8D" title="Saō">two</a> <a href="/wiki/U%C5%8D" title="Uō">guards</a> were attacked by <a href="/wiki/Kokuy%C5%8D" title="Kokuyō">unknown</a> <a href="/wiki/Sekiei" title="Sekiei">assailants</a>, the village was put on lockdown. Naruto and his advisers then oversaw Ino probe Uō's mind for answers, learning that <a href="/wiki/Mitsuki" title="Mitsuki">Mitsuki</a> had left willingly with the attackers. When Naruto revealed to the others Mitsuki was in fact Orochimaru's son, much outrage followed, prompting Naruto to give his rational on why he accepted Mitsuki into Konoha. Later, Naruto was informed that Boruto and Sarada left the village to find Mitsuki, leading to him dispatching <a href="/wiki/Team_10_(Moegi)" title="Team 10 (Moegi)">Team 10</a> to retrieve the pair. When Naruto learned that the attackers were on route to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Earth" title="Land of Earth">Land of Earth</a>, he contacted <a href="/wiki/Kurotsuchi" title="Kurotsuchi">Kurotsuchi</a>, who promised to investigate the matter herself and return the Konoha genin pursing Mitsuki. While discussing Mitsuki's apparent betrayal, Konohamaru insisted he be the one to bring his student back, which Naruto reluctantly agreed to. Naruto later attempted to contact Kurotsuchi, but was told she wasn't available, leading to him becoming suspicious something was happening in <a href="/wiki/Iwagakure" title="Iwagakure">Iwagakure</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ce/%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20190204110248" class="image"><img alt="Ōnoki&#39;s Funeral" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ōnoki&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ce/%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190204110248" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ce/%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20190204110248" class="image"><img alt="Ōnoki&#39;s Funeral" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ce/%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190204110248" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ōnoki&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ce/%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190204110248" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:%C5%8Cnoki%27s_Funeral.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto attending Ōnoki's funeral.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Naruto's fears were proven correct when Shikadai contacted his father via phone, revealing that Iwagakure was taken over as part of a plan by Ōnoki. Knowing that they couldn't act hastily, Naruto talks with the other officials and decided that he would join Shikamaru in meeting with the other daimyō to get their support on engaging this personal matter. After getting approval, Naruto and an escort moved out, and allowed his son's peers to come with him. Upon arriving at the batted village, Naruto applauded Konohamaru's work during the Iwa's internal struggle. Naruto stayed in the village and attended Ōnoki's funeral, prompting him to say the <a href="/wiki/Tsuchikage" title="Tsuchikage">Tsuchikage</a> left behind a grand legacy and lesson about perseverance. After returning to the village, while personally applauding Boruto and Sarada for loyally supporting Mitsuki, whose own efforts were revealed to have saved Iwa, he still was reluctantly forced to strip the Team 7 genin of their shinobi status as punishment for deserting the village. Later, Kurotsuchi's gratitude and recommendation convinced Naruto to reinstate them.
</p>
<h3><span id="Konohamaru.27s_Love_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Konohamaru's_Love_Arc">Konohamaru's Love Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D67&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Konohamaru%27s_Love_Arc" title="Konohamaru&#39;s Love Arc">Konohamaru's Love Arc</a></span>
In the anime, due to Konohamaru spying on <a href="/wiki/Asaki" title="Asaki">Asaki</a>, a complaint was filed against him, prompting Naruto to place him under house arrest.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="One-Tail_Escort_Arc">One-Tail Escort Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D68&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/One-Tail_Escort_Arc" title="One-Tail Escort Arc">One-Tail Escort Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c5/Biju_Conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20200604154217" class="image"><img alt="Biju Conference" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Biju Conference.png" data-image-key="Biju_Conference.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c5/Biju_Conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200604154217" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c5/Biju_Conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20200604154217" class="image"><img alt="Biju Conference" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c5/Biju_Conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200604154217" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Biju Conference.png" data-image-key="Biju_Conference.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c5/Biju_Conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200604154217" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Biju_Conference.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto meets with the tailed beasts to discuss Urashiki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, after Sai delivered a sealed <a href="/wiki/Shukaku" title="Shukaku">Shukaku</a> in a tea kettle to Naruto as a result of Gaara being unable to protect it in the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Wind" title="Land of Wind">Land of Wind</a> from <a href="/wiki/Urashiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Urashiki Ōtsutsuki">Urashiki Ōtsutsuki</a>, Shukaku explained it only made it to Konoha due to Boruto acting as a decoy against their pursuer. Informing Shikamaru he was going to the scene, Sasuke approached the pair and told him that wasn't necessary, as Sasuke had earlier protected Boruto and forced Urashiki to retreat. Three days later, Naruto and Gaara discussed the incident in his office. Afterwards, Naruto had a Shadow Clone see the Kazekage off at the Thunder Rail station. Some time later, Naruto brought Shukaku to his house until an official safe house was decided on. Later that evening, Naruto had a telepathic meeting with some of the other tailed beasts to discuss how to handle being targeted. As a result of guarding Shukaku, Naruto got to spend time with his family, before escorting Shukaku to his safe house.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Time_Slip_Arc">Time Slip Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D69&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Time_Slip_Arc" title="Time Slip Arc">Time Slip Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/9c/Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021025200" class="image"><img alt="Young Naruto and Boruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Young Naruto and Boruto.png" data-image-key="Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/9c/Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221021025200" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/9c/Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021025200" class="image"><img alt="Young Naruto and Boruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/9c/Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221021025200" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Young Naruto and Boruto.png" data-image-key="Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/9c/Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221021025200" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Young_Naruto_and_Boruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A young Naruto and Boruto discussing Boruto's father.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, Naruto was notified that Urashiki was on the move again, being even more indiscriminate in his stealing of chakra. While pleased that all of the Five Great Shinobi Nations were on alert and willing to share all intel on Urashiki, Shikamaru voiced his concern about Mirai's sudden disappearance and also wondered what their enemy true goal was for gathering chakra. Later, Naruto decided to have the genin test new surveillance equipment designed to follow their location. During the field test, Urashiki was spotted in the area. This prompted most of the Konoha-nin in the village to engage, while Shikamaru stayed in the Hokage Office to help protect Naruto. Urashiki managed to get hold of a device that allowed him to travel into the past, prompting Sasuke and Boruto being sent back alongside him to the time period shortly after Sasuke's defection. A teenage Naruto and Jiraiya encountered the pair, who were disguising their identities and their occupations as travelling performers. As they were foreigners, Tsunade has Naruto and Jiraiya look over them. Spending time with Boruto, Naruto allowed him to sleep at his apartment, where Boruto vaguely talked about his father, speaking about both his feats and his flaws, where Naruto was intrigued to hear about, noting that Boruto enjoyed talking about his family, and inquired Boruto if he hated his father, to which Boruto denied.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4f/Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20200127235047" class="image"><img alt="Boruto training with Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Boruto training with Naruto.png" data-image-key="Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4f/Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200127235047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4f/Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20200127235047" class="image"><img alt="Boruto training with Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4f/Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200127235047" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Boruto training with Naruto.png" data-image-key="Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4f/Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200127235047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Boruto_training_with_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto training with Boruto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The day after cleaning up a bathhouse together, Urashiki targeted Naruto. Failing at extracting Kurama's chakra, Urashiki instead captured him and trapped Boruto, Sasuke and Jiraiya in a rock prison before retreating. Using a cave for a hideout, Urashiki forced Naruto's seal to emerge and used his chakra in an attempt to forcibly extract Kurama' chakra from within Naruto. Urashiki's actions caused Kurama's chakra to leak out, forcing Naruto to undergo his <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki_Forms" title="Jinchūriki Forms">Version 1</a> transformation. Arriving to rescue Naruto, Boruto attempted to reason with his father, but Naruto had since completely lost his common sense and attacked Boruto. Jiraiya managed to subdue the Nine-Tails' chakra with a seal, and Sasuke forced Urashiki to retreat. Afterwards, Jiraiya offered to train Naruto and Boruto to prepare them for Urashiki. The following day, Naruto began working with Boruto to synchronise their chakra to create a new cooperation ninjutsu under Jiraiya's guidance. After Boruto left to clear his head, Sasuke approached Naruto with food from Jiraiya, and told Naruto about how "a friend" struggled for years to help him after he lost his way, but never gave up until finally succeeding, which renewed Naruto's conviction.
</p><p>Continuing his training the next day, the pair were approached by Sakura, who had found Sasuke's note from the future, and questioned why it Sasuke's name on it before shortly leaving with an answer. Naruto and Boruto resumed their training, which ultimately left them exhausted. They were then approached again by Urashiki, who subdued the pair. Jiraiya and Sasuke joined the fight. Deciding the foe's newest technique was too dangerous, Sasuke tackled himself and Urashiki over the ledge and into a river to let his allies escape. While tending to Jiraiya's wounds, the group tried to figure out how to deal with Urashiki. Boruto realised that in the fight, the blood splattered on Urashiki was drying much faster than Boruto's. After engaging the foe again to test a theory, they concluded that Urashiki's technique lets him <a href="/wiki/Temporal_Rewind" title="Temporal Rewind">warp into the past</a> by several seconds, giving him a pseudo-clairvoyance from his experiences. Urashiki attacked the Konoha-nin again, where Jiraiya contained everyone in his <a href="/wiki/Summoning:_Toad_Mouth_Bind" title="Summoning: Toad Mouth Bind">Summoning: Toad Mouth Bind</a>. During which, Naruto unleashed a continued barrage of clones on Urashiki. While he easily countered the assault with his technique, Urashiki inadvertently poisoned himself from the acidic vapours of the great toad's belly far sooner than the Konoha-nin due to his repeated time-warp. Once Jiraiya released the summoning, Naruto and Boruto then proceeded to knockout Urashiki with a <a href="/wiki/Rasengan" title="Rasengan">Rasengan</a> assault.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ae/The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20191209060007" class="image"><img alt="The Last Battle, Urashiki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Last Battle, Urashiki.png" data-image-key="The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ae/The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191209060007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ae/The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20191209060007" class="image"><img alt="The Last Battle, Urashiki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ae/The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191209060007" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Last Battle, Urashiki.png" data-image-key="The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/ae/The_Last_Battle%2C_Urashiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191209060007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Last_Battle,_Urashiki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Boruto facing Urashiki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Enraged, Urashiki awoke and consumed all his accumulated chakra and his eyes, leading to him undergoing a transformation that strengthened him. Jiraiya and the two genin were quickly overwhelmed by Urashiki's continued assaults, even with the aid of the returning Sasuke. Urashiki deliberately held back on Naruto, hoping to anger him enough into unleashing the Nine-Tails' chakra. His efforts ultimately succeeded when Jiraiya took a hit that was intended for Naruto, triggering his transformation. Boruto, however, managed to reach Naruto and together were able to perfect their <a href="/wiki/Parent_and_Child_Rasengan" title="Parent and Child Rasengan">new collaboration technique</a>. With the combined effort of Jiraiya and Sasuke, the two kids were able to plough through Urashiki's final attack and obliterate him. After the battle, both Naruto and Boruto lose consciousness due to their exhaustion. Days after Naruto and Boruto recovered at the Konoha hospital, he was upset to hear that Boruto and Sasuke would be leaving now that their mission was completed. Before they left, Naruto gave Boruto a gift. Sasuke used his Sharingan to <a href="/wiki/Genjutsu:_Sharingan" title="Genjutsu: Sharingan">erase</a> everyone's memories of the events to preserve the timeline. On seeing the Sharingan, Naruto had what appeared to be a brief moment of recognising Sasuke before losing consciousness.
</p><p>Upon the pair returning, Naruto was approached by Sasuke who explained the recent situation he and Boruto had. Naruto was amazed at such a tale. Later, while visiting Jiraiya's grave to pay his respect, he was approached by Boruto, who decided to share with Naruto the gift of special ramen given by his past self. Sometime later, Sumire was officially transferred to the <a href="/wiki/Scientific_Ninja_Weapons_Team" title="Scientific Ninja Weapons Team">Scientific Ninja Weapons Team</a>. Naruto reached out to the Land of Iron and requested an exchange student to take Sumire's spot on <a href="/wiki/Team_15" title="Team 15">Team 15</a>. Shikamaru was concerned about his experimental move of mixing shinobi with samurai, but Naruto insisted it would help close the gap between the two. Later, Naruto attended his father-in-law's birthday, impressed by Boruto getting past his aversion mushy feelings to suggest a regular family photo.
</p>
<h3><span id="Sasuke_Shinden:_The_Teacher.27s_Star_Pupil"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sasuke_Shinden:_The_Teacher's_Star_Pupil">Sasuke Shinden: The Teacher's Star Pupil</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D70&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Shinden:_The_Teacher%27s_Star_Pupil" title="Sasuke Shinden: The Teacher&#39;s Star Pupil">Sasuke Shinden: The Teacher's Star Pupil</a></span>
Naruto appears in this novel.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mujina_Bandits_Arc">Mujina Bandits Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D71&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Mujina_Bandits_Arc" title="Mujina Bandits Arc">Mujina Bandits Arc</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shikamaru_Shinden" class="mw-redirect" title="Shikamaru Shinden">Shikamaru Shinden</a></span>
In the anime, Naruto set up a mission for <a href="/wiki/Team_7_(Konohamaru)" title="Team 7 (Konohamaru)">Team 7</a> to infiltrate <a href="/wiki/H%C5%8Dzuki_Castle" title="Hōzuki Castle">Hōzuki Castle</a> to verify the information about the <a href="/wiki/Mujina_Bandits" title="Mujina Bandits">Mujina Bandits</a> offered by <a href="/wiki/Kokuri" title="Kokuri">Kokuri</a> in exchange for protection. After losing contact from <a href="/wiki/Muj%C5%8D" title="Mujō">Mujō</a>, the prison warder who was working with Konohagakure, Naruto sent Sai and a team to investigate. Ultimately, the succeeded in returning "<a href="/wiki/Shojoji" title="Shojoji">Kokuri</a>" to the village to question him about the Mujina Bandits before letting the man go free.
</p><p>At the Hokage building, Naruto hosted a Kage Summit, during which the Kage bickered about topics concerning Konoha, leading to <a href="/wiki/Kurotsuchi" title="Kurotsuchi">Kurotsuchi</a> demanding Konoha to disclose all of its confidential information as the village's proof to peace by the next summit, and said <a href="/wiki/Iwagakure" title="Iwagakure">Iwagakure</a> would leave the Five Great Shinobi Country alliance if they didn't. Afterwards the summit ended. Naruto was told then by Shikamaru that the reason why Kurotsuchi was acting that way was because she was being pressured by the Earth Daimyō to invade the Land of Flowers for the corps they had to offer and expressed sadness that Kurotsuchi didn't tell them as he believed that the Shinobi Union would have definitely aided her when it came to food scarcity and other issues and the potential of another war, remembering the casualties of the last war and not wanting to use and introduce the next generation to the horrors of war. Naruto found hope, however, when Shikamaru said they could negotiate with her so the invasion won't happen.<sup id="cite_ref-SS_65-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SS-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unfortunately, in the next Kage Summit, Naruto's revelation of Kurotsuchi's true intentions only cause <a href="/wiki/Darui" title="Darui">Darui</a> to angrily threaten to kill Kurotsuchi and to add things worse, Naruto and Sasuke's strength were used as a boon for Kurotsuchi's cause, as they had the power to take over the continent and the imbalance in strength between Konoha and the other villages were thus immense. Despite Naruto's attempts to ensure Konoha would not try to take over the world, Shikamaru responded by paralysing and threatening to crush Kurotsuchi's neck, much to Naruto's horror and fury. Quickly, Naruto used his chakra to break out of Shikamaru's shadow and angrily put Shikamaru in place before attempting to plea for peace but he could not sway Kurotsuchi or Darui, who made it clear they would go to war if the invasion were to occur. Furious over the outcome, Naruto angrily confronted Shikamaru when they walked home but was rebuffed by his friend, who told him to think with his head and start responding harshly enough.<sup id="cite_ref-SS_65-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SS-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Several months after the Hōzuki Castle mission, Naruto discussed Katasuke being under mind control with Sai and Ibiki, and had them continue their investigation while Shikamaru handled Katasuki. Afterwards, <a href="/wiki/Mirai_Sarutobi" title="Mirai Sarutobi">Mirai Sarutobi</a> informed Naruto that Team Konohamaru successfully captured the Mujina Bandits, much to his joy. As <a href="/wiki/Shojoji" title="Shojoji">Shojoji</a> was discussed, Naruto told everyone that they had to hurry up and handle the <a href="/wiki/Missing-nin" title="Missing-nin">missing-nin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> Shikamaru then informed Naruto of his upcoming meeting with the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Daimy%C5%8D" class="mw-redirect" title="Fire Daimyō">Fire Daimyō</a> <a href="/wiki/Ikky%C5%AB_Madoka" title="Ikkyū Madoka">Ikkyū Madoka</a>, which Naruto had forgotten was later during the day. During which, he discussed financial matter with Ikkyū.<sup id="cite_ref-SS_65-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SS-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kara_Actuation_Arc">Kara Actuation Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D72&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kara_Actuation_Arc" title="Kara Actuation Arc">Kara Actuation Arc</a></span>
Later in the anime, Team 25 and Sasuke were sent to investigate the information extracted from the captured Shojoji about Kara's existence in Amegakure. Upon their return, they learned that Kara had long ago abandoned their facility in Amegakure and were performing biological experiments. They also learned that there were in fact civilians who sympathised with Kara and its goals. Naruto was concerned to learn that Amegakure was in shambles as it had yet to make any recovery since the Fourth Shinobi World War. He was determined to help the village.
</p><p>Naruto learned that <a href="/wiki/Victor" title="Victor">Victor</a>, the president of the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Valleys" title="Land of Valleys">Land of Valleys</a>' premiere medical and research company, was a member of <a href="/wiki/Kara" title="Kara">Kara</a> who somehow obtained a sample of the First Hokage's cells. Naruto was greatly concerned that <a href="/wiki/Team_7_(Konohamaru)" title="Team 7 (Konohamaru)">Team 7</a> was defeated by two Inners. Upon seeing Boruto in treatment, he was certain that Boruto would be fine. Afterwards, Naruto discussed with his advisers on the next move. Shikamaru offered to use his connections in the Land of Valleys to get permission to investigate Victor's company. Three days later, it was approved for Naruto to send <a href="/wiki/Mugino" title="Mugino">Mugino</a> and Konohamaru to stealthily investigate. Later, Naruto sent <a href="/wiki/Team_10_(Moegi)" title="Team 10 (Moegi)">Team 10</a> on a joint mission with <a href="/wiki/Team_Shinki" title="Team Shinki">Team Shinki</a> to retrieve Urashiki's puppet. He later listened to Shikadai's report on the mission which greatly concerned and disturbed him.
</p><p>After Boruto recovered from his new training, Naruto gave his son permission to return to the Land of Valleys to return the wedding ring of their recent client's husband to her. Following the defeat of Victor and his amoral experiments, Naruto received a report on the events. Upon Konohamaru and Mugino's return, Konoha leadership discussed how to handle Kara, having learned influential figures like Victor were associated with the organisation and finding evidence in their investigation that Kara had spies all around. While many considered closing off the gates to Konohagakure to stop the flow of information, Naruto was torn on this, valuing the new peace between the village and the rest of the world. After talking various officials in the village, and witnessing Boruto and his friends work on an experiment to improve wireless communications, Naruto decided to not close the gates as it would deter cooperation with the outside world, instead deciding to reinforce security.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ao_Arc">Ao Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D73&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Ao_Arc" title="Ao Arc">Ao Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/19/Boruto_vs._Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20210126181720" class="image"><img alt="Boruto vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Boruto vs. Naruto.png" data-image-key="Boruto_vs._Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/19/Boruto_vs._Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210126181720" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/19/Boruto_vs._Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20210126181720" class="image"><img alt="Boruto vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/19/Boruto_vs._Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210126181720" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Boruto vs. Naruto.png" data-image-key="Boruto_vs._Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/19/Boruto_vs._Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210126181720" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Boruto_vs._Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto facing Boruto.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, Naruto attended the memorial service for the fallen people of the Fourth Shinobi World War. Later, Naruto joins his son in a sparring match at the <a href="/wiki/Training_Hall" title="Training Hall">Training Hall</a>, to test out Katasuke's new invention that was fitted on his arm. During the match, Naruto <a href="/wiki/Earth_Release:_Earth-Style_Wall" title="Earth Release: Earth-Style Wall">defends</a> himself from Boruto, and uses the invention to absorb his <a href="/wiki/Water_Release:_Surging_Sea" title="Water Release: Surging Sea">son</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lightning_Release:_Thunderclap_Arrow" title="Lightning Release: Thunderclap Arrow">techniques</a>, before defeating him with a single kick. Afterwards at the Hokage's office, Naruto informs Boruto of the technology he used against him, which angered Boruto. Before Naruto could explain himself, Sasuke arrives and interrupts their conversation, calming Boruto down by pointing out the need for them with the coming danger of enemies like the <a href="/wiki/%C5%8Ctsutsuki_Clan" title="Ōtsutsuki Clan">Ōtsutsuki Clan</a>.
</p><p>Naruto also admitted to knowing about Boruto's mark on his right palm, which was another reason Naruto approved the development of this advanced weaponry. While Boruto still insisted they should rely solely on ninjutsu like in the Chūnin Exams, Naruto noted that the Chūnin Exams were to test one's growth as a ninja, where as they are now in a battle for survival. Katasuke then arrived to retrieve his prototype, to which Naruto assigned Team Konohamaru a C-rank mission to escort the lead scientist back to the lab in Ryūben City. While Boruto stormed off in a huff, Naruto asked his genin team-mates to watch over him should anything happen with his mark.
</p><p>As Konohamaru failed to report from his mission, Naruto contacted Boruto's team at the <a href="/wiki/Scientific_Ninja_Weapons_Team" title="Scientific Ninja Weapons Team">Scientific Ninja Weapons Team</a>'s lab, who were nearest to Konohamaru's last reported location. He instructed them to search the area but be careful and not recklessly engage any foes. While Shikamaru reminded him that Team Konohamaru were all very capable for their age, Naruto insisted that he was more concerned about the possibility of them running into the organisation <a href="/wiki/Kara" title="Kara">Kara</a> as Konohamaru's mission was to investigate a mysterious airship.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kawaki_Arc">Kawaki Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D74&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kawaki_Arc" title="Kawaki Arc">Kawaki Arc</a></span>
When Team 7 returned with news of Mugino's demise at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Ao" title="Ao">Ao</a>, who was in leagues with Kara, they also revealed a boy with ties to Kara named <a href="/wiki/Kawaki" title="Kawaki">Kawaki</a>. In the anime, he was detained at the <a href="/wiki/Advanced_Technology_Research_Institute" title="Advanced Technology Research Institute">Advanced Technology Research Institute</a> in Ryūtan City, prompting Naruto and Sai to go immediately and meet the boy. On the train ride, Sai noted that it was risky to take such a mysterious boy back to the village. Naruto understood Sai's fear, knowing that Kara's desire of the boy could lead to the village becoming a battlefield again. Upon arriving in the station, they learned that Kawaki escaped and was on a rampage. Before Naruto and Sai could act, they met with Boruto and Sumire, the latter insisted to not hurt Kawaki. She noted that Kawaki's rampage stemmed from emotional scars due to his troubled past. Taking Sumire's words to heart, Naruto stopped Kawaki's passively, subduing him until he tired himself out and collapsed.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210418141702" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Comforts Kawaki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Comforts Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210418141702" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210418141702" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Comforts Kawaki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210418141702" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Comforts Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/ca/Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210418141702" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Comforts_Kawaki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto comforts Kawaki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto decided he was most suitable to monitor Kawaki, and held a Kage Summit to discuss the situation. Following the unanimous agreement from other Kage with Naruto, he took the boy to his house, during which he foiled Kawaki's attempts at fleeing. There, Kawaki attempting to escape, but Naruto intimidated him into submission. His escape attempt resulted in Himawari's vase being destroyed. Naruto intervened when Boruto and Kawaki began fighting, and later overheard Kawaki speaking of his hardship as a result of his Kāma. Afterwards, Naruto took Kawaki to <a href="/wiki/Yamanaka_Flowers" title="Yamanaka Flowers">Yamanaka Flowers</a> to pick a new vase, where he hugged Kawaki after he had a panic attack. Sometime later, Naruto and Boruto sparred; he defeated his son, even while Boruto used his Kāma. Naruto offered for Kawaki to try sparring with Boruto next time, but Kawaki declined as he couldn't use chakra, prompting Naruto to insist that all can learn to do so and that having strong rivals will help one in accomplishing great things.
</p><p>Later, Boruto decided to take Kawaki's offer of learning what he knows about their Kāma. Deciding to do so through sparring, the two children quickly activated their respective marks. While Boruto kept up in hand-to-hand combat, Kawaki's usage of his modified body put Boruto on the defensive. Kawaki then launched a blast at Naruto with the intent of him absorbing it like previously, only for Boruto to instead damage his hand. Naruto called off the match and told the two to perform the Seal of Reconciliation. The event made their marks react and caused Boruto's hand to instantly heal. Before pushing the subject, Naruto was alerted of an intruder. Naruto told his son to take Himawari away while he stayed with Kawaki, certain that the intruder was after Kawaki. His assumption proved correct as they were quickly met by <a href="/wiki/Delta" title="Delta">Delta</a>. She demanded Naruto hand over Kawaki to her, and Kawaki confirmed her identity as an Inner from Kara. Naruto instructed Boruto to protect Himawari and Kawaki to protect himself.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Delta_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517080202" class="image"><img alt="Delta Vs Naruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Delta Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Delta_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Delta_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210517080202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Delta_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20210517080202" class="image"><img alt="Delta Vs Naruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Delta_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210517080202" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Delta Vs Naruto.png" data-image-key="Delta_Vs_Naruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/0/05/Delta_Vs_Naruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210517080202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Delta_Vs_Naruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto fighting Delta.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Fighting her, Naruto initially outperformed her with taijutsu, but she began making use of her shinobi-ware to launch sneak attacks and absorb his Rasengan. Naruto entered his Six Paths Sage Mode, but Delta was eventually able to stab him and pin him down. He tried to discern her motives for wanting Kawaki, but she saw through his deception, and noticed he was already healing, considering Naruto to be a monster as well. While Naruto was continually forced to hold back in fear of the spectators' safety, he continued to gradually wear down his foe, leading to Delta using her Destruction Beam against Naruto to combat his regenerative ability. Eventually, Delta targets Himawari, leading to Naruto blocking the attack with his body, but is uninjured as Kawaki sacrificed his right arm to block the attack. Enraged at her tactics, Naruto resumed the fight and quickly overwhelmed her. Naruto, having seen her return his Rasengan that she absorbed, deduces that there was a limit to how much chakra her eyes can absorb since the chakra or attack had to be stored somewhere in her body rather than dissipating and vanishing, prompting him to overpower and defeat Delta with his <a href="/wiki/Super-Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Super-Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan">Super-Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan</a>. Defeated, Delta's body self-destructed, forcing Naruto to flee the vicinity with the children.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20211007092723" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Training Kawaki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Training Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007092723" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20211007092723" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Training Kawaki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007092723" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Training Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007092723" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Training_Kawaki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto training Kawaki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, when bringing Kawaki to Katasuke to repair Kawaki's arm, the scientist informed him that the technology in Kawaki's body was too advanced for him to handle. Finding an alternate solution, Naruto gave Kawaki one of his prosthetic arms and channelled some of his chakra into Kawaki to make it work. Shocked at how sincere Naruto was at being nice, Kawaki asked to learn ninjutsu, which Naruto agreed to and began training him. Quite a while after Delta's defeat, while Naruto and Kawaki were at his house, he notices Kawaki in distress, resulting in his Kāma creating a portal which Jigen emerged from. Wanting to take his son back, Naruto attempted to attack him but was repelled away and impaled by chakra draining rods. Activating his chakra mode, Naruto kicks Jigen away from Kawaki. Jigen then proceeded to activate his Kāma. Fearing for the Hokage's safety, with Jigen's power entirely above Delta's and capable of either killing or severely injuring Naruto, Kawaki stepped in and submitted, agreeing to back willingly with Jigen if he spared Naruto. While Jigen agreed to the terms, Naruto refused to comply. Jigen responded by teleporting himself and Naruto to another dimension.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20210624075356" class="image"><img alt="Jigen vs Shinobi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jigen vs Shinobi.png" data-image-key="Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210624075356" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20210624075356" class="image"><img alt="Jigen vs Shinobi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210624075356" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jigen vs Shinobi.png" data-image-key="Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c2/Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210624075356" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jigen_vs_Shinobi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and Sasuke facing Jigen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Jigen attempted to strand Naruto there, he was attacked and stopped by Sasuke. Being away from Konoha and free to fight with all their power, the pair engaged in battle with Jigen, leading to Sasuke deducing their opponent's fighting style involved shrinking himself and his rods. Pressuring Jigen, the Kara member taped into his Kāma and grew a horn. Upon seeing Jigen's development, Sasuke revealed how he resembled an <a href="/wiki/Isshiki_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Isshiki Ōtsutsuki">unknown</a> Ōtsutsuki member, and that Jigen had ties with a juvenile Ten-Tails. As Sasuke also revealed that Jigen's goal was to drain the entire planet of all its chakra, the two shinobi decided to fight with their full power. Despite their strong avatar forms and team-work, Jigen ploughed through their defences. As he swiftly wore down and pummelled his foes, he restrained the pair with rods and decided to keep Naruto alive because of Kurama in him while killing Sasuke due to his Rinnegan's Space-Time Ninjutsu. Accepting the truth, Naruto had his clones hold off Jigen while he convinced Sasuke to escape despite his friend's protests. Jigen revealed that he was after Boruto Uzumaki for his Kāma and sealed Naruto in a giant pot which he shrunk, leaving Naruto trapped within the foreign dimension. Afterwards, <a href="/wiki/Boro" title="Boro">Boro</a> stood guard over the pot, during which Boruto and Kawaki used their Kama to <a href="/wiki/K%C4%81ma_Rift" title="Kāma Rift">transport</a> Naruto's unconscious body out before killing the Kara member.
</p><p>Returning to Konoha, they were all taken to the hospital for treatment. As Naruto made a quick recovery, he was impressed to hear of the genin's work, and joked that rebellious genin seemed to still be a thing. In the anime, they discussed the recent events. Kawaki informed them that each member of Kara was modified with Shinobi-Ware, granting them abilities besides ninjutsu. After everyone else left, Shikamaru discussed with Naruto on how best to deal with Kawaki, as his Kāma acted as a direct path to Konoha at any time for Kara. Upon learning of Boro's cult, Naruto assigned Sai and Konohamaru to investigate, hoping to discover new information on the new whereabouts of Kara's Ten-Tails. They returned and reported Boro's scheme for getting new cultists and using them as subjects for Kara's Vessel experiments, as well as that despite her defeat to Naruto, Delta was somehow still active, having destroyed the cult's base.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/23/Amado%27s_Interrogation.png/revision/latest?cb=20211007093031" class="image"><img alt="Amado&#39;s Interrogation" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Amado&#39;s Interrogation.png" data-image-key="Amado%27s_Interrogation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/23/Amado%27s_Interrogation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007093031" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/23/Amado%27s_Interrogation.png/revision/latest?cb=20211007093031" class="image"><img alt="Amado&#39;s Interrogation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/23/Amado%27s_Interrogation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007093031" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Amado&#39;s Interrogation.png" data-image-key="Amado%27s_Interrogation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/2/23/Amado%27s_Interrogation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211007093031" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Amado%27s_Interrogation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto interrogates Amado.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Naruto was informed by Ino of Shikadai being taken hostage by <a href="/wiki/Amado" class="mw-redirect" title="Amado">Amado</a>. Though he wished to speak to Shikamaru, he was glad to learn of Naruto's rescue, and revealed he wished to defect to Konoha, offering intel on Kara, Jigen, their Ten-Tails, and the Ōtsutsuki. After Naruto gave his word as Hokage to not go back on the deal provided his intel was good, Amado began explaining all he knew. He revealed that how the Ōtsutsuki have since before recorded history been travelling from planet to planet, harvesting its chakra for the sake of evolving itself while destroying the planet in the process, using the Ten-Tails for the process. He revealed that Jigen himself was turned into an Ōtsutsuki from being branded by his Kāma of Isshiki. Amado also revealed to have sabotaged the blimp to free Kawaki and likewise ensure that Sasuke would get the intel of Isshiki. Amado's glasses began beeping. His glasses were taken off, revealing a holographic projection of Jigen talking with his accomplice <a href="/wiki/Koji_Kashin" title="Koji Kashin">Koji Kashin</a> intended to kill Jigen. As Naruto was intrigued by Koji's techniques and battle tactics, Amado insisted that Naruto accept his request to officially join Konohagakure with full amnesty and protection in order to hear more of his secrets, which Naruto agreed. Amado carried on his explanation, sharing what he knew of Jigen, the Ōtsutsuki, and Kāma. He stressed how a full rebirth of the Ōtsutsuki must be avoided, and claimed he'd teach them how to kill an Ōtsutsuki. When Jigen's death triggered Isshiki's resurrection in his body, Amado explained this also erased Kawaki's Kāma to avoid duplicates, leading Shikamaru to realise that without any remaining Kāma, Isshiki was vulnerable to a permanent death.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210912131716" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Meets Isshiki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Meets Isshiki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210912131716" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210912131716" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Meets Isshiki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210912131716" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Meets Isshiki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/a/a1/Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210912131716" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Meets_Isshiki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto halts Isshiki's search.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Amado was officially made a citizen of Konohagakure, made aware of his rights and limitations, he warned them of Isshiki's immediate focus on rebranding Kawaki. He advised Naruto against taking the fight to Isshiki, and stressed that had to protect Kawaki against being rebranded. Naruto took his advice and ordered a civilian evacuation, as Isshiki would seek Kawaki in Konoha. Naruto was against Boruto staying to fight him, but where interrupted by an alert of Isshiki's arrival. Naruto ordered Boruto to join the evacuation as he went to confront Isshiki. Isshiki was surprised to see Naruto had escaped, but demanded for Kawaki. When Naruto refused, Isshiki began shrinking various targets in the village to destroy it. Naruto activated his <a href="/wiki/Six_Paths_Sage_Mode" title="Six Paths Sage Mode">Six Paths Sage Mode</a>, but Isshiki easily overpowered him. Sasuke soon joined the fight, levelling the battlefield. He then launched his sword at Isshiki. As Isshiki attempted to shrink it, it was revealed to Boruto <a href="/wiki/Transformation_Technique" title="Transformation Technique">transformed</a>. As Naruto was horrified by his son's arrival, Boruto activated his <a href="/wiki/K%C4%81ma" title="Kāma">Kāma</a>, <a href="/wiki/K%C4%81ma_Rift" title="Kāma Rift">teleporting</a> himself and Isshiki to another dimension. Naruto and Sasuke followed through the latter's Rinnegan. As the Konoha-nin faced down Isshiki, he decided the best way to get Kawaki was to present Sasuke and Naruto's corpses to the village. The fight quickly resumed, with Naruto and Sasuke's team-work managing to push Isshiki on the defence as he began shrinking all their attacks. Quickly however, Isshiki demonstrated a new technique, manifesting and manipulating <a href="/wiki/Disruption_Cube" title="Disruption Cube">massive black cubes</a> that separated the duo.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/62/Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20211001062832" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Overwhelming Isshiki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Overwhelming Isshiki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/62/Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211001062832" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/62/Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20211001062832" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Overwhelming Isshiki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/62/Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211001062832" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Overwhelming Isshiki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/6/62/Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211001062832" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Overwhelming_Isshiki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto overwhelming Isshiki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Realising he was running out of options, Kurama asked Naruto if he was really willing to sacrifice himself to stop Isshiki. Naruto confirmed it, and Kurama offered a last-ditch strategy which would have a high risk of death from using it. Accepting his duties as Hokage, Naruto faced Isshiki and took on a new form of <a href="/wiki/Baryon_Mode" title="Baryon Mode">Baryon Mode</a>. Kurama explained to Naruto that the form is like nuclear fusion, consuming all their respective energy and that he must be careful not to make any unnecessary movements or thoughts. The new form baffled everyone with its sheer power. Naruto quickly began overwhelming Isshiki, constantly countering and dodging the foes various assaults. Soon after, the strain of Baryon Mode began catching up as Naruto began to tire. Kurama noted this form gradually drains away all life-forces, including Naruto's. However, it would also drain Isshiki's with each contact, meaning they just had to keep pressuring Isshiki until his already diminished lifespan ran out. As Isshiki began getting desperate, he took advantage of Naruto's chakra connection to Kawaki through the latter's prosthetic arm. From this, he teleported Kawaki to them with the goal of rebranding Kawaki before his time ran out. As Kawaki tried to escape Isshiki, he opted to use Kawaki's love for Naruto against him, assaulting the downed Hokage. Despite Naruto's insistence that Kawaki forget about him, Kawaki ultimately showed himself and attacked using the ninjutsu Naruto taught him. Isshiki easily negated it and branded Kawaki again, only for it to be revealed as a shadow clone.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7b/Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png/revision/latest?cb=20211003131558" class="image"><img alt="Kurama&#39;s Life Fades Away" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kurama&#39;s Life Fades Away.png" data-image-key="Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7b/Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211003131558" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7b/Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png/revision/latest?cb=20211003131558" class="image"><img alt="Kurama&#39;s Life Fades Away" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7b/Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211003131558" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kurama&#39;s Life Fades Away.png" data-image-key="Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/7/7b/Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211003131558" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kurama%27s_Life_Fades_Away.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto watches Kurama's life fade away.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Finally, Isshiki's time ran out and he crumbled to dust. Sasuke then asked Naruto about his new power, but before he could answer, Boruto, being controlled by <a href="/wiki/Momoshiki" class="mw-redirect" title="Momoshiki">Momoshiki</a>, suddenly stabbed Sasuke's left eye. Naruto attempted to help fighting Momoshiki, but collapsed, feeling heavy as lead, and passed out. Inside his subconscious, Naruto had a final conversation with Kurama. He told the kitsune that he had no ill will to Kurama despite the loss of his parents. As Naruto was prepared to die and voiced his concerns for the village, Kurama revealed that Naruto would awake soon and fine, as it was Kurama's life that was gambled from using Baryon Mode. Kurama assured Naruto that it never actually lied to Naruto, but knew the Hokage wouldn't risk Kurama's own life so he hid the truth. As Kurama's life began to fade, it warned Naruto that he would lose all access to Kurama's chakra and abilities, meaning he would have to be more careful from now on. Naruto desperately reached out for Kurama before waking up to see Boruto, Sasuke, and Kawaki standing over him. 
</p>
