<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/13/Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20211017201017" class="image"><img alt="Naruto comforts Boruto" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto comforts Boruto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/13/Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211017201017" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/13/Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png/revision/latest?cb=20211017201017" class="image"><img alt="Naruto comforts Boruto" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/13/Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211017201017" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto comforts Boruto.png" data-image-key="Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/1/13/Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211017201017" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_comforts_Boruto.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto comforts Boruto over his Kāma.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Sasuke's Rinnegan and Kawaki's Kāma gone, it was up to Boruto to use his mark to bring everyone back with aid from Kawaki. Upon returning to the village, Naruto was relieved. In the anime, shortly after returning, Naruto was examined by Sakura and Katasuke for any remaining traces of Kurama's essence and capacities. The tests found nothing, confirming that Kurama's death would considerably drop Naruto's abilities and fighting potential. Naruto admitted that Kurama's power had felt like cheating, and despite the void left behind, he chose not to wallow on it, believing that Kurama would make fun of him over it. Afterwards, Naruto received confirmation that Boruto's Kāma was accelerating, and decided to inform Boruto himself. He vowed to do everything in his power to save Boruto. When Kawaki returned his prosthetic hand, having his natural one restored by Amado, Naruto offered to make him a genin. 
</p>
<h3><span id="Ch.C5.ABnin_Re-Examination_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Chūnin_Re-Examination_Arc">Chūnin Re-Examination Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D75&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Ch%C5%ABnin_Re-Examination_Arc" title="Chūnin Re-Examination Arc">Chūnin Re-Examination Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png/revision/latest?cb=20211205140359" class="image"><img alt="Chūnin Ceremony" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Chūnin Ceremony.png" data-image-key="Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205140359" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png/revision/latest?cb=20211205140359" class="image"><img alt="Chūnin Ceremony" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205140359" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Chūnin Ceremony.png" data-image-key="Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/9/91/Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205140359" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ch%C5%ABnin_Ceremony.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto attending the chūnin ceremony.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, Naruto had the Chūnin Exam that Momoshiki interrupted reorganised, as a way to boost morale and promote more capable chūnin. Naruto acted as a proctor during the second portion of the exams, evaluating the genin's abilities. During the final exam, Naruto invited Kawaki to attended, and watched the matches alongside Sai and Shikamaru. Commentating on the matches, Naruto and Shikamaru agreed that Boruto and Mitsuki would be disqualified for being late to their match. After the event, he asked Kawaki what he thought, leading to him expressing interest in becoming a genin. Later, after assigning Konohamaru and Mirai a mission, Naruto allowed Konohamaru students to assist him when Mirai returned to the village alone and injured. After Team 7 succeeded in their mission, Naruto hosted the promotion ceremony for the new chūnin, assigning them as captains of their teams.
</p><p>As Naruto decided to test Kawaki for qualification as a shinobi, Shikamaru voiced his concerns, feeling that his modified body would be a prime target for enemies to go after. Naruto however insisted that for Kawaki to grow, he needed to experience the outside world and make friends who could protect him. Because Kawaki fared poorly in D-rank missions with different teams, lacking team-work, Shikamaru deemed him unfit for being a shinobi. He and Naruto agreed to assign him a C-rank escort mission with Team 10 as a final chance to qualify as a genin. Konohamaru arrived and handed him intel on a recently discovered dead body. They wondered about a connection with five other similar incidents in other countries. They determined there was a connection, as all of them were from the Land of Calm Seas. As Team 10 was escorting a client there, Naruto sent Team 7 as backup, as they were out in a mission nearby. At the end of the mission, Boruto reported to Naruto how the Calm Seas Daimyō was exploiting his people. While Naruto couldn't directly interfere, he could send a medical team as a form of aid relief. Later, Kawaki asked for another chance to prove himself, but Naruto revealed that based on Shikadai's report, he passed the exam, and would take missions as a genin under him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Great_Sea_Battle_of_Kirigakure_Arc">Great Sea Battle of Kirigakure Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D76&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Great_Sea_Battle_of_Kirigakure_Arc" title="Great Sea Battle of Kirigakure Arc">Great Sea Battle of Kirigakure Arc</a></span>
In the anime, the Land of Water faced a civil war against the <a href="/wiki/Funato_Clan" title="Funato Clan">Funato Clan</a>. <a href="/wiki/Team_5" title="Team 5">Team 5</a> and <a href="/wiki/Team_7_(Konohamaru)" title="Team 7 (Konohamaru)">Team 7</a> accidentally found themselves caught in it. Aiding Kirigakure, the genin were able to help end the war peacefully. Upon the genin's return to Konohagakure, Naruto informed them of the aftermath from Chōjūrō. As Boruto asked about the fate of his new friend <a href="/wiki/Ikada_Funato" title="Ikada Funato">Ikada Funato</a>, a ship-builder who was drawn to the war after his <a href="/wiki/Seiren_Funato" title="Seiren Funato">sister's</a> death. Kawaki voiced that he deserved punishment as an enemy commander. Boruto insisted that Ikada was a good person and was key in ending the war. As Kawaki stormed off annoyed at Boruto, Naruto approached Boruto, commending him for his efforts in the war and sympathising with Boruto's new view. He encouraged Boruto to make up with Kawaki. Naruto soon after found the two boys instead coming to blows with each other. Naruto cheerfully watched the fight until the two collapsed against each other. Working off their aggression, the two put aside their differences. Naruto approached them, telling Boruto about Ikada's lenient punishment of surveillance under <a href="/wiki/Kajiki" title="Kajiki">Kajiki</a>'s care. Naruto treated them to some ramen.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png/revision/latest?cb=20220717181504" class="image"><img alt="Uzumaki family&#39;s vacation" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Uzumaki family&#39;s vacation.png" data-image-key="Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220717181504" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png/revision/latest?cb=20220717181504" class="image"><img alt="Uzumaki family&#39;s vacation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220717181504" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Uzumaki family&#39;s vacation.png" data-image-key="Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/c/c7/Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220717181504" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Uzumaki_family%27s_vacation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto and his family on vacation.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto later went on a family vacation to a hot spring inn that Himawari won in a raffle, sending Konohamaru in his place to the filming of the next Kagemasa movie where he was to make a guest appearance and use the Rasengan on the climax. At the inn, he and Hinata beat Boruto and Kawaki at ping-pong due to their superior team-work. Naruto later lost to Himawari at a card matching game, and assured Kawaki he was part of the family.
</p>
<div style="clear: left;"></div>
<h3><span id="Kawaki_.26_Himawari_Academy_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Kawaki_&amp;_Himawari_Academy_Arc">Kawaki &amp; Himawari Academy Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D77&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kawaki_%26_Himawari_Academy_Arc" title="Kawaki &amp; Himawari Academy Arc">Kawaki &amp; Himawari Academy Arc</a></span>
In the anime, Naruto and Shikamaru assigned Kawaki a secret mission, to protect Princess <a href="/wiki/Kae_Yukiwari" title="Kae Yukiwari">Kae Yukiwari</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Bamboo" title="Land of Bamboo">Land of Bamboo</a> while she attended the Academy as an exchange student. They explained that Kae's father discovered an assassination plot targeting his daughter, and sent her there while he investigated the matter domestically, Kae herself unaware of the threat. Naruto picked Kawaki because of his lower profile with the public, and offered some advice on how to connect with the students. Naruto gave a speech during the opening ceremony, and was later pleased by Kawaki's report of having befriended Kae. He also felt that Kawaki had something to learn from attending the Academy, despite his advanced fighting skills.
</p><p>Following a terrorist attack on the Academy that served as a diversion for an attempt on Kae's life, Konoha leadership learned that Kawaki didn't report the possibility of an attack, and removed him from the mission. Naruto told Kawaki to stay home until further notice. However, Kawaki later thwarted another attempt on Kae's life, and Naruto informed him that it allowed Batora to report his investigation and arrest the <a href="/wiki/Bamboo_Minister" title="Bamboo Minister">Land of Bamboo's minister</a> as the mastermind behind the plot.
</p><p>While reviewing background files, <a href="/wiki/Hana_Kaka" title="Hana Kaka">Hana Kaka</a> was discovered to hail from the Land of Bamboo, leading to the full uncovering of the plot against Kae. After other conspirators were arrested by Sai and Team 25, Sai, Shikamaru, and Kawaki reported the events to Naruto. Naruto was amenable to Hana's wish to merely suppress her assassin personality in order to teach her to live for more than just her mission. Her wish to maybe one day be friends with it reminded him of his history with Kurama. Naruto was glad that Kawaki's time in the Academy helped him grow, and he was later pleased by how engrossed Himawari was with the Academy, despite still not having decided whether she wanted to be a shinobi or not.
</p>
<h3><span id="Code.27s_Assault_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Code's_Assault_Arc">Code's Assault Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D78&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Code%27s_Assault_Arc" title="Code&#39;s Assault Arc">Code's Assault Arc</a></span>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png/revision/latest?cb=20230212175959" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Shikamaru and Sai discussing Code" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Shikamaru and Sai discussing Code.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230212175959" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png/revision/latest?cb=20230212175959" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Shikamaru and Sai discussing Code" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230212175959" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Shikamaru and Sai discussing Code.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/ba/Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230212175959" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Shikamaru_and_Sai_discussing_Code.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto, Sai, and Shikamaru talking about Code's movements.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Naruto and Shikamaru decided to indefinitely take Boruto off active-duty while deciding on how to deal with his Kāma, helping him pass time with various interviews from the media about his victory over Isshiki. After Amado finished restoring Kawaki's arm, he talked to Naruto about the remaining Kara-threats including their Ten-Tails seed as well as <a href="/wiki/Code" title="Code">Code</a>, who would inevitably seek out and kill all who were responsible for Isshiki's death. Hearing such a threat, Naruto requested Shikamaru to set up a Kage Summit. During the Kage meeting, they discussed Code, Amado's trustworthiness, and the issue of Momoshiki taking over Boruto, to which Naruto swore to handle it should the need arise. He later approached Amado to deal with Boruto's Kāma. He provided him with pills he developed as a means to defeat Jigen. As the Byakugan originates with the Ōtsutsuki, he theorised that weakening it might interfere with the Kāma's progress. As Boruto was given the pills and explained the nature of them, Naruto was horrified at how recklessly Boruto decided to take them. Later, Naruto and Konohamaru watched the Team 7 and Kawaki training together.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bb/Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226182411" class="image"><img alt="Naruto declares Kawaki his son" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto declares Kawaki his son.png" data-image-key="Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bb/Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230226182411" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bb/Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226182411" class="image"><img alt="Naruto declares Kawaki his son" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bb/Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230226182411" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto declares Kawaki his son.png" data-image-key="Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/b/bb/Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230226182411" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_declares_Kawaki_his_son.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto declares that Kawaki is his son.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Naruto found Kawaki moping about his lack of acceptance in the village. Naruto brought him back home, where a welcome dinner party was held for Kawaki. Naruto and his family made it clear that he was welcomed to stay as long as he desired. Naruto further insisted that this was the very reason he became Hokage. While Kawaki was taking magazines out to the trash, Naruto dozed off on the dinner table. When Boruto discovered Kawaki's ruse to avoid surveillance, he exposed it to Naruto, who confirmed it with Nishi as Kawaki released his shadow clone. He notified Ino and Shikamaru of the development, and was against Boruto leaving to find Kawaki, as he was under surveillance for the same reason and returned to discussing the search with Ino. When Ino determined it was futile to search through sensing, Naruto thought back to Boruto's words and searched for him, and confirmed with Nishi he was nowhere nearby.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230319122830" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Rescuing Kawaki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Rescuing Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230319122830" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230319122830" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Rescuing Kawaki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230319122830" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Rescuing Kawaki.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/82/Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230319122830" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Rescuing_Kawaki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto rescues Kawaki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Using Sage Mode, Naruto was able to locate Boruto and Kawaki, alongside an <a href="/wiki/Code" title="Code">unknown individual</a>. Hinata attempted to join him, but he stressed she had to take care of Himawari if something happened to him. As Naruto left two shadow clones on standby to store up more senjutsu chakra, Shikamaru arrived, refusing to let Naruto leave the village against the threat without him since the Hokage now no longer had Kurama for additional power. Shikamaru reminded Naruto that he cannot maintain Sage Mode for long anymore, but Naruto insisted that he can maintain it longer on his own drawing from years of experience. They arrive in time to save Kawaki from having his arm broken by Momoshiki, who had taken over Boruto again. Naruto checked on Kawaki, who begged him to flee, fearing his death. Naruto refused to abandon anyone. Code took Shikamaru hostage, who in turn told Naruto to ignore him and attack. Momoshiki decided to help Code killing Naruto, who was also a problem for him, and attacked with an <a href="/wiki/Ultra-Big_Ball_Rasengan" title="Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan">Ultra-Big Ball Rasengan</a>. He was surprised to see Kawaki absorbing the jutsu with a new Kāma.
</p><p>Naruto continued to watch in disbelief as Kawaki began attacking Momoshiki with no restraint, displaying Isshiki's jutsu in the process. Eventually, Naruto intervened, as Kawaki's attacked would have killed Boruto. He tried to reason with Kawaki, who remained committed to killing Momoshiki. Boruto managed to hold back Momoshiki's personality for a moment, and pushed Naruto out of the way, allowing Kawaki to strike through his chest. Code opted to leave and released Shikamaru. While Kawaki was overwhelming Code, he pulled Daemon through the Claw Mark of his face, reflecting Kawaki's attack and knocking him out before leaving. Shikamaru tried to snap Naruto out of his stupor, and began to consider how to deal with Kawaki, arguing with Naruto, who still wanted to support Kawaki. He was stunned when Boruto woke up, his injuries completely healed.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Omnipotence_Arc">Omnipotence Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D79&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Omnipotence_Arc" title="Omnipotence Arc">Omnipotence Arc</a></span>
After everyone returned to the village, Naruto kept watch over Kawaki as Shikamaru had Sumire examine him. They and Ibiki discussed how to handle Kawaki, and Naruto intended to have a long talk with Kawaki when he wakes up. Sumire noticed the heavy atmosphere around Naruto and asked Shikamaru about it. He claimed Naruto was just exhausted from almost being killed.
</p><p>When Kawaki woke up, he asked Naruto if he'd condemn him for killing Boruto. Naruto revealed Boruto was fine because of his Kāma. He added was grateful that Kawaki was there, otherwise they might all have died, and that Boruto felt the same. As Naruto reassured him that he belonged in Konoha and was family, Ino alerted him of Code and <a href="/wiki/Ada" title="Ada">Ada</a>'s invasion. Naruto feigned a previous appointment and left after confirming that Boruto was fine to a startled Sumire. After Code and Ada left taking Amado with them, Naruto listened as Shikamaru explained Ada's alluring ability and speculated on the other cyborg that Code employed in his battle the previous night. When Kawaki acted callous when considering Amado's possible death and deriding Shikamaru, Naruto censored him.
</p><p>As Shikamaru briefed Team 7 on their new surveillance mission living with Ada and Daemon, Naruto discussed it with Sasuke, explaining how Shikamaru managed to covertly control Boruto and Kawaki into acting more cautiously by entrusting them with responsibility in the form of a mission. When Naruto noticed Sasuke noticing something, Sasuke dismissed it. After Ada and Daemon departed for their new home, Naruto joined Shikamaru in getting Amado to share everything he was still keeping secret. He listened as Amado explained the <a href="/wiki/Shinjutsu" title="Shinjutsu">shinjutsu</a> nature of Ada's and Daemon's abilities, their origins in <a href="/wiki/Shibai_%C5%8Ctsutsuki" title="Shibai Ōtsutsuki">Shibai Ōtsutsuki</a>'s remains, and Amado's goal of using Kawaki's Kāma to resurrect his daughter <a href="/wiki/Akebi" class="mw-redirect" title="Akebi">Akebi</a>. When Shikamaru asked Ada to confirm Amado's claims with her <a href="/wiki/Senrigan" title="Senrigan">Senrigan</a>, Naruto found it a bit excessive. He was satisfied with Amado's goal, and decided he wouldn't interfere in his matters with Kawaki if it didn't endanger Konoha. Naruto agreed to Ada's request to call it a day, as they had just arrived in the village. 
</p><p>While preparing for dinner with Hinata, they were joined by Kawaki, who asked Naruto not to inform the sensors of his presence. Naruto listened as Kawaki reiterated how much he changed because of Naruto, and how he came to think that shinobi and good people like Naruto would be the first to die in any conflict with Ōtsutsuki. When Kawaki said he'd eliminate all the Ōtsutsuki to protect Naruto, including Boruto, Naruto refused to let Kawaki do this. Not wanting to hurt Naruto, nor let him get in the way, Kawaki sent Naruto and Hinata away with <a href="/wiki/Daikokuten" title="Daikokuten">Daikokuten</a>, where they'd be suspended in time, unable to think, and requiring no air or sustenance.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Era:_Part_II">New Era: Part II</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D80&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Boruto.27s_Return_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Boruto's_Return_Arc">Boruto's Return Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D81&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Boruto%27s_Return_Arc" title="Boruto&#39;s Return Arc">Boruto's Return Arc</a></span>
Three years later, Kawaki visited the unconscious Naruto and Hinata.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Flashforward">Flashforward</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D82&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the wake of Konoha's destruction four years after the <a href="/wiki/%C5%8Ctsutsuki" class="mw-redirect" title="Ōtsutsuki">Ōtsutsuki</a> attack on the village, <a href="/wiki/Kawaki" title="Kawaki">Kawaki</a> tells <a href="/wiki/Boruto" class="mw-redirect" title="Boruto">Boruto</a> that he will send him to where he sent the Seventh Hokage.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_Other_Media">In Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D83&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Movies">Movies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D84&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_the_Movie:_Ninja_Clash_in_the_Land_of_Snow">Naruto the Movie: Ninja Clash in the Land of Snow</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D85&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_the_Movie:_Ninja_Clash_in_the_Land_of_Snow" title="Naruto the Movie: Ninja Clash in the Land of Snow">Naruto the Movie: Ninja Clash in the Land of Snow</a></span>
<a href="/wiki/Team_Kakashi" class="mw-redirect" title="Team Kakashi">Team 7</a> is dispatched to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Snow" title="Land of Snow">Land of Snow</a> to protect the lead actress <a href="/wiki/Koyuki_Kazahana" title="Koyuki Kazahana">Koyuki Kazahana</a>, during the shooting of the new Princess Gale movie.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_the_Movie:_Legend_of_the_Stone_of_Gelel">Naruto the Movie: Legend of the Stone of Gelel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D86&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_the_Movie:_Legend_of_the_Stone_of_Gelel" title="Naruto the Movie: Legend of the Stone of Gelel">Naruto the Movie: Legend of the Stone of Gelel</a></span>
Naruto, Sakura and Shikamaru are sent to track and bring a ferret back to its owner. However, when the group is attacked by mysterious soldiers, they embark on to something big.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_the_Movie:_Guardians_of_the_Crescent_Moon_Kingdom">Naruto the Movie: Guardians of the Crescent Moon Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D87&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_the_Movie:_Guardians_of_the_Crescent_Moon_Kingdom" title="Naruto the Movie: Guardians of the Crescent Moon Kingdom">Naruto the Movie: Guardians of the Crescent Moon Kingdom</a></span>
Naruto, Sakura, Rock Lee and Kakashi are assigned to protect the future prince of the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_the_Moon" title="Land of the Moon">Land of the Moon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hikaru_Tsuki" title="Hikaru Tsuki">Hikaru Tsuki</a>.
</p>
<h4><span id="Naruto_Shipp.C5.ABden_the_Movie"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_Shippūden_the_Movie">Naruto Shippūden the Movie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D88&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Shipp%C5%ABden_the_Movie" title="Naruto Shippūden the Movie">Naruto Shippūden the Movie</a></span>

</p>
<h4><span id="Naruto_Shipp.C5.ABden_the_Movie:_Bonds"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_Shippūden_the_Movie:_Bonds">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: Bonds</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D89&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Shipp%C5%ABden_the_Movie:_Bonds" title="Naruto Shippūden the Movie: Bonds">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: Bonds</a></span>

</p>
<h4><span id="Naruto_Shipp.C5.ABden_the_Movie:_Will_of_Fire"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_Shippūden_the_Movie:_Will_of_Fire">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: Will of Fire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D90&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Shipp%C5%ABden_the_Movie:_The_Will_of_Fire" title="Naruto Shippūden the Movie: The Will of Fire">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: The Will of Fire</a></span>

<h4><span id="Naruto_Shipp.C5.ABden_the_Movie:_The_Lost_Tower"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_Shippūden_the_Movie:_The_Lost_Tower">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: The Lost Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D91&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Shipp%C5%ABden_the_Movie:_The_Lost_Tower" title="Naruto Shippūden the Movie: The Lost Tower">Naruto Shippūden the Movie: The Lost Tower</a></span>
Naruto is sent on a mission to stop <a href="/wiki/Mukade" title="Mukade">Mukade</a>. However, during the mission Naruto is sent 20 years into the past.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Naruto_the_Movie:_Blood_Prison">Naruto the Movie: Blood Prison</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D92&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Naruto_the_Movie:_Blood_Prison" title="Naruto the Movie: Blood Prison">Naruto the Movie: Blood Prison</a></span>
Naruto gets framed for the attempted assassination of the Raikage. In his subsequent attempts to break out of the <a href="/wiki/H%C5%8Dzuki_Castle" title="Hōzuki Castle">prison</a>, he gradually discovers the prison's dark secrets.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Road_to_Ninja:_Naruto_the_Movie">Road to Ninja: Naruto the Movie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D93&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Road_to_Ninja:_Naruto_the_Movie" title="Road to Ninja: Naruto the Movie">Road to Ninja: Naruto the Movie</a></span>
Naruto and Sakura end up in an alternate reality in a test version of Project <a href="/wiki/Eye_of_the_Moon_Plan" title="Eye of the Moon Plan">Eye of the Moon Plan</a> where Naruto never lost his parents and many characters have different personalities.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D94&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_video_games" title="List of video games">List of video games</a></span>
As the main character of the series, Naruto is a playable character in every <i>Naruto</i> video game. As the series has progressed, Naruto has become playable in various forms, often with different move-sets for each. New video game-exclusive forms are also available at times, such as a version of Naruto wearing <a href="/wiki/Might_Guy" title="Might Guy">Might Guy</a>'s jump suit, a version wearing <a href="https://dragonball.fandom.com/wiki/Son_Goku" class="extiw" title="w:c:dragonball:Son Goku">Son Gokū's Turtle School Uniform</a>, Naruto from <i><a href="/wiki/Shipp%C5%AB!_Konoha_Gakuen_Den!" title="Shippū! Konoha Gakuen Den!">Shippū! Konoha Gakuen Den!</a></i>, and "<a href="/wiki/Mecha-Naruto" title="Mecha-Naruto">Mecha-Naruto</a>." The video games also put some extra emphasis on his taijutsu; most of the time Naruto in the past fights akin to a brawler; while in his incarnation from <i>The Last: Naruto the Movie</i>, he instead fights more like a hand-to-hand boxer.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Live_Spectacle_Naruto">Live Spectacle Naruto</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D95&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="box headnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Live_Spectacle_Naruto" title="Live Spectacle Naruto">Live Spectacle Naruto</a></span>
Koudai Matsuoka plays as Naruto in this stage play adaption.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Creation_and_Conception">Creation and Conception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D96&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>When creating Naruto, <a href="/wiki/Masashi_Kishimoto" title="Masashi Kishimoto">Masashi Kishimoto</a> incorporated into the character a number of traits he felt made an ideal hero: a straightforward way of thinking, a mischievous side, and many of the attributes possessed by <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goku" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Goku">Son Gokū</a> from the <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dragon_Ball" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dragon Ball">Dragon Ball</a></i> franchise. He also made sure to keep Naruto "simple and stupid," since he does not like smart characters. Naruto himself is not modeled after anyone in particular, being conceived as childlike, with something of a dark side as a result of his harsh past. Despite this, he is always positive, making him unique in Kishimoto's eyes.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8b/FIRST_NARUTO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100227203135" class="image"><img alt="FIRST NARUTO" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="162" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="FIRST NARUTO.jpg" data-image-key="FIRST_NARUTO.jpg" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8b/FIRST_NARUTO.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100227203135" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8b/FIRST_NARUTO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100227203135" class="image"><img alt="FIRST NARUTO" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8b/FIRST_NARUTO.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100227203135" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="162" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="FIRST NARUTO.jpg" data-image-key="FIRST_NARUTO.jpg" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/8/8b/FIRST_NARUTO.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100227203135" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:FIRST_NARUTO.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The first version of Naruto that Masashi Kishimoto drew.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Naruto's wardrobe is based on clothing Kishimoto wore when he was younger; according to Kishimoto, using a pre-existing design would not have made Naruto unique, whereas something original would have made him stand out too much. The orange colouring of his costume is used to make Naruto "pop," with blues often being used to complement the orange. Because Naruto is associated with spirals, swirl patterns are incorporated into his costume. Initial illustrations of Naruto had him wearing boots, but Kishimoto substituted these for sandals, because he likes drawing toes. The goggles that Naruto used to wear were also replaced with a forehead protector, because the goggles themselves were too time-consuming to draw. Kishimoto said that he felt glad that his character had blond hair and blue eyes. The editor of <i>Shōnen Jump</i> in the United States added that Kishimoto implied that the traits may have led the character to appeal to a Western audience. Kishimoto said that he most identifies with Naruto out of all of the <i>Naruto</i> characters (in an interview with the U.S. <i>Shōnen Jump</i>, Kishimoto stated that his childhood was like that of Naruto's years while he was enrolled in the Academy).
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4b/Naruto_Appearances.png/revision/latest?cb=20150630074159" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Appearances" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="230" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Naruto Appearances.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Appearances.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4b/Naruto_Appearances.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150630074159" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4b/Naruto_Appearances.png/revision/latest?cb=20150630074159" class="image"><img alt="Naruto Appearances" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4b/Naruto_Appearances.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150630074159" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="230" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Naruto Appearances.png" data-image-key="Naruto_Appearances.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/4/4b/Naruto_Appearances.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150630074159" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Naruto_Appearances.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Naruto's appearances throughout the series.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the Japanese versions of <i>Naruto</i>, Naruto often ends his sentences with the addendum "<a href="/wiki/Catchphrases_and_Verbal_Tics#Dattebayo.2C_Dattebane_and_Dattebasa" title="Catchphrases and Verbal Tics">-ttebayo</a>" (which gives a similar effect to ending a sentence with "you know?"). Kishimoto wanted to give Naruto a childlike catchphrase, and "dattebayo" came to mind. It complemented Naruto's character, and served as a verbal tic that showed him to be something of a brat. Throughout the beginning of the English <a href="https://animanga.fandom.com/wiki/anime" class="extiw" title="w:c:animanga:anime">anime</a>, the dub replaced "dattebayo" and "-ttebayo" with the phrase "believe it!" to mirror the effect, as well as to match the character's lip movements.
</p>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D97&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="youthwiki">
<tbody><tr>
<td><div class="floatleft"><img alt="Springtime of Youth" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" title="Springtime of Youth" width="40" height="33" data-image-name="Youth symbol.png" data-image-key="Youth_symbol.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/naruto/images/3/39/Youth_symbol.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/40?cb=20130120020002" class="lazyload" /></div>
</td>
<td><small>The <a href="https://springtimeofyouth.fandom.com/wiki/" class="extiw" title="w:c:springtimeofyouth"><i>Springtime of Youth</i> wiki</a> has an article about this topic:
<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b><a href="https://springtimeofyouth.fandom.com/wiki/Naruto_Uzumaki" class="extiw" title="w:c:springtimeofyouth:Naruto Uzumaki">Naruto Uzumaki</a></b></div></small>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul><li>Spiral patterns are a recurring theme in <i>Naruto</i>, especially in relation to the character of Naruto Uzumaki himself. The name "Naruto" is short for "<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narutomaki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Narutomaki">narutomaki</a>" (<span lang="ja">なると巻き</span>), a kind of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kamaboko" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kamaboko">kamaboko</a> with a pink spiral design in the middle that is used as a topping for ramen, which is Naruto's favourite food. His family name "Uzumaki" can mean "<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Whirlpool" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Whirlpool">whirlpool</a>" or "<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maelstrom" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Maelstrom">maelstrom</a>." His full name is also a reference to the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naruto_whirlpools" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Naruto whirlpools">Naruto whirlpools</a> (<span lang="ja">鳴門の渦潮</span>&#44; <i>Naruto no uzushio</i>), named after the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naruto,_Tokushima" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Naruto, Tokushima">city in the Tokushima Prefecture</a> in Japan. In addition, Naruto's mother, Kushina Uzumaki, is a relative to the <a href="/wiki/Uzumaki_clan" class="mw-redirect" title="Uzumaki clan">Uzumaki clan</a> from <a href="/wiki/Uzushiogakure" title="Uzushiogakure">Uzushiogakure</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Whirlpools" title="Land of Whirlpools">Land of Whirlpools</a>, who used the spiral pattern as both their clan and village symbol.</li>
<li>According to the databook(s):
<ul><li>Naruto's hobbies are pulling pranks and watering plants.</li>
<li>Naruto wishes to fight <a href="/wiki/Sasuke_Uchiha" title="Sasuke Uchiha">Sasuke Uchiha</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Third_Hokage" class="mw-redirect" title="Third Hokage">Third Hokage</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-d1_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-d1-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and members of <a href="/wiki/Akatsuki" title="Akatsuki">Akatsuki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-d2_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-d2-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-d3_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-d3-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Naruto's favourite foods are <a href="/wiki/Ichiraku" class="mw-redirect" title="Ichiraku">Ichiraku</a> <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ramen" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ramen">ramen</a> and <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/red_bean_soup" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:red bean soup">red bean soup</a>. His least favourite are fresh <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/vegetable" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:vegetable">vegetables</a>, which others, especially Kakashi (barring Hinata) have attempted to make him eat with little success in other material.</li>
<li>Naruto has completed 16 official missions in total: 7 D-rank, 1 C-rank, 2 B-rank, 6 A-rank, 0 S-rank.</li>
<li>Naruto's favourite phrase is "a large serving of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/miso" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:miso">miso</a> ramen with <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Char_siu" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Char siu">roasted pork fillet</a>" (<span lang="ja">味噌チャーシュー大盛り</span>&#44; <i>miso chāshū ōmori</i>).</li></ul></li>
<li>According to character trivia from <i><a href="/wiki/Boruto:_Naruto_Next_Generations" title="Boruto: Naruto Next Generations">Boruto: Naruto Next Generations</a></i>:
<ul><li>His attributes are: 120 in perception, 160 in dexterity, 170 in negotiations, 110 in strength, 90 in intelligence, and unknown in chakra.</li>
<li>He was also given a skill rating in these particular areas:
<ul><li>Evasion: ★★★★★</li>
<li>Unarmed Hand-to-hand Fighting: ★★★★☆</li>
<li>Manners: ★★☆☆☆</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>According to <a href="/wiki/Hy%C5%8D_no_Sho" title="Hyō no Sho">Hyō no Sho</a>, while in the <a href="/wiki/Academy" title="Academy">Academy</a>, Naruto had an A in positivity, a B taijutsu, and an F in ninjutsu, genjutsu, cooperation, and classroom attitude.</li>
<li>October 10, Naruto's birthday, was <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:">Health and Sports Day</a> in Japan when his character was conceived. The holiday, however, was later moved to the second Monday of October in 1999.</li>
<li>Naruto consistently ranked in the top two (taking first place twice) in the first five official <i>Shōnen Jump</i> character popularity polls. However, in the sixth character poll, he was ranked fourth. According to the third databook character poll, which adds up all the votes from the first six polls, Naruto took second place. In the most recent poll, Naruto regained his status and reached first.
<ul><li>Naruto is one of four characters to have always stayed in the top ten of every character popularity poll.</li></ul></li>
<li>Naruto is the fourth known jinchūriki known to have survived the extraction of a tailed beast, along with Hagoromo Ōtsutsuki, Kushina Uzumaki, and Obito Uchiha.<sup id="cite_ref-ch661_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch661-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Naruto's mother was nicknamed the "Red Hot-Blooded Habanero" while his father was famed as the "Yellow Flash." Naruto's appropriate self-styled title of "<b>Konoha's Orange Hokage</b>" refers to the fact that the colour orange is a mixture of red and yellow.</li>
<li>When Naruto first became a genin, while using his <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Technique" title="Sexy Technique">Sexy Technique</a>, his settei reveals that he is 160cm tall.</li>
<li>Kishimoto's various concept art of Naruto for <i>The Last: Naruto the Movie</i> showed that his height had gone through various changes: first 170cm, then 173cm, and finally 180cm.</li>
<li>Despite Naruto being a user of the Truth-Seeking Balls and gaining Hagoromo's power, both of which contain Yin-Yang Release, Yin Release is not listed as one of his natures in the fourth databook.<sup id="cite_ref-d4_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-d4-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eiichiro Oda">Eiichiro Oda</a>, author of <i><a href="https://onepiece.fandom.com/wiki/_One_Piece_(manga)" class="extiw" title="w:c:onepiece: One Piece (manga)">One Piece</a></i>, stated that his character <a href="https://onepiece.fandom.com/wiki/Sanji" class="extiw" title="w:c:onepiece:Sanji">Sanji</a>'s name was originally going to be Naruto, but changed it because the <i>Naruto</i> series was about to become serialised and wanted to avoid confusion.
<ul><li>Naruto makes an undetailed background appearance on the cover page of the <a href="https://onepiece.fandom.com/wiki/Chapter_766" class="extiw" title="w:c:onepiece:Chapter 766">766th chapter</a> of <i>One Piece</i>, where the person behind <a href="https://onepiece.fandom.com/wiki/Nami" class="extiw" title="w:c:onepiece:Nami">Nami</a> (who is wearing a changpao with the Konoha symbol) is implied to be Naruto. Also, both main characters are seen eating each others' respective favourite foods, as Naruto is eating meat, and <a href="https://onepiece.fandom.com/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" class="extiw" title="w:c:onepiece:Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> is eating ramen. Additionally, this chapter was released on the same week as the release of the <a href="/wiki/The_Seal_of_Reconciliation" title="The Seal of Reconciliation">final</a> <a href="/wiki/Naruto_Uzumaki!!_(chapter_700)" title="Naruto Uzumaki!! (chapter 700)">two</a> <i>Naruto</i> manga chapters.</li>
<li>In the 700th chapter of the <i>Naruto</i> manga, the symbol of the Straw Hat Pirates appears on the forehead protector of Naruto's statue as part of <a href="/wiki/Boruto" class="mw-redirect" title="Boruto">Boruto</a>'s graffiti.</li></ul></li>
<li>While Naruto was initially the shortest of the <a href="/wiki/Konoha_11" title="Konoha 11">Konoha 11</a>, he ultimately becomes second tallest, after Shino.</li>
<li>In the original manga pilot, Naruto was actually a demon fox and lived his life as a human boy and the Nine-Tailed Fox that attacked the village was his father.</li>
<li>Although he was never raised by Minato, Naruto seemingly inherited his father's fighting style of almost never relying on hand seals, with the exception of his <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Clone_Technique" title="Shadow Clone Technique">signature technique</a>.</li>
<li>In the anime, Naruto is a lightweight drinker.<sup id="cite_ref-BE18_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BE18-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Quotes">Quotes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fnaruto.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FNaruto_Uzumaki%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D98&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li>(To <a href="/wiki/Kakashi" class="mw-redirect" title="Kakashi">Kakashi</a>) "<i>And my future dream is to be the greatest <a href="/wiki/Hokage" title="Hokage">Hokage</a>! Then the whole village will stop disrespecting me and start treating me like I'm somebody. Somebody important!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Ibiki" class="mw-redirect" title="Ibiki">Ibiki</a>) "<i>Don't underestimate me! I don't quit and I don't run! You can act tough all you want! You're not gonna scare me off! No way! I don't care if I do get stuck as a <a href="/wiki/Genin" title="Genin">genin</a> for the rest of my life! I'll still be Hokage someday!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Neji" class="mw-redirect" title="Neji">Neji</a>) "<i>I'm not gonna run away, I never go back on my word! That's my <b><a href="/wiki/Nind%C5%8D" title="Nindō">nindō</a></b>: my ninja way!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Gaara" title="Gaara">Gaara</a>) "<i>It's almost unbearable, isn't it… the pain of being all alone. I know that feeling; I've been there, in that dark and lonely place, but now there are others, other people who mean a lot to me. I care more about them than I do myself, and I won't let anyone hurt them. That's why I'll never give up. I will stop you, even if I have to kill you! They saved me from myself. They rescued me from my loneliness. They were the first to accept me as who I am. They're my friends.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Pain" class="mw-redirect" title="Pain">Pain</a>) "<i>Just give up… on trying to make me give up!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Nagato" title="Nagato">Nagato</a>, reciting a line from <a href="/wiki/Jiraiya" title="Jiraiya">Jiraiya</a>'s <a href="/wiki/The_Tale_of_the_Utterly_Gutsy_Shinobi" title="The Tale of the Utterly Gutsy Shinobi">first book</a>) "<i>Then I will break that curse. If there's such thing as peace, I will find it. I won't give up!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-ch448_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch448-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Sasuke" class="mw-redirect" title="Sasuke">Sasuke</a>) "<i>If you attack <a href="/wiki/Konoha" class="mw-redirect" title="Konoha">Konoha</a>, I will have to fight you… So save up your hatred and take it all on me, I'm the only one who can take it! It's the only thing I can do! I will shoulder your hatred and die with you! Because I'm your friend!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Kushina" class="mw-redirect" title="Kushina">his mother</a>) "<i>Don't apologise… I had a lot of hard times growing up as a <a href="/wiki/Jinch%C5%ABriki" title="Jinchūriki">jinchūriki</a>, but I never blamed you or <a href="/wiki/Minato_Namikaze" title="Minato Namikaze">Dad</a>. I couldn't understand what a parent's love was like because you guys were never there… so I could only guess… But now I know… I live because you and Dad gave your lives for me and filled me up with love before the Nine-Tails was inside me! So here I am, happy and healthy! I'm glad I ended up being your son!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Kurama" title="Kurama">Kurama</a>) "<i>You're not the monster fox anymore. You're one of my teammates from Konoha… <b>Kurama.</b></i>"<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Obito" class="mw-redirect" title="Obito">Obito</a>) "<i>Quit it with your stupid reasoning! I meant to say that I'll stand any pain for my friends!! I'm not gonna give up on them!! It might just be me being selfish, but… not having my friends here… is the most painful thing for me!! <b>Period!!!!</b></i>"<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(About <a href="/wiki/Hinata" class="mw-redirect" title="Hinata">Hinata</a>) "<i>Hinata… This big idiot finally understands… The real meaning of the scarf you gave to me when you went with <a href="/wiki/Toneri" class="mw-redirect" title="Toneri">Toneri</a>… I know now, from the scarf you painstakingly knitted and took so long to finish, that your love can't be unravelled so easily… Wait for me… This whole time, you always loved me for the way I am… Now, as a man, there's something I must tell you… Hinata, I swear I <b>will</b> save you!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To Hinata) "<i>Hinata… Do you remember that lesson in class? The one with, "If the end of the world came, who would you spend your last day with?" I couldn't write anyone's name down. I didn't know my parents, and I didn't have any friends… But now, I know exactly whom I'd choose. I want to be with you. Now and forever, until I die… I want to be with you, Hinata!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-TheLast_21-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheLast-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Boruto" class="mw-redirect" title="Boruto">his son</a>) "<i>Boruto… with what I do now, all the people in this village are like a family. So there will be times that you won't be able to have me as a father all to yourself. I know this must be hard for you… but you must learn to endure it. You're a shinobi too, aren't you?</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>(To <a href="/wiki/Konohagakure" title="Konohagakure">the village</a>) "<i>However, I believe there are many who are dissatisfied. This village is still undergoing development. And during all this, there are those who are facing hard and demanding times. But I don't agree with that. Changing the things before us, a little by little, even one thing at a time, will make the world a better place. I want Konohagakure to be a place where people smile and enjoy their lives. Will you lend me your strength? Let's change Konohagakure together!</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
